AliExpress Seller Basic Rules (Violations and Penalty Rules)

Release date: /

Revision date: August 18, 2025

Note: Texts highlighted in red are revisions or additions made this time.

Chapter III Violations and Penalty Rules
========================================

Section I Violation Handling Measures
-------------------------------------

**Article 69** To safeguard the legitimate rights and interests of consumers, operators, and AliExpress, the platform may impose the following measures on members during the violation handling period in accordance with these rules. These measures may remain in effect until the risk is deemed largely controllable by AliExpress, at which point they may be partially or fully lifted:

(i) Warning – AliExpress may issue a verbal or written warning to sellers regarding improper conduct.

(ii) Search Ranking Adjustment – This refers to the adjustment of the ranking of all or part of a store's goods in search results.

(iii) Product Visibility Block – This refers to all goods (including compliant and non-compliant items) that will be hidden from front-end search results and only visible in the seller's own store.

(iv) In-platform Messaging Restriction – This refers to the restriction on sending in-platform messages within the AliExpress platform.

(v) Review Removal – This refers to the removal of store ratings and review content; removed reviews will not be counted in performance metrics.

(vi) Goods Listing Restriction – This refers to the restriction on posting new goods by the member on AliExpress.

(vii) Brand Delisting – This refers to the restriction or prohibition of displaying goods under specific brands on the platform.

(viii) Goods Delisting – This refers to the removal of a member’s product(s) from sale by AliExpress as a penalty measure.

(ix) Goods Deletion – This refers to the deletion of goods from the member's account by AliExpress as a penalty measure.

(x) Marketing Participation Restriction – This refers to the restriction to sellers on participating in marketing campaigns organized or supported by the platform.

(xi) Operating Privilege Closure – This refers to the closure of a seller's right to operate within specific or all business categories.

(xii) Advance Payment Feature Closure – This refers to closing the seller's access to early fund withdrawal services.

(xiii) Increase in Security Deposit for Stores – This refers to the requirement for violating stores to pay an increased security deposit in order to continue operating. Sellers must, within 14 days of receiving the payment notice, top up the store's security deposit to no less than CNY 30,000 before normal business operations can resume. Otherwise, all goods under the store may be subject to visibility restrictions in certain countries or regions.

(xiv) Account Freeze – This refers to the takedown of all active goods and restriction on new goods listings.

(xv) Seller Funds Freeze – This refers to the freeze of the seller's account funds (including but not limited to Alipay International and AliExpress accounts) until the platform determines that risks are under control.

(xvi) Account Closure – This refers to the freezing of the account, restriction on sending in-platform messages, suspension of store access, and a 180-day freeze on seller funds.

(xvii) AliExpress reserves the right to review and process the seller's remaining orders based on the severity of the violation at the time of account closure.

(xviii) Country-Specific Sales Restriction – This refers to the restriction on selling goods to specific countries.

(xix) Credit and Sales Record Deletion – This refers to the deletion of all or part of the seller's credit points and/or sales records for all or selected goods.

In addition to the aforementioned violation handling measures, if a seller violates applicable national laws, regulations, or platform rules, and such violation directly or indirectly causes AliExpress to suffer significant losses, AliExpress reserves the right to hold the seller fully liable for all resulting damages. These losses include, but are not limited to: any direct or indirect penalties imposed by regulatory authorities due to the seller's illegal actions; costs incurred by AliExpress in taking remedial actions to protect the legitimate rights and interests of the platform, other sellers, or buyers; any liquidated damages or compensation payable by AliExpress to third parties as a result of legal rulings; refunds, penalties, or compensation paid by AliExpress on behalf of the seller to buyers; legal fees incurred by AliExpress; and any other necessary expenses for mitigating adverse impact.

AliExpress will handle ongoing orders as follows:

1\. Orders placed but not paid by buyers: Orders will be closed.

2\. Orders paid but pending risk control review, and not yet shipped by seller: Orders will be closed, and full refunds will be issued to buyers. (Note: The platform defines "shipment" based on whether the seller has filled in and submitted a valid tracking number.)

3\. Orders paid and passed risk control review, but not yet shipped by seller: Orders will be frozen. The seller must provide shipping proof and procurement proof (and relevant qualification certificates for certain products). If the seller fails to provide valid documentation, the order will be closed and fully refunded to the buyer; if the documentation is verified, the order will be unfrozen and proceed through the normal transaction flow. (Note: The platform defines "shipment" based on whether the seller has filled in and submitted a valid tracking number.)

4\. Orders already shipped but with no disputes raised: Orders will be frozen. The seller must provide shipping proof and procurement proof (and relevant qualification certificates for certain products). If the seller fails to provide valid documentation, the order will be closed and fully refunded to the buyer; if the documentation is verified, the order will be unfrozen and proceed through the normal transaction flow.

5\. Orders with existing disputes: The seller must provide supporting evidence within the appeal period specified by the AliExpress platform. AliExpress will make a determination based on the evidence submitted by both the buyer and the seller.

6\. Orders successfully completed but not yet disbursed: The order payment will be frozen. The seller must provide shipping proof and procurement proof (and relevant qualification certificates for certain products). If the seller fails to provide valid documentation, the full order amount will be refunded to the buyer.

7\. Other order situations: For any other circumstances not explicitly covered above, the AliExpress platform may handle such cases at its discretion, and may require the seller to submit relevant supporting documentation for assessment.

8\. If a member is suspected of registering or controlling additional accounts on the AliExpress platform, the above order handling measures will also apply to orders associated with such related accounts.

Section II Violation Types and Handling Measures
------------------------------------------------

**Article 70** The platform classifies violations into four distinct point-based systems according to the nature of the misconduct: Intellectual Property Prohibited and Restricted Sales Violations, Transaction and Other Violations, Goods Information Quality Violations, and Severe Intellectual Property Violations. Each of the four point systems operates independently in terms of point deduction, accumulation, and enforcement of penalties.

**Article 71** Intellectual Property Prohibited and Restricted Sales Violations include general intellectual property infringement and illegal publication of prohibited or restricted items. When a seller accumulates 48 points under this category, the account will be closed.

**Article** **72** Severe Intellectual Property Violations include acts of serious intellectual property infringement. Accounts will be closed upon the third confirmed violation. If the infringement is deemed particularly severe, the account will be immediately closed without needing to reach three violations.

**Article 73** Transaction and Other Violations include transaction violations and other behaviors strictly prohibited by the platform. Once 48 points are accumulated under this category, the account will be closed.

**Article 74** Goods Information Quality Violations include misleading listings such as search manipulation and other publication-related violations. If a seller accumulates 12 points or every multiple of 12, the account will be frozen for 7 days.

**Article 75** Point reset logic: Each violation under the four point systems is calculated on a rolling 12-month (365-day) basis. For example, if 6 points are deducted at 12:00 PM on February 1, 2013, those 6 points will be reset at 12:00 PM on February 1, 2014.

**Article 76** AliExpress Four Point Systems and Penalty Threshold Overview:

|     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Violation Type** | **Violation Threshold** | **Penalties** |
| Severe Intellectual Property Violations | First violation | Freeze (based on violation record) |
| Second violation | (1) Violating accounts: freeze (based on violation record), and increase the store's security deposit.<br><br>(2) Other store accounts under the same entity: restricted from publishing new goods, and increase the stores' security deposit.<br><br>(3) No new stores allowed under the same entity. |
| Third violation | (1) Violating accounts: closed.<br><br>(2) Other store accounts under the same entity: store closure or restriction in certain countries/regions.<br><br>(3) No new stores allowed under the same entity. |
| Intellectual Property Prohibited and Restricted Sales Violations | 2 points | Warning |
| 6 points | Restriction on goods operations for 3 days |
| 12 points | Account freeze for 7 days |
| 24 points | (1) Violating accounts: 14-day freeze, and increase the store's security deposit.<br><br>(2) Other store accounts under the same entity: restricted from publishing new goods, and increase the stores' security deposit.<br><br>(3) No new accounts allowed under the same entity. |
| 36 points | (1) Violating accounts: 30-day freeze, and increase the store's security deposit.<br><br>(2) Other store accounts under the same entity: restricted from publishing new goods, and increase the stores' security deposit.<br><br>(3) No new accounts allowed under the same entity. |
| 48 points | (1) Violating accounts: closed.<br><br>(2) Other store accounts under the same entity: store closure or restriction in certain countries/regions.<br><br>(3) No new stores allowed under the same entity. |
| Transaction and Other Violations | 12 points | Account freeze for 7 days |
| 24 points | Account freeze for 14 days |
| 36 points | Account freeze for 30 days |
| 48 points | Closure |
| Goods Information Quality Violations | 12 points and every multiple of 12 | Account freeze for 7 days |

**Article 77** If the business entity operating a seller account is suspected of registering or controlling other accounts on the platform simultaneously, AliExpress may take actions such as freezing the related accounts, increasing the related stores' security deposit, restricting operations in certain countries or regions, or removing the related stores from the platform. In cases involving malicious or intentional serious violations, or where infringement is particularly egregious or extreme, the platform will close all stores under that entity and reserves the right to confiscate all security deposits paid by those stores.

**Article 78** If a seller is subject to account closure or removal from the platform due to violations of platform rules, AliExpress shall, in order to protect the legitimate rights and interests of buyers and rights holders, freeze the seller's Alipay International account and AliExpress account for six months. In cases where the violation is particularly serious or egregious, the platform reserves the right to extend the freeze period to one year or two years. For violations that significantly disrupt platform order and cause actual harm to the platform or other sellers, AliExpress reserves the right to freeze the seller's Alipay International account and AliExpress account until reasonable compensation has been made to the affected party.

**Article 79** During the freeze period, the seller is prohibited from making withdrawals or conducting any other fund operations via their Alipay International or AliExpress account. All funds in these accounts will remain frozen.

**Article 80** During the freeze period, if the seller does not incur any refund, compensation, or dispute obligations, then upon the expiration of the freeze period, the platform will return any remaining funds in the Alipay International account (if any) to the seller and close the Alipay International account.

**Article 81** During the freeze period, if the seller becomes liable for refunds or compensation due to disputes, chargebacks by banks, or other reasons, the platform reserves the right to process the corresponding refunds or compensation directly from the seller's Alipay International and/or AliExpress account. Upon expiration of the freeze period, the remaining account balance (if any) will be returned to the seller, and both the Alipay International and AliExpress accounts will be closed.

**Section III Four Categories of Violations and Penalties**
-----------------------------------------------------------

### **Intellectual Property Prohibited and Restricted Sales Violations**

**Article 82** Intellectual Property Prohibited and Restricted Sales Violations

For details, please refer to [AliExpress Intellectual Property Policy](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/uz0s1adxynipabwp) and the[AliExpress Prohibited and Restricted Product Information List](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/zqnolc0rqiqao6qv).

### **Severe Intellectual Property Violations**

**Article 83** Severe Intellectual Property Violations

For details, please refer to [AliExpress Intellectual Property Policy](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/uz0s1adxynipabwp).

### **Transaction and Other Violations**

**Article 84** Transaction Violations

(i) Order uploading rate rules: Refer to [AliExpress – Rules on Order Uploading Rate Assessment](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/or0ke0y5pdhgf7od).

(ii) False shipment: Refer to [AliExpress – Rules on False Shipment](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/hy3as9n49ekvb7a1).

(iii) Goods review rules: Refer to [AliExpress – Rules on Goods Review](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/180243868).

(iv) Malicious harassment: Refer to [AliExpress – Rules on Malicious Harassment](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/axg44ig2bowc6csi).

(v) Illegal profit: Refer to [AliExpress – Rules on Illegal Profit](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523667).

(vi) Severe disruption of platform order: Refer to [AliExpress – Rules on Severe Disruption of Platform Order](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/za7e3eg6onvy5bvz).

(vii) Unfair competition: Refer to [AliExpress – Rules on Unfair Competition](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/az66gglzglli8550).

(viii) Breach of commitment: Refer to [AliExpress – Penalty Rules for Breach of Commitment](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/lqyk79adyv4vz23i).

(ix) Inducing early receipt: Refer to [AliExpress – Rules on Inducing Early Receipt](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/npckm15bnq1o8q7q).

(x) Inducing off-platform transactions: Refer to [AliExpress – Rules on Inducing Off-Platform Transactions](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/hrg33kyw7bgp865k).

(xi) Seriously malicious ultra-low prices: Refer to [AliExpress – Rules on Seriously Malicious Ultra-Low Prices](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/ni7afhwvz07u35g3).

(xii) Forgery of qualification certificates or appeal materials: Sellers must ensure that submitted qualification certificates or appeal documents are truthful and legally valid. If there is obvious suspicion of forgery, or if such materials are verified as fake by the rights holder, official authorities, or other recognized institutions, AliExpress reserves the right to penalize or permanently close the seller's account.

(xiii) Any other conduct that AliExpress deems as violating the platform rules, disrupting market order, or infringing on the rights of consumers or other sellers. AliExpress reserves the right to publish or notify additional or amended violations within a reasonable period.

(xiv) Disclosure of personal information: Refer to [AliExpress – Rules on Personal Information Disclosure](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/kez3g8zgkcyfogig).

(xv) Non-shipment after the transaction: Refer to [AliExpress – Rules on Non-shipment After the Transaction](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/sgw3pg859cwz6gr7).

(xvi) Credit and sales volume manipulation: Refer to [AliExpress – Rules on Credit and Sales Volume Manipulation and its supplemental interpretations](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/rvqmvo98oy8a16lg).

(xvii) Truthful declaration obligation: Click to view [AliExpress Reaffirmation of Sellers'Obligation for Truthful Declarations](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/iuyog7o0kugyecek).

(xviii) Abuse of reporting mechanism: Refer to [AliExpress – Rules on Abuse of Reporting](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/137699600).

**Article 85** Others

**I. Improper Gains**

Unfair profiteering refers to the behavior of members using improper means to seek benefits, including:

(i) Members offer money, gifts, entertainment, hospitality, or commercial opportunities to AliExpress staff and/or their affiliates;

(ii) Members seek improper benefits from AliExpress staff through other means.

If a member is found to have engaged in improper gain, regardless of whether any benefit was actually obtained: The member's store(s) and any affiliated store(s) will be permanently closed; AliExpress will permanently cease to provide or accept any products or services from the member; if the member has violated improper gain policies or committed other dishonest behavior on other Alibaba Group platforms (including but not limited to Alibaba China Site, Alibaba International Site, Taobao, and Tmall), leading to account closure, AliExpress reserves the right to take equivalent action on the member's AliExpress accounts, whether owned or controlled by them.

For service providers found to have engaged in improper gain, AliExpress will permanently cease to provide or accept any products or services from them; stores operated by the service provider must switch to self-operation or another provider within three months of receiving AliExpress notification. If they fail to do so within the specified time, AliExpress will impose supervision measures on the store until the required changes are completed.

If the member truthfully and voluntarily discloses or actively reports their involvement in improper gain, AliExpress may, at its discretion, apply lenient or mitigated penalties.

From the date an investigation into improper gain is initiated, AliExpress will restrict the member's store(s) and related store(s) from participating in any marketing activities until the investigation concludes.

If a member explicitly expresses intent to engage in improper gain toward AliExpress staff and/or their affiliates, or has already initiated such behavior, the member's store(s) will be permanently closed, even if the attempt was unsuccessful due to reasons beyond the member's control.

The following circumstances shall be deemed as acts of improper gain:

(i) The seller is an AliExpress employee – the member's store will be immediately and permanently closed.

(ii) The seller is an affiliate of an AliExpress employee who failed to declare the relationship in accordance with the Alibaba Group Code of Business Conduct, and the employee leveraged their position – the member's store will be immediately and permanently closed.

**II. Improper Marketing Practices**

Sellers must engage in marketing in a lawful, compliant, and reasonable manner. Without prior consent from the buyer, sellers must not contact buyers in a disruptive way for marketing purposes. This includes, but is not limited to, sending emails, making phone calls, sending SMS messages, or using AliExpress system tools to reach out to buyers for promotional activities.

### Goods Information Quality Violations

**Article 86** Goods Information Quality Violations

(i) Search manipulation: Click to view [AliExpress – Rules on Search Manipulation](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/wfbcvewgc2ygsr3y).

(ii) Unauthorized use of seller images: Click to view [AliExpress – Rules on Unauthorized Use of Seller Images](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/hl8e39yii6upga3c).

(iii) Inactive product management: Click to view [AliExpress – Rules on Managing Inactive Goods](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/gnsxrmqy0qn99xeh).

(iv) Posting non-contracted goods: Click to view [Rules and Implementation Details for Posting Non-Contracted Goods](https://aliexpressrulecenter.yuque.com/lh72i0/ad75rh/ein966dgfxcinsfd).

(v) Inclusion of Contact Information or Advertisement-Oriented Goods

It is strictly prohibited to display any form of contact information in product listings, including but not limited to email addresses, WeChat IDs, phone numbers, QQ, MSN, Skype, etc., whether in text fields or images. Sellers must not publish any promotional content for the purpose of advertising their store or products that includes such contact details or external links to third-party platforms (non-AliExpress), including but not limited to links or information embedded in goods titles, images, or detailed descriptions. Listings that attempt to attract buyers through promotional content while providing vague product descriptions or offering no actual product are considered violations. The inclusion of links to non-AliExpress websites in any part of the product description is strictly forbidden.

For such violations, AliExpress reserves the right to reject or remove the goods listing. If a seller accumulates a large number of such listings or commits repeated violations, AliExpress may, based on the severity of the behavior, deduct points and/or impose direct account penalties accordingly.

(vi) Posting confusing goods: Click to view [AliExpress – Rules on Posting Confusing Goods](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/138584482).

(vii) Other improper listing behaviors: Click to view [AliExpress – Rules on Other Improper Listing Behaviors](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/132945377).

(viii) Substandard store information quality: Click to view [AliExpress – Rules on Substandard Store Information Quality Management](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/181832351).

Section IV Liquidated Damages
-----------------------------

**Article 87** If a seller accumulates a total of 48 penalty points due to severe intellectual property violations, prohibited/restricted product listings, transaction violations and other violations, or if the account is directly closed in accordance with platform rules, the platform reserves the right to fully confiscate the security deposit paid on that account as compensation for the seller's breach of contract. If the seller is found to have committed intentional and serious violations, engaged in particularly egregious infringement, or clearly acted with malicious intent to evade platform control rules, the platform also reserves the right to confiscate the security deposit paid by the other associated accounts under the same entity.

**Article 88** If the remaining balance of the security deposit is insufficient for AliExpress to deduct the corresponding amount of the liquidated damages, the seller shall be responsible for paying the shortfall to AliExpress. If MYBank only fulfills part of the penalty to the platform, the seller shall be responsible for paying the shortfall to AliExpress.

**Article 89** If the seller's actions cause greater actual losses to the platform, AliExpress reserves the right to pursue further compensation from the seller until the full amount of the loss is recovered.

Update of Enforcement Actions for Intellectual Property Rights (IPR)

Release date: /

Revision date: January 16, 2025

  

Infringement Claims on AliExpress
---------------------------------

Any posting or sale of products that infringe on intellectual property rights is prohibited on AliExpress.

If a seller posts or sells products that infringe on another party’s intellectual property right, it may be complained by intellectual property rights owners or buyers. The platform will also initiate random check on the information of products (including Off-Shelf products) and product listings. If any suspicious infringement is found, the information will be rejected or removed and the penalty will be imposed according to the specific circumstance of infringement.

1、The Intellectual Property Rights (IPR) Protection Policy
----------------------------------------------------------

|     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Types of IPR Infringements** | **Types of Infringements** |     | **Penalty** |     |
| Trademark rights Infringement | **Serious violation:**<br><br>Unauthorized use of a mark that is identical or very similar to the registered trademark on the same class of product and/or on its packaging. |     | 1）Membership termination upon three violations. Under certain extreme / conspicuous situations, intentional/malicious serious violations, Membership termination upon one violation.<br><br>2）AliExpress may charge the liquidated damages according to the Clause 6 of Annex below. |     |
| **General violation:** Other circumstances of trademark infringement. |     | 1）No penalty point incurred for the first violation;<br><br>2）6 penalty points incurred for each repeat violation;<br><br>3）48 penalty points cumulatively incurred results in membership termination. |     |
| Copyrights Infringement | Any unauthorized use of copyrighted materials, such as text, images, viodes, music, software, will amount to copyright infringement.<br><br>**Physical product violation:**<br><br>1）the product or its packaging is pirated；<br><br>2）the physical product or its packaging is not a pirate, but includes unauthorized copyrighted works；<br><br>**Information violation:**<br><br>The product or its packaging not infringing, but there’s unauthorized use of copyrighted works, such as pictures or texts etc. on the product listing(s) |     | 1）No penalty point incurred for the first violation;<br><br>2）6 penalty points incurred for each repeat violation;<br><br>3）48 penalty points cumulatively incurred results in membership termination. |     |
| Patent rights<br><br>Infringement | Design, design patent, utility model, and invention patent rights infringements<br><br>(General or serious violation would be determined on a case-by-case basis). |     | 1）No penalty point incurred for the first violation;<br><br>2）6 penalty points incurred for each repeat violation;<br><br>3）48 penalty points cumulatively incurred results in membership termination.<br><br>(Membership termination upon three violations in case of serious violation.) |     |
| **Annex**<br><br>1、Applicable enforcement actions shall be imposed based on the complaint, the product listing status as at the time when the complaint filed by rights holder is received or when random check was conducted.  <br>2、All of general violations and copyrights Infringements including rights holders' complaints (which include circumstances where a complaint is filed but no counter-notice is submitted by the seller within the specified time limit, or where the counter-notice submitted by the user is rejected) and random checks by AliExpress within a day shall incur no more than 6 penalty points.<br><br>3、All of serious violations including rights holders' successful complaints (which include circumstances where a complaint is filed but no counter-notice is submitted by the seller within the specified time limit, or where the counter-notice submitted by the user is rejected) and random checks by AliExpress within three days shall be counted as one serious violation only. Membership will be terminated upon a total of three serious violations regardless of the type of IPR infringement involved.<br><br>4、AliExpress has the right to impose penalties against violations and infringements conducted by sellers and take actions against sellers, including but not limited to<br><br>（1）rejection, removal ,certain countr(ies)/region(s) geo-blocking of product listings or information;<br><br>（2）selling restrictions;<br><br>（3）suspension of accounts ; and<br><br>（4）termination of accounts （including all associated accounts of the same entity）. For any terminated account, AliExpress has the right to collect liquidated damages and take appropriate measures to prevent the account holder from registering AliExpress again.  <br>5、All violations (except account terminations) shall be recorded for 365 days from the date of penalty imposed.<br><br>6、Intentional and malicious conduct includes the use of methods designed to evade detection and enforcement, including but not limited to:<br><br>（1）listings linked to third-party sites like social media platforms and chat applications (e.g. hidden links);<br><br>（2）in-site IM channels;<br><br>（3）multiple listings in a single store featuring images with blurred and/or obscured marks and/or engaging in obviously inappropriate suggestive behavior for the display and sale of infringing information (the platform shall decide on a case-by-case basis).<br><br>Upon a final determination (after appeals are exhausted) that a seller committing IPR violations has engaged in intentional and malicious conduct, AliExpress may assess liquidated damages of RMB 45,000 or more. AliExpress may collect the damages by charging the seller's Alipay International and associated accounts, AliExpress account, and AliExpress deposit. AliExpress may pursue necessary action against the seller to collect any remaining balance.<br><br>7、Under certain extreme / conspicuous situations, AliExpress reserves the right to terminate [AliExpress seller service agreement](https://sell.aliexpress.com/zh/__pc/7rgg17qbAa.htm) and [Free Membership Agreement](https://rule.alibaba.com/rule/detail/2042.htm?spm=a271m.8038972.1999288231.3.eE6vyM), user account and any and all accounts determined to be related to such user by AliExpress at its sole discretion, and / or to implement other measures that AliExpress considers appropriate at its discretion for the purpose of protecting the legitimate rights and interests of consumers and rights holders and maintaining the normal operation order on AliExpress. In such circumstances, in addition to directly terminating the user account, AliExpress is also entitled to freeze the funds in the International Alipay account and AliExpress account associated with the user and to charge the liquidated damages according to the fixed amount in Clause 6 for Intentional/malicious serious violations or ask the seller to compensate AliExpress for the losses incurred by seller's infringement behaviors so as to ensure that the legitimate rights and interests can be protected etc. . “Extreme / conspicuous situations”includes but not limited to:<br><br>（1）Where repeat infringement acts committed by user are considered as serious；<br><br>（2）Where litigation has already been initiated or legal demands have been requested by intellectual property rights holder against/to AliExpress；<br><br>（3）User being sued by intellectual property rights holder, or being investigated by judiciary, enforcement or administrative authorities with respect to suspected infringements；<br><br>（4）Requests from judiciary, enforcement or administrative authorities to terminate any account or take any relevant measures；<br><br>（5）Other circumstances that constitute serious violation.<br><br>8、AliExpress reserves the rights of final interpretation and decision and all relevant rights thereof.<br><br>9、In the event of inconsistency between the Chinese and the non-Chinese version of these rules, [the Chinese version shall prevail.](https://sell.aliexpress.com/zh/__pc/ipr_rules.htm) |     |     |     |     |

2、AliExpress expects members to:
--------------------------------

（1）Respect intellectual property rights of others;  
（2）Develop and promote private-label brands;  
（3）List branded products only after our verification of relevant supporting documents.

AliExpress Community Guidelines

Release date: /

Revision date: July 22, 2025

  

Welcome to AliExpress ("AliExpress" or "we/us") content community (the “Community”)! The Community is a place where consumers around the world can share life experiences, participate in discussions, and share feedback about products and services. We work with you to build a caring, respectful, friendly, and engaging community. Please read and follow these Guidelines to maintain the integrity of the Community.

1\. Scope of application
------------------------

1.1 We encourage you to use AliExpress social functions in line with these Guidelines, including but not limited to:

(1) Share your feedback/review and comments on the products you purchased,

(2) Share your life on AliExpress Feed/Inspiration Channel,

(3) Use AliExpress in-app live streaming feature,

(4) Upload user avatar and profile information, and

(5) Use interactive communication features, e.g. Asking Everyone, IM feature, etc.

1.2 By accessing or using our Community features, you agree to our [Terms of Use](https://rule.alibaba.com/rule/detail/2041.htm?spm=a271m.8038972.1999288231.4.5b826d828ZjyPz) and [Free Membership Agreement](https://rule.alibaba.com/rule/detail/2042.htm?spm=a271m.8038972.1999288231.3.5b826d82BuVhKR) and to follow these Guidelines and other applicable rules, policies and guidelines on AliExpress as amended from time to time. These Guidelines will apply to the content you submit to the Community (including texts, images, videos, and links), your use of Community features, and your interactions with other users in the Community.

2\. Appropriate behaviour and respect others
--------------------------------------------

A caring and respectful Community is built on mutual respect, understanding and appreciation. AliExpress trusts all Community users and we hope that users should also observe the following guidelines:

(1) No discrimination. Do not post discriminatory content or any content inciting discrimination. For example, do not express hatred or intolerance of others based on their ethnicity, race, nationality, gender or gender identity, religion, sexual orientation, age, or disability, and do not promote organizations or individuals that make such inappropriate comments.

(2) Do not annoy others. Do not post content that is libellous, defamatory, harassing, threatening, insulting, obscene, pornographic, obscene, or offensive. For example, do not hurt others with insulting remarks, do not deliberately fabricate false information to damage the reputation of others, do not use foul language or profane language, do not send repeated, similar and similar messages to others repeatedly by forwarding, commenting, @others, asking for attention and other ways.

(3) Do not post false information. Do not post content that is untrue, false, exaggerated or misleading. For example, do not use false identity, do not fabricate details to distort the event, do not exaggerate the fact in the description, mislead others, avoid using absolute terms to make false propaganda.

(4) Do not post inappropriate information. Please do not post content that is contrary to public order and good morals, promotes unhealthy thoughts/lifestyles, or causes public discomfort. For example, don't post content that may cause viewers discomfort, and don't post content that includes overeating, blood/violence, dangerous behavior, bad child behavior, etc.

3\. Be helpful
--------------

The Community aims to provide accurate, relevant and helpful content to users, and the Community encourages all users to provide content based on real demands and experience. To make the Community features more specific and topic oriented, we also encourage you to submit content that is relevant to a specific topic.

We are always committed to improving your shopping experience, and suggest that comments should be relevant to the products. If you have any questions about merchants, logistics, packaging, etc., please click Help Centre to seek assistance or solutions.

4\. Encouraged behaviour
------------------------

We value our Community and hope to provide users with interesting and useful content. The following sharing will be of particular interest to Community users :

(1) Deliver short videos conveying messages about your love and passion for life, and how you cherish wonderful moments in daily life.

(2) Pictures showing beauty and taste of a healthy life.

(3) Short videos which tell a story, or contain interesting elements, or tailor-made content.

(4) A good warm-up with an interesting and entertaining environment prepared for livestreaming, which creates a professional, trustworthy and interactive atmosphere with audiences and keeps their attention to the livestreaming.

(5) Other creative content.

5\. Prohibited behaviour
------------------------

5.1 Post infringing content. We are committed to technological innovation and intellectual property protection. You must not infringe others’ intellectual property rights (trademark, copyright, patent, etc.) or other rights when you post content or interact with other users in the Community. You should only post content created by you or content that you are permitted to use.

5.2 Post content that may create transaction risks. To create a Community where users can trust, share and interact with each other, please do not post content that violates AliExpress promotion rules or that may cause transaction risks. For example, do not use any means, directly or indirectly, to induce users to conduct any offline transactions (including through third-party platform accounts, Alipay, bank transfer, etc.); do not post advertisements or solicitations, including any names, URLs, QR codes, logos, contact and account information, of third-party websites or apps (e.g. social networking, shopping guide, group buying, shopping platform).

5.3 Abuse of platform features and post spam content. Do not use any means technological or otherwise) to abuse platform features, products, or functions, including to benefit from artificially increasing the number of views, likes, comments, etc., or repeatedly posting the same messages.

5.4 Post prohibited content.

5.4.1 "Prohibited **content**" refers to information that endangers national and social security or other sensitive information and prohibited content as defined under the applicable national laws and regulations of the respective country and jurisdiction. We may remove any content and, in exercising such discretion, to ensure proportionality to the risk such content poses to other users of the Services. The content thatclassified as "primary priority content" is strictly prohibited by AliExpress, it includes but not limited to:

(1) pornographic content,

(2) content which encourages, promotes or provides instructions for suicide,

(3) content which encourages, promotes or provides instructions for deliberate self-injury, and

(4) content which encourages, promotes or provides instructions for eating disorders or related behaviours.

Besides, "priority content" is also prohibited, it includes but not limited to abuse and hate content, bullying content, violent content, harmful substances content, and dangerous stunts and challenges content.

5.4.2 Other “Prohibited Content” includes content which:

(1) violates the fundamental principles under the applicable laws of the respective country;

(2) endangers the unity, sovereignty, and territorial integrity of the respective country;

(3) leaks state secrets, endangers national security, or damages national honour and interests;

(4) incites ethnic hatred and discrimination, undermines ethnic unity, or infringes ethnic customs and habits;

(5) undermines religious policies and promotes extreme religious beliefs and superstitions;

(6) disseminates rumours to disrupt social order and destabilize social stability;

(7) promotes gambling, violence, homicide, terror, drug abuse, pyramid schemes, self-abuse, or instigates crimes;

(8) incites unlawful assemblies, associations, processions, demonstrations, and gathering crowds to disrupt social order;

(9) contains obscene and pornographic information, including but not limited to:

1) sexually explicit images or descriptions or pornographic and vulgar content;

2) photos or videos containing nudity or sexually explicit images, or photos, videos, audios or texts containing sexual undertones, innuendoes, insinuations, or any other content implying sexual intent or arousal.

3) vulgar information, e.g. clothes that barely cover the intimate parts of human body, dressed in revealing clothes, topless or bare-chested photos, photos of naked children, breastfeeding, etc, except for the descriptions, illustrations and reviews in relation to product features.

(10) contains other content prohibited by the laws and regulations of the respective country.

Doxing and invasion of privacy. Do not post personal information of other Community users, including phone numbers, private email addresses, mailing addresses, credit card numbers, etc.

Impersonate AliExpress official account to conduct fraudulent and deceptive activities. It is prohibited to impersonate AliExpress official account to contact other users or conduct other fraudulent and deceptive activities.

6\. Protection of personal information and privacy
--------------------------------------------------

We value privacy of all Community users and are committed to protecting your personal information. When using Community features, please pay attention to the following:

be cautious when publishing your personal information such as name, birthday, contact information, and photos in the Community. If you publish content which contains personal information of another user or other users, you should inform such user(s) and obtain the prior express consent of such user(s).

we do not provide services to minors. If the content you choose to publish contains personal information of minors, you must notify their parents or guardians in advance and obtain the prior express consent from their parents or guardians.

we will not ask you to provide personal information or publish any of your personal information in the Community without informing you and obtaining your consent. Please do not disclose your password to anyone in the Community.

if you share your computer or device with others, please do not save your login information (for example, user ID and password) in the same computer or device. Remember to log out of your account and close the browser after use.

Do not share your own login information or login information of other users on the AliExpress platform.

We will take appropriate technical and organisational measures to prevent unauthorised access to the Community, maintain data accuracy, and ensure use of the information in our possession for the purposes stated.

For more details, please see [AliExpress.com Privacy Policy](http://terms.alicdn.com/legal-agreement/terms/suit_bu1_aliexpress/suit_bu1_aliexpress201909171350_82407.html)

7\. Implementation
------------------

7.1.1 Together we build our Community.

We welcome your participation in building the Community together with us. We highly value your ideas and thoughts. If you have any comments and suggestions for us, please click “Help Centre” to contact us.

You can click “report” link on the relevant page to report violations if you believe any user or content violates these Guidelines, and we will follow up and take actions in accordance with these Guidelines. Let us work together to build a better Community!

Examples of “report”:

7.1.2 Termination and cancellation

We are always committed to making the Community a caring and warm place for all the users. We encourage users to share with us as much as possible their authentic comments and suggestions, and we also hope users will be considerate and responsible when posting content. We will take the following actions against inappropriate behaviour and content:

Block content

Delete content

Disenable the function of publishing content

Suspension of your account

Closure of your account

AliExpress Live Broadcasting Platform Management Regulations

Release date: /

Revision date: September 5, 2024

  

Article 1 \[Scope of Application\]
----------------------------------

These regulations apply to all users (referred to collectively as "**Users**") who publish or broadcast content on the AliExpress live broadcasting platform (“**AliExpress Live**”). By publishing or broadcasting content on AliExpress Live on the AliExpress Live website ([https://live.aliexpress.com](https://live.aliexpress.com/)) or the AliExpress application, you agree or are deemed to have agreed that your access and use of AliExpress Live shall be subject to and regulated by these regulations.

Article 2 \[Effectiveness Level\]
---------------------------------

These regulations are supplemental to the [AliExpress Free Membership Agreement](https://terms.alicdn.com/legal-agreement/terms/suit_bu1_aliexpress/suit_bu1_aliexpress202204182115_37406.html),[AliExpress Terms of Use](https://terms.alicdn.com/legal-agreement/terms/suit_bu1_aliexpress/suit_bu1_aliexpress202204182115_66077.html?spm=a2g0o.new_account_index.0.0.244d25b9T2HONe), [AliExpress Prohibited and Restricted Sales Rules](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/?tocUuid=KqeTC8M1puePAZkT), [AliExpress Intellectual Property Rules](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/?tocUuid=E0vEu_6L2JILeQTi) and [AliExpress Community Guidelines](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/137261302). In case of any conflict or inconsistency between the provisions of these regulations and those of the foregoing agreements and rules, these regulations shall prevail.

Article 3 \[Admission\]
-----------------------

1、Live Streamer

1.1 AliExpress users who apply and are granted permission to access the live broadcasting function on AliExpress Live are referred to as Live Streamers.

1.2 Live Streamers must be at least 18 of age.

1.3 AliExpress reserves the right to formulate and implement special requirements for AliExpress users to be granted access to the live broadcasting function on AliExpress Live from time to time.

2、Merchant Streamer

2.1 AliExpress seller with a normal store status with a certain number of loyal fans, customer operation capabilities, and hosting qualities are referred to as Merchant Streamers and may be granted permission to access the live broadcasting function on AliExpress Live.

2.2 AliExpress reserves the right to formulate and implement special requirements for AliExpress sellers to be granted access to the live broadcasting function on AliExpress Live from time to time.

3、Interactive Viewers

3.1 AliExpress users who have completed the account registration can interact with the streamers (i.e. comment) during the live broadcasting on AliExpress Live and are referred to as Interactive Viewers.

3.2 Consent from guardians must be sought in advance for Interactive Viewers who are under the age of 18 if required by applicable laws and regulations.

Article 4 \[Information Publication\]
-------------------------------------

All Users who publish or broadcast content on AliExpress Live (including Live Streamers, Merchant Streamers and Interactive Viewers) are prohibited from:

1、publishing harmful information, such as sensitive information, obscene and pornographic information, etc.;

2、publishing false information, such as false advertising, fake prize draw, discrepancies between promoted product information and actual information, etc.;

3、faking activity information;

4、publishing spam advertisements;

5、publishing any other information that violates applicable laws and regulations or is not allowed to be published by the AliExpress Live under these regulations, including as set out in the Violation Handling Overview.

Article 5 \[Code of Conduct\]
-----------------------------

1、All Users who publish or broadcast content on AliExpress Live (including Live Streamers, Merchant Streamers and Interactive Viewers) are prohibited from:

1.1 engaging in promotion activity that violates the platform agreements or rules, such as promoting products that may involve counterfeit goods or violating platform promotion rules;

1.2 engaging in behaviors that may lead to transaction risks, such as guiding users to engage in offline transactions or posting products or information from external websites;

1.3 infringing upon the rights of others, such as leaking others' information, improper use of others' rights, or harassing others, as well as infringing intellectual property rights of others;

1.4 disrupting platform order, such as engaging in fraud or cheating, providing false information, etc.;

1.5 violating commitments and guarantees to users or the platform;

1.6 violating the streamer requirements published or updated by AliExpress from time to time;

1.7 engaging in any of the activities set out in the Violation Handling Overview.

2、All Users are responsible for the activities conducted on their account, including the publishing or broadcasting of any content on AliExpress Live, and must ensure that their activities are in compliance with applicable laws and regulations.

3、All Users:

3.1 must keep their account information (including password and other login details) confidential and secure; and

3.2 must not provide any third party with access to their account. If any User knows or suspects any unauthorised access to or use of their account, the User must promptly notify AliExpress through Customer Service – Help Center.

4、Once the Live Streamer or the Merchant Streamer has created a live stream, AliExpress shall be entitled to review the title, cover picture, preview and proposed merchandise of the live stream for content moderation and safety evaluation purposes.

Article 6 \[Violation Handling\]
--------------------------------

1、Streamers:

In the event of a violation of these regulations by streamer, in addition to any of the penalties that may be imposed (as set out in the Violation Handling Overview), AliExpress reserves the right to issue warnings, take down the live broadcast, delete live content, freeze live broadcasting function, or terminate the account of any Live Streamer or Merchant Streamers immediately and without prior notice.

2、Interactive Viewers:

In the event of a violation of these regulations by Interactive Viewer, in addition to any of the penalties that may be imposed (as set out in the Violation Handling Overview), AliExpress reserves the right to delete the violating content, suspend live broadcast commenting function, or disable live broadcast commenting function of any Interactive Viewer immediately and without prior notice.

For specific violations and corresponding handling measures and penalties, please refer to the Violation Handling Overview.

3、In addition to the penalties set out in the Violation Handling Overview and the right of termination under Article 7, AliExpress reserves the right to bring legal proceedings against any User as AliExpress feels is necessary or as required or permitted under law. AliExpress further reserves the right to report Users and disclose any information relating to Users’ accounts, streaming and commenting activity to law enforcement authorities if it deems necessary or if it is required or permitted under applicable law.

Article 7 \[Termination\]
-------------------------

In addition to any of the penalties that may be imposed (as set out in the Violation Handling Overview), the account of any Live Streamer or Merchant Streamers may be terminated immediately in the following circumstances:

1、no longer satisfying the admission criteria specified in Article 3 of these regulations.

2、being subject to termination as listed in the Violation Handling Overview.

3、violating any applicable laws and regulations or guidelines.

4、no live broadcasting activity within three months.

5、streamer has been convicted of a serious crime or offense anywhere in the world or has engaged in violent or illegal acts whether offline or online on any online platform in the opinion of AliExpress.

Article 8 \[Reinstatement after Termination\]
---------------------------------------------

Live Streamer or Merchant Streamer whose account is:

1、terminated under Article 7.1 or 7.4 may apply for reinstatement.

2、terminated under Article 7.2 will be subject to the provisions listed in the Violation Handling Overview.

3、terminated under Article 7.3 or 7.5 will not be allowed to apply for reinstatement.

Any reinstatement shall be at the sole and absolute discretion of AliExpress and AliExpress is not obligated to approve any reinstatement application.

Article 9 \[Exclusion of Liability\]
------------------------------------

ALIEXPRESS AND ITS AFFILIATED COMPANIES EXCLUDE THEIR LIABILITY FOR ALL ACTIONS THAT THEY MAY TAKE IN RESPONSE TO VIOLATIONS OF THESE REGULATIONS. THE ACTIONS THAT ALIEXPRESS AND ITS AFFILIATED COMPANIES MAY TAKE ARE NOT LIMITED TO THOSE DESCRIBED ABOVE, AND ALIEXPRESS AND ITS AFFILIATED COMPANIES MAY TAKE ANY OTHER ACTION THAT THEY REASONABLY DEEM APPROPRIATE. THE USER SHALL INDEMNIFY ALIEXPRESS AND ITS AFFILIATED COMPANIES ON DEMAND AGAINST ALL CLAIMS, DEMANDS, LIABILITIES, LOSSES, DAMAGES, COSTS AND EXPENSES ARISING DIRECTLY OR INDIRECTLY FROM A BREACH OF THESE REGULATIONS OR AS A RESULT OF ANY ACT OR OMISSION OF THE USER IN RELATION TO THE USE OF ALIEXPRESS LIVE.

Article 10 \[Revision\]
-----------------------

AliExpress reserves the right to update these regulations time to time and the revised regulations will be published on [https://rule.aliexpress.com](https://rule.aliexpress.com/). If Users do not agree to these updated regulations, they should immediately stop using any of the functions available on AliExpress Live. Continued use of the platform indicates acceptance of the revised regulations.

AliExpress Review Policy

Release date: July 31, 2024

Revision date: September 11, 2025

  

1\. Scope of application
========================

In order to ensure that every user of the AliExpress.com platform (referred to in this policy as "AliExpress" or the "Platform") can enjoy a fair and honest shopping experience, and to maintain a fair and competitive business environment, AliExpress has established this review policy (the “**Review Policy**”).

This Review Policy applies to all users of the Platform who submit for publication on the Platform any form of comment, evaluation, opinion, recommendation or rating about an experience with a product, a seller or the Platform (such user being a “**Reviewer**” and their comment, evaluation, opinion, recommendation or rating being a “**Review**”). This Review Policy sets out certain rules which all Reviewers, and the Reviews they submit, must comply with.

This Review Policy does not apply to feedback and/or complaints from users which are not intended for publication. To open a dispute or submit a report about a seller, please click [here](https://www.aliexpress.com/p/seller-report/nav.html). For any other support, please contact our help centre [here](https://helpcenter.aliexpress.com/s/BuyerHelp?spm=a2g0o.home.sitefooter.1.33f16278V1Kb6k&language=en_US&tsuCode=ByrCmn&terminal=pc&region=UK&suid=1030142508201815392141239C3682).

2\. How to submit a Review
==========================

A user may submit a Review in relation to a completed order by clicking on "Write a review" within the "My orders" page when logged into their AliExpress account. Logged in users may also submit answers through the app about products they have purchased, which may constitute a Review (if the definition in section 1 above is met), in response to other users' questions.

Reviewers should submit Reviews with the following purposes in mind:

1) to provide sellers with honest feedback regarding their experience with the relevant product; and

2) to help other buyer users obtain genuine information about products.

3\. Review Rules
================

All Reviews must reflect the Reviewer’s genuine experience with a product purchased on the Platform, a seller on the Platform or another aspect of the Platform and meet the requirements of applicable laws and regulations, as well as the [AliExpress Community Guidelines](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/137261302).

The following practices are **not permitted** on the Platform:

**(1) Submission of fake Reviews**, being Reviews which are not based on the Reviewer’s genuine experience of a product purchased on the Platform, a seller on the Platform or another aspect of the Platform.

**(2) Submission of incentivised Reviews**, being Reviews provided in exchange for rewards by sellers or third parties (such as money, coupons, gift cards, free or discounted products, etc.) and Reviews from or on behalf of individuals with a financial interest in the product or seller.

**(3) Submission of malicious Reviews**, being Reviews intended to damage a seller’s reputation or business which are not isolated, genuine Reviews.

**(4) Aggregation of hijacked Reviews**, which means the aggregation of Reviews which represent that they relate to a particular product, when in reality they relate to a different product.

Users who suspect that a Review contravenes this Review Policy may report that review to us for further investigation by clicking on the ellipsis provided next that Review.

4\. Violations and penalties
============================

AliExpress will remove any fake, incentivised, malicious and/or hijacked Reviews identified on the Platform, as well as any other Reviews which AliExpress deems to violate this Review Policy. Where applicable, AliExpress will update a seller’s or product’s average rating and review count to exclude any removed Reviews.

AliExpress may also take further action against violations of this Review Policy, including but not limited to by taking one or more of the following steps in relation to a product or a seller:

1) demoting search rankings for products where necessary as a result of any updated average rating;

2) banning user accounts;

3) banning users from leaving Reviews;

4) disapplying Review functionalities in relation to certain products;

5) removing all Reviews for a seller or a product;

6) delisting product listings;

7) refunding orders which were placed in reliance on a Review which breaches this Review Policy; and/or

8) where a seller is engaging in the submission of Reviews which breach this Review Policy, imposing a penalty on the seller which is proportionate, in AliExpress’ reasonable opinion, to the severity of the violation, determined as follows:

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| **Violation Category** | **Penalty Measures** |
| Minor Violation | 6 points |
| Moderate Violation | 12 points |
| Serious Violation | 24 points |
| Particularly Severe Violation | 48 points |

For more information on the measures that we may take based on the points accumulated, please refer to the [AliExpress "Credit and Sales Manipulation" Rules Supplemental Explanation](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/137340756).

AliExpress

[1\. Scope of application](#Lruv2)

[2\. How to submit a Review](#kDccX)

[3\. Review Rules](#noquL)

[4\. Violations and penalties](#lAbhV)
