Illustration of Search Related Violations and Enforcement Actions

In order to ensure the search experience of buyers and provide a fair competition environment for sellers, AliExpress Platform will continuously take efforts against search related violations.

AliExpress Platform will monitor and take enforcement actions against search related violations according to this Illustration of Search Related Violations and Enforcement Actions (these “**Rules**”).

PART I DISPLAY OF PRODUCT INFORMATION: ABUSE IN POSTING
=======================================================

Chapter I Categories Put Wrong
------------------------------

### 1.1. Definition

“Catogries Put Wrong”refers to the product category selected or set to post a product is inconsistent with the actual category of the product, for instance, the product category selected or set for “fabric” is “wedding dress” and the special transaction items such as gifts / additional shipping fees / price difference / VIP / drop shipping are not categorized as other special categories.  
“Catogries Put Wrong”may result in display of the product on the website under a wrong category. The AliExpress Platform will regulate and deal with the problems of product categorization. Please note that you are required to check your product categorization and rectify the wrong category, and to select / fill in the correct category information for newly posted products.

### 1.2 Enforcement Actions against “Catogries Put Wrong”

Enforcement actions includes adjusting search rankings, deleting the products and taking the products off shelves will be taken against the products displayed under the wrong categories. Measures of adjusting search rankings will be taken against all products or part of the products (including products involved in “Catogries Put Wrong” and products not involved in “Catogries Put Wrong”) in a store whose products listed in violation of these Rules reach a certain amount. In the case of serious violation, all products in the store will be blocked. In the case of significant violation, the seller’s account will be frozen or closed.

### 1.3 Illustrations (including but not limited to the following)

#### 1.3.1“Catogries Put Wrong” Example 1

Example: NuBra is wrongly put under the category of dress.

Example: Frame case is wrongly put under the category of watchband.

#### 1.3.2 “Catogries Put Wrong” Example 2: special links for payment such as links for additional shipping fees / price difference / VIP

Special links (such as special order links for a specific customer, additional shipping fees / price differences, balance payment or refund, special links for payment, discount or coupon, customized commodity, down payment, AE gift card, gift, mobile top-up, overseas warehousing, presale and other special links) are not put under the designated special categories in compliance with the relevant rules.

Example: Links for additional shipping fees / price difference are put under the category of tools and other categories, instead of special category.

Chapter 2 Title Description Violation
-------------------------------------

### 2.1 Definition

Title Description Violation refers to abuse of key words of titles, such as titles with unclear product names, titles with repetitious keywords, product names in titles inconsistent with actual product names, titles inconsistent with categories, brand names in titles inconsistent with actual brand names and units in titles inconsistent with available units in stock, etc.

### 2.2 Enforcement Actions against Title Description Violation

Enforcement actions including adjusting search rankings, deleting the products and taking the products off shelves will be taken against the products involved in Title Description Violation. Measures of adjusting search rankings will be taken against all products or part of the products (including products involved in violation and products not involved in violation) in a store whose posted products in violation of these Rules reach a certain amount. In the case of serious violation, all products in the store will be blocked. In the case of significant violation, the seller’s account will be frozen or closed.

### 2.3 Illustrations (including but not limited to the following)

#### 2.3.1 Title abuse

Product names in titles are inconsistent with the actual product names.

Example: the actual products are hairpin, but the word “Headband” appears in the title.

#### 2.3.2 Titles with repetitious words

Keywords are repeatedly used in product title description.

Example: keyword “Shoes” is repeatedly used in product title description.

Chapter 3 Attributes Select Wrong
---------------------------------

### 3.1 Definition

Attributes Select Wrong refers to the product attribute selected is inconsistent with the actual attribute of the product, although the category of the product posted is correctly selected.

Attributes Select Wrong may result in display of the products on the website under a wrong attribute. The AliExpress Platform will regulate and rectify those products containing wrong attributes. Please note that you are required to check your product attributes and rectify the wrong ones, and to select / fill in the correct attribute information for newly posted products.

### 3.2 Enforcement Actions against Attributes Select Wrong

Enforcement actions including adjusting search rankings, deleting the products and taking the products off shelves will be taken against the products involved Attributes Select Wrong. Measures of adjusting search rankings will be taken against all products or part of the products (including products involved in violation and products not involved in violation) in a store whose posted products in violation of these Rules reach a certain amount. In the case of serious violation, all products in the store will be blocked. In the case of significant violation, the seller’s account will be frozen or closed.

### 3.3 Illustrations (including but not limited to the following)

#### 3.3.1 Attributes Select Wrong Examples

Example: the neckline of the product is round neck, but the seller posts it as "V-Neck ".

Chapter 4 Repeated Posting of Products
--------------------------------------

### 4.1 Definition

Repeated Posting of Products refers to the products information posted is identical with or substantially similar in terms of main information (such as image, title, price, attribute, etc.) with other products posted in the same store or in other stores opened by the same seller or by the same entity as identified by the AliExpress Platform o based on multiple factors.

Please be reminded that Repeated Posting of Products is strictly prohibited. The seller shall avoid directly using the main images of the posted products or copying the titles and attributes of the posted products when posting new products. In addition to showing the differences in the main images, the seller shall also fill in key information on the products such as title, attribute and other detailed description.

### 4.2 Enforcement Actions against Repeated Posting of Products

Enforcement actions including adjusting search rankings, deleting the products and taking the products off shelves will be taken against the products involved in Repeated Posting of Products. Measures of adjusting search rankings will be taken against all or part of the products (including products which violate these Rules and products which do not violate these Rules) in a store whose posted products in violation of these Rules reach a certain amount. In the case of serious violation, all products in the store will be blocked. In the case of extremely serious violation, the seller’s account will be frozen or closed.

### 4.3 Illustrations (including but not limited to the following)

#### 4.3.1 Repeated Posting of Products Example 1: Repeated Posting of Products with same main image

Example: for the same product in the same store, if the main image of one product is exactly the same as the other and their titles, attributes, prices and other information are substantially similar, the product would be identified as Repeated Posting of Products.

#### 4.3.2 Repeated Posting of Products Example 2: Repeated Posting of Products with different angle/background/color, etc.

Example: for the same product in the same store, if the main images of the product are only different in shooting angle or background, and the attributes, price and other information of one product is substantially similar to the other, the product would be identified as Repeated Posting of Products.

#### 4.3.3 Repeated Posting of Products Example 3: multiple stores opened by the same seller or same entity identified by AliExpress Platform based on multiple factors post or sell the same product repeatedly.

Example: if the main images of the products are only different in color, and their attributes, prices and other information are substantially similar, the product would be identified as Repeated Posting of Products.

Chapter 5 Other Description Violations
--------------------------------------

### 5.1 Definition

Other Description Violations refer to non-standard display of product information which does not constitute Categories Put Wrong, Title Description Violation, Attributes Select Wrong or Repeated Posting of Products, which includes that: 1) the main images of products do not conform to the required standard, such as images comprising text only, images that may cause discomfort; 2) the measurement units of products do not follow the typical standard for sale, for instance, shoes are not sold in pairs; or 3) units of products posted are inconsistent with available units in stock and other descriptions which may easily lead to buyers’ complaints. For example, units of the product posted are 100pcs/lot while the units in stock are only 50pcs

### 5.2 Enforcement Actions against Other Description Violations

Enforcement actions including adjusting search rankings, deleting the products and taking the products off shelves will be taken against the products involved in Other Description Violations. Measures of adjusting search rankings will be taken against all products or part of the products (including products involved in violation and products not involved in violation) in a store whose posted products in violation of these Rules reach a certain amount. In the case of serious violation, all products in the store will be blocked. In the case of significant violation, the seller’s account will be frozen or closed.

If Other Description Violations also constitute other improper posting actions provided in Article 86 (6) of the AliExpress Platform Rules for the AliExpress Sellers, the AliExpress Platform also has the right to take actions against the seller pursuant to this Article 86 (6).

PART II PRICE RELATED VIOLATIONS
================================

Chapter 1 Unfair Low Price
--------------------------

### 1.1 Definition

Unfair Low Price refers to the fact that a seller posts a product at a low price which deviates substantially from the regular sale price of the product.

### 1.2 Enforcement Actions against Unfair Low Price

Enforcement actions include adjusting search rankings, deleting the products and taking the products off shelves will be taken against the products involved in Unfair Low Price. Measures of adjusting search rankings will be taken against all products or part of the products (including products involved in violation and products not involved in violation) in a store whose posted products in violation of these Rules reach a certain amount. In the case of serious violation, all products in the store will be blocked. In the case of significant violation, the seller’s account will be frozen or closed.

If a seller involves in a large amount of Unfair Low Price violations, the AliExpress Platform also has the right to take actions against the seller pursuant to the AliExpress Rules for Unfair Low Price Competition.

### 1.3 Illustrations (including but not limited to the following types)

#### 1.3.1 Unfair Low Price Example 1

The product usually sold at a price of more than US$30 is posted for sale at a low price that deviates substantially from the regular sale price.

Chapter 2 Unfair High Price
---------------------------

### 2.1 Definition

Unfair High Price refers to the fact that a seller posts a product at a high price which deviates substantially from the regular sale price of the product.

### 2.2 Enforcement Actions against Unfair High Price

Enforcement actions including adjusting search rankings, deleting the products and taking the products off shelves will be taken against the products involved in Unfair High Price. Measures of adjusting search rankings will be taken against all products or part of the products (including products involved in violation and products not involved in violation) in a store whose posted products in violation of these Rules reach a certain amount. In the case of serious violation, all products in the store will be blocked. In the case of significant violation, the seller’s account will be frozen or closed.

### 2.3 Illustrations (including but not limited to the following types)

#### 2.3.1 Unfair High Price Example 1

Example: the sale price of the Bikini Set is abnormal, which significantly deviates from the regular sale price.

Chapter 3 Low Price with High Shipping Fee
------------------------------------------

### 3.1 Definition

Low Price with High Shipping Fee refers to a low price set for the product with a high shipping fee which deviates from the regular shipping fees.

### 3.2 Enforcement Actions against Low Price with High Shipping Fee

Enforcement actions including adjusting search rankings, deleting the products and taking the products off shelves will be taken against the products involved in Low Price with High Shipping Fee. Measures of adjusting search rankings will be taken against all products or part of the products (including products involved in violation and products not involved in violation) in a store whose posted products in violation of these Rules reach a certain amount. In the case of serious violation, all products in the store will be blocked. In the case of significant violation, the seller’s account will be frozen or closed.

### 3.3 Illustrations (including but not limited to the following types)

#### 3.3.1 Low Price with High Shipping Fee Example

Example: the shipping fee is abnormally high, which may easily leads to buyers’ complaints.

Chapter 4 Wrong SKU
-------------------

### 4.1 Definition

Wrong SKU refers to abuse of SKU setting features (such as setting specifications, quantities, units, shipping fees and other information in an abnormal manner, or changing key product elements through setting of SKU) by the seller to post SKUs in high or low price that deviates from the regular price, or to post SKUs that are not available for sale (including not available for sale in a normal manner) or delivery.

### 4.2 Enforcement Actions against Wrong SKU

Enforcement actions including adjusting search rankings, deleting the products and taking the products off shelves will be taken against the products displayed under the wrong categories. Measures of adjusting search rankings will be taken against all products or part of the products (including products involved in violation and products not involved in violation) in a store whose products listed in violation of these Rules reach a certain amount. In the case of serious violation, all products in the store will be blocked. In the case of significant violation, the seller’s account will be frozen or closed.  
If Wrong SKU also constitutes other improper posting specified in Article 86 (6) of the AliExpress Rules for the AliExpress Sellers, as applicable, the AliExpress Platform also has the right to take actions against the seller pursuant to this Article 86 (6).

### 4.3 Illustrations (including but not limited to the following types)

#### 4.3.1 Example 1 - zero inventory SKU: the inventory of a product’s SKU is set as 0 so that buyers are not able to purchase the product.

#### 4.3.2 Example 2 – no real product for the SKU: the SKU is set without a real product, for instance, there exists no product image or no product size, and the SKU is described with vague words and expressions such as “freight”, “None” or "Other".

Example: the lowest price is set for the SKU without specific size in order to attract more traffic to the product.

#### 4.3.3 Example 3 - SKUs in different categories: products in different categories (for instance, main parts and spare parts, a set of commodities and single items, tops and pants) are set as one product’s SKUs.

#### 4.3.4 Example 4 - SKUs with different functions / of different materials: products (i) with different functions / of different materials and (ii) with large price differences (for instance, electric and non-electric products, PU and real leather products, high-end and low-end products) are set as one product’s SKUs.

#### 4.3.5 Example 5 - “Wrong SKU” of overseas warehouse: products set with overseas warehouse cannot be delivered to the country where the overseas warehouse is located, or the setting of overseas warehouse is used to set low product price with high shipping fees, etc.

Example: products set with overseas warehouse cannot be delivered to the country where the overseas warehouse is located, for instance, a product can be shipped from “United States” but cannot be delivered to the United States.

Example: the setting of overseas warehouse is used to set low product price with high shipping fees, for instance, the price of the product shipped from China is US$10.08 with no shipping fee, and the price of the same product (in the same type and size) shipped from the United States is US$5.11 with a shipping fee of US$12.62, and the same product (in the same type and size) shipped from the United States with a price of US$5.11 cannot be delivered to countries other than the United States (prices are for display purposes only).

#### 4.3.6 Example 6 - SKU set with abnormal price: some SKUs are set with abnormal prices which are obviously much higher or lower than the regular prices. For example, the price of the product in normal size and color is set at US$1 while the price of the same product in some other size and color is set at more than USD$400,000.

#### 4.3.7 Example 7 - SKU with different quantity units: quantity units (such as the number of pieces) are set for non-quantity unit SKUs with large price differences, or the product is posted with abnormal quantity units, for instance, color options are set with different number of pieces instead of different colors and the price difference for different color options is relatively large; the products that shall be sold in pairs are set with the SKU of a single item of one pair and the SKU of one pair of the product.

Example: color options are set with different number of pieces, and the price difference between different color options is large and the lowest price does not match the product details displayed in the main product picture, which may easily lead to buyers’ complaints.

Example: for the products that are usually sold in pairs, one piece of the pair of the product and one pair of the product are set in the same product link.

#### 4.3.8 Any other abnormal SKU settings with large price differences, which may affect buyers’ search and shopping experience.

PART III TRANSACTION RELATED VIOLATIONS
=======================================

Chapter 1 Credit Sale Hype Up
-----------------------------

### 1\. Credit Sale Hype Up

#### 1.1 Definition

Credit Sale Hype Up refers to increasing sales of a product and credit rating by abnormal means of transaction.

#### 1.2 Enforcement Actions against Credit Sale Hype Up

1.2.1 If Credit Sale Hype Up is committed for the first time, the AliExpress Platform will delete the relevant credit and sales, adjust the search rankings, delete the product, take the product off shelves, close the relevant order and refund the money, and deduct 6 points/time, 12 points/time, 24 points/time or 48 points/time or close the seller’s account depending on the seriousness of violation.

1.2.2 If Credit Sale Hype Up is committed for the second time or more, the AliExpress Platform has the right to close the seller’s account directly regardless of the seriousness of violation. If the AliExpress Platform does not take actions to close the seller’s account, it has the right to take other enforcement actions, including deleting the relevant credit and sales, adjusting the search rankings, deleting the product, taking the product off shelves, closing the relevant order and refunding the money, and deducting the points.

The AliExpress Platform will announce on a regular basis of enforcement actions against sellers that have committed Credit Sale Hype Up, and will, at all costs, take all measures against sellers that sell fake and inferior products using their credit rating obtained through Credit Sale Hype Up and take legal actions against such sellers. Please note that the AliExpress Platform highly values integrity and every seller must uphold this value.

Chapter 2 Product Change
------------------------

### 2.1 Definition

Product Change refers to change of product through editing the key attributes of a product that has been posted for sale such as category, brand, model, configuration, material and function, etc, which results in the change of the posted product into another product. The seller shall post a new product if the product is upgraded. Editing of a product that has been posted for sale due to upgrade of the product will be regarded as Product Change.

### 2.2 Enforcement Actions against Product Change

Enforcement actions including adjusting search rankings, deleting the products and taking the products off shelves will be taken against the products involved in Product Change. Measures of adjusting search rankings will be taken against all products or part of the products (including products involved in violation and products not involved in violation) in a store whose posted products in violation of these Rules reach a certain amount. In the case of serious violation, all products in the store will be blocked. In the case of significant violation, the seller’s account will be frozen or closed.

### 2.3 Illustrations (including but not limited to the following types)

#### 2.3.1 Example 1: product A is changed to product B of a completely different category.

(a): The product originally posted for sale is socks while the product currently displayed for sale is T-shirt.

(b): The product originally posted for sale is night lamp while the product currently displayed for sale is crystal light.

(c): The products originally posted for sale are tissues and sofas (posted in one and the same product ID, which is an example of Wrong SKU) while the products currently displayed for sale are sofas.

#### 2.3.2 Example 2: product A is changed to product B of a completely different brand.

(a): The products originally posted for sale are Nike sneakers while the products currently displayed for sale are Adidas sneakers.

#### 2.3.3 Example 3: product A is changed to product B of a completely different model, or the refurbished product is changed to a brand-new product.

(a): The product originally posted for sale is iPhone 6 while the product currently displayed for sale is iPhone 6s.

(b): The product originally posted for sale is refurbished iPhone while the product currently displayed for sale is brand new iPhone.

#### 2.3.4 Example 4: product A is changed to product B with a different configuration

(a): The products originally posted for sale are toys without remote control function while the products currently displayed for sale are toys with remote control function.

(b): The products originally posted for sale are PU shoes while the products currently displayed for sale are genuine leather shoes.

In the event of inconsistency, ambiguity or conflict between the English and the non-English version of these rules, the English version shall prevail.

AliExpress Rules of Prohibited and Controlled Items - A Detailed Guidance

Release date: July 30, 2024

Revision date: November 5, 2025

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| (I) Illicit Drugs, Drug Precursors, and Paraphernalia |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |
| 【Overview】<br><br>AliExpress strictly prohibits the posting of any information related to illicit drugs, narcotics, tranquilizers, psychotropic substances, medicinal toxic drugs, precursors, drug paraphernalia and tools for drug manufacturing, detoxification drugs, and medical institution preparations. AliExpress members are required to comply with AliExpress' product listing rules and post information based on the actual product conditions. Violators will face penalties under national laws and regulations and the platform rules.<br><br>The platform imposes strict control over prohibited goods. Goods that contain raw materials for drug manufacturing, drug components, or substances with drug components, even if not specified in national laws and regulations, may incur penalties. AliExpress reserves the right to modify and supplement the provided list.<br><br>【Related Articles and Latest Announcements】<br><br>[AliExpress Warning Announcement on the Strict Prohibition of the Sale of Fentanyl Substances](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/156158201?spm=a2g3p.rule_index.0.0.4b21RFlvRFlv06)<br><br>[AliExpress Announcement on the Rectification of Product Information Containing the Word "Marijuana"](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/156158314)<br><br>[AliExpress Announcement on the Prohibition of the Sale of Certain Products to Russia](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/156160134)<br><br>[AliExpress Announcement on the Prohibition of the Sale of Tablet Presses](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/156158572?spm=a2g3p.rule_index.0.0.4b21RFlvRFlv06)<br><br>[AliExpress Interpretation of Rules Regarding Drug Paraphernalia](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/156159047?spm=a2g3p.rule_index.0.0.4b21RFlvRFlv06)<br><br>【Reference List】<br><br>AliExpress prohibits the posting of any narcotic drug-related information. The following list is provided by a third party for reference only. AliExpress does not guarantee the completeness, accuracy, or timeliness of the content.<br><br>Click to download: [Narcotic Drugs Catalog and Psychotropic Substances Catalog (2013).doc](http://img.alibaba.com/kf/HTB1_TKdHpXXXXXKXVXX8i0XFXXX4.doc)<br><br>Click to download: [Supplementary List of Non-Medical Narcotic Drugs and Psychotropic Substances (2015).xlsx](http://img.alibaba.com/kf/HTB1uKzaJVXXXXbwXpXXCV8eFXXXD.xlsx)<br><br>Click to download: [Supplementary List of Non-Medical Narcotic Drugs and Psychotropic Substances (2021](https://files.alicdn.com/tpsservice/8336d9f9710bbf3ba3d450121366058d.xlsx))<br><br>Click to download: [List of Precursors.xlsx](https://office-cn-shanghai.imm.aliyuncs.com/office/w/69847c5763d8e17d3f488bbbaa5805bd90a467af?_w_tokentype=1#6edd) |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |
| 1、Narcotics, Tranquilizers, Psychotropic Drugs, Natural Drugs, Synthetic Drugs, and Class I Precursor Chemicals |     |     |     |     |     | Serious Violation: up to 48 Points Deduction |     |     |     |     |     |
| \*\*\*Regulatory Basis\*\*\*<br><br>In compliance with Chinese laws and regulations such as the Criminal Law of the People's Republic of China, Drug Control Law of the People's Republic of China, Anti-Dope Regulations, Regulations on the Control of Anesthetic and Psychotropic Drugs, Notice on the Control of Non-Medical Narcotic Drugs and Psychotropic Drugs, The Measures Regarding the Administration of Drug Information Service over the Internet, and Regulations on the Administration of Precursor Chemicals; the Anabolic Steroid Control Act of 2004, Uniform Controlled Substances Act, and DEA List of Chemicals in the United States of America; the Misuse of Drugs Act 1971 in the United Kingdom, and international policies and regulations such as the United Nations Convention on Psychotropic Substances and Convention Against Illicit Traffic in Narcotic Drugs and Psychotropic Substances, the posting of information on anesthetic drugs, psychotropic drugs, medicinal toxic drugs, radioactive drugs, detoxification drugs, and medical institution preparations is prohibited.<br><br>This basis is for reference only and does not guarantee completeness, accuracy, or timeliness. AliExpress reserves the right to modify and supplement the content.<br><br>Related Links:<br><br>[DEA information on illegal drugs](http://www.justice.gov/dea/pubs/abuse/)<br><br>[DEA Controlled Substances](http://www.deadiversion.usdoj.gov/schedules/index.html)<br><br>[Controlled Substances Act](http://www.fda.gov/regulatoryinformation/legislation/ucm148726.htm)<br><br>[Title 21 of the Controlled Substances Act, which defines "drug paraphernalia"](http://www.deadiversion.usdoj.gov/21cfr/21usc/863.htm)<br><br>[FDA restrictions on "human growth hormone"](http://www.gpo.gov/fdsys/pkg/USCODE-2009-title21/html/USCODE-2009-title21-chap9-subchapIII-sec333.htm)<br><br>[FDA safety announcement on "human growth hormone"](http://www.fda.gov/Drugs/DrugSafety/ucm237773.htm)<br><br>[Federal Food, Drug, and Cosmetic Act](http://www.fda.gov/opacom/laws/fdcact/fdctoc.htm)<br><br>\*\*\*Reminder\*\*\*<br><br>AliExpress strictly prohibits the posting of any information on narcotics, anesthetic drugs, psychotropic substances, medicinal toxic drugs, etc. According to the[Regulations on the Administration of Precursor Chemicals](http://www.gov.cn/zhengce/content/2008-03/28/content_6314.htm), precursors are divided into three categories. Category I includes the main raw materials that can be used for drug manufacturing, and posting information about Category I products is a serious violation (48 points deduction per violation); Categories II and III include chemical agents that can be used for drug manufacturing.<br><br>Please comply with AliExpress' product listing rules and publish information based on the actual product conditions. Violators shall face penalties under national laws and regulations and the platform rules. The platform imposes strict control over prohibited goods. Goods that contain raw materials for drug manufacturing, drug components, or substances with drug components, even if not specified in the national regulations, may incur penalties.<br><br>\*\*\*Risk Examples\*\*\*<br><br>**·** Narcotic Drugs and Tranquilizers (e.g., cocaine, fentanyl, heroin, hydrocodone, lidocaine, morphine, oxycodone, pethidine, and propofol)<br><br>**·** Psychotropic Drugs (e.g., barbital, cathinone, mephedrone, modafinil, tapentadol, phentermine, tramadol, zopiclone, and flurazepam)<br><br>**·** Natural Drugs (e.g., kratom, salvia divinorum, peyote, and psilocybin mushroom)<br><br>**·** Synthetic Drugs (e.g., AB-CHMINACA, 5-MeO-DMT, JWH-018, HU-308, cannabicyclohexanol, and UR-144)<br><br>**·** Category I Precursors Chemicals (e.g., pseudoephedrine, ephedrine hydrochloride, and piperonal) |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |
| 2、Category II Precursors Chemicals, Steroids |     |     |     |     |     | General Violation: 6 Points Deduction per Violation |     |     |     |     |     |

According to the Regulations on the Administration of Precursor Chemicals, precursors chemicals are divided into three categories. | (II) Hazardous Chemicals |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |
| 【Overview】<br><br>AliExpress prohibits the posting of product information regarding toxic, highly toxic, flammable, explosive, radioactive, ozone-depleting substances, and other hazardous or dangerous chemicals.<br><br>The platform imposes strict control over hazardous chemicals. Those not listed in related national catalogs may still incur penalties. The following list is provided by a third party and is for reference only. AliExpress does not guarantee the completeness, accuracy, or timeliness of the content. AliExpress reserves the right to modify and supplement the following list.<br><br>References:<br><br>Catalog of Hazardous Chemicals in China (2015)<br><br>【Related Articles and Latest Announcements】<br><br>[Announcement on Adjustments to the Sale Prohibition and Control of Pesticides](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/160018994) |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |
| 1、Explosives and detonators; |     |     |     |     |     | Serious Violation: up to 48 Points Deduction;<br><br>General Violation: 6 Points Deduction per Violation |     |     |     |     |     |
| \*\*\*Regulatory Basis\*\*\*<br><br>The Criminal Law of the People's Republic of China, Regulations on the Safety Management of Hazardous Chemicals, the Catalog of Hazardous Chemicals in China (2015), the List of Explosive Materials (ATF) in the United States of America, and other laws and regulations worldwide.<br><br>This basis is for reference only and does not guarantee completeness, accuracy, or timeliness. AliExpress reserves the right to modify and supplement the content.<br><br>\*\*\*Reminder\*\*\*<br><br>AliExpress prohibits the posting of any product information related to explosives and detonators.<br><br>\*\*\*Risk Examples\*\*\*<br><br>Serious Violation (up to 48 points deduction)<br><br>Explosive substances (e.g., emulsion explosives, hexogen, and ammonium nitrate explosives)<br><br>General Violation (6 points deduction per violation) |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |

| (III) Firearms and Ammunition |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |
| 【Overview】<br><br>AliExpress prohibits the listing of biological, chemical, nuclear weapons, and other weapons of mass destruction, as well as any information that provides related services, instructions for use, consultation, production, and additives, and violates international law; and the listing of military weapons and equipment, firearms and ammunition and their main accessories, imitation guns and imitation crafts, and other hazardous products. |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |
| 1、Weapons of Mass Destruction, Real Guns, Ammunition, Military Equipment and Related Equipment |     |     |     |     |     | Serious Violation, Maximum 48 points Deduction |     |     |     |     |     |
| \*\*\*Regulatory basis\*\*\*<br><br>Treaty on the Non-Proliferation of Nuclear Weapons;<br><br>Arms Trade Treaty;<br><br>Convention on Conventional Weapons;<br><br>Program of Action to Prevent, Combat and Eliminate the Illicit Trade in Small Arms and Light Weapons in All Aspects;<br><br>Gun Control Law of the People's Republic of China;<br><br>Other relevant domestic and international laws and regulations.<br><br>This basis is for reference only and does not guarantee completeness, accuracy and timeliness. AliExpress reserves the right to modify and supplement the content.<br><br>\*\*\*Reminder\*\*\*<br><br>AliExpress prohibits the listing of any biological, chemical, nuclear weapons, and other weapons of mass destruction, as well as any information that provides services, instructions for use, consultation, production, and additives and violates any international laws; the listing of arms, military equipment or related equipment; and the listing of any firearms, ammunition and ammunition parts propelled by gas, chemicals or gunpowder.<br><br>\*\*\*Risk Examples\*\*\*<br><br>(1) Weapons of mass destruction: nuclear weapons, biological and chemical weapons and related equipment, accessories, etc.<br><br>(2) Arms: missiles, rocket systems and related equipment, main parts and accessories, etc.<br><br>(3) Military equipment: military radars, military transport vehicles, military drones, military communication equipment and systems and main parts, etc.<br><br>(4) Real guns: shotguns, pistols, submachine guns, starting guns, modified nail guns, electromagnetic coil guns, camouflage guns of any form, etc.<br><br>(5) Ammunition: land mines, naval mines, bombs, bullets, nail bullets, perforating bullets, artillery shells and projectiles, launching equipment, main parts such as propellant charges, ammunition belts, etc.<br><br>AliExpress imposes strict control over weapons of mass destruction, arms and related equipment. Those not listed in related national catalogs may still incur penalties. The following list is provided by a third party and is for reference only. AliExpress does not guarantee the completeness, accuracy and timeliness of the content.<br><br>For specific requirements and interpretations regarding the sale of firearms and firearm parts, please refer to the [Interpretation and Listing Specifications for Prohibition and Restriction on the Sale of Firearms and Parts](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/149215586).<br><br>References:<br><br>**·** United Nations Disarmament Affairs - Weapons<br><br>**·** Export Control List for Military Products of the People's Republic of China<br><br>**·** Regulations and List of Nuclear Export Control of the People's Republic of China |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |
| 2、Imitation Guns and Gun Parts |     |     |     |     |     | General Violation, 6 Points Deduction/Violation |     |     |     |     |     |
| \*\*\*Regulatory Basis\*\*\*<br><br>Law of the People's Republic of China on Control of Guns;<br><br>Notice of the Ministry of Public Security on Issuing the 'Identification Standards for Imitation Guns';<br><br>Notice of the Ministry of Public Security on Resolutely Prohibiting the Production and Sale of Imitation Pistols Such As Steel Ball Guns, Stun Guns, and Tear Gas Guns;<br><br>Notice of the Ministry of Public Security on Managing Paintball Guns as Firearms;<br><br>Other relevant laws and regulations.<br><br>This basis is for reference only and does not guarantee completeness, accuracy, or timeliness. AliExpress reserves the right to modify and supplement the content.<br><br>\*\*\*Reminder\*\*\*<br><br>AliExpress prohibits the listing of firearm products that meet the identification standards for imitation firearms as stipulated by Chinese law, as well as the main parts of real firearms or imitation firearms, including internal and external parts of firearms.<br><br>\*\*\*Risk Examples\*\*\*<br><br>(1) Imitation firearms (e.g., air guns, BB guns, paintball guns, steel ball guns, harpoon guns, pen guns, matchstick guns, and miniature cannons)<br><br>(2) Main parts of firearms (e.g., buttstocks, grips, firearm mounts, magazines, triggers, trigger guards, suppressors, flash suppressors, firearm springs, air gun actions, gas cylinders, firearm gases, air gun valve bodies, modified nail gun parts, internal parts of AirForce Condor air rifles, internal parts of PCP air rifles)<br><br>References:<br><br>[Law of the People's Republic of China on Control of Guns](https://flk.npc.gov.cn/detail2.html?MmM5MDlmZGQ2NzhiZjE3OTAxNjc4YmY3OGUwMTA3OGY)<br><br>[Notice from the Ministry of Public Security on Issuing the 'Identification Standards for Imitation Guns](https://www.gov.cn/zwgk/2008-02/27/content_902728.htm)'<br><br>[AliExpress Announcement on the Prohibition of the Sale of Auto/Motorcycle Parts Suspected of Being Convertible into Gun Silencers](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/180112229)<br><br>\*\*\*FAQs\*\*\*<br><br>Is it allowed to list BB pellets on AliExpress?<br><br>AliExpress prohibits the listing of bullets for real guns, lead pellets, and metal BB pellets. However, it is permissible to list plastic and soft bullets intended for toy guns, provided that the muzzle energy does not exceed the threshold defined in the imitation gun identification standards specified in the Identification Criteria for the Injurious Force of Firearms in Forensic Science (1.8 J/cm2). |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |
| 3、Potentially Hazardous Crafts |     |     |     |     |     | General Violation, 2 Points Deduction/Violation |     |     |     |     |     |
| \*\*\*Regulatory Basis\*\*\*<br><br>Relevant laws and regulations of China, Hong Kong, China, the US, Singapore and other countries and regions, as well as import and export regulations.<br><br>This basis is for reference only and does not guarantee completeness, accuracy and timeliness. However, you cannot list products or parts that are identified as imitation guns and related parts according to the Notice of the Ministry of Public Security on Issuing the 'Identification Standards for Imitation Guns'. |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |

| (Ⅵ) Medicinal Products |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |
| 【Overview】<br><br>AliExpress strictly prohibits the listing or sale of of medicinaldrugs products, including but not limited to prescription drugs, over-the-counter drugs, psychoactive drugs, toxic traditional Chinese medicinal materials, orally administered drugs containing prohibited ingredients, sex drugs, weight loss drugs, and health products.<br><br>The following list of control basis is provided by a third party and is for reference only. AliExpress does not guarantee the completeness, accuracy, or timeliness of the content, and reserves the right to modify/update and supplement the list and the specific control scope.<br><br>Related Links (for reference only):<br><br>[China National Medical Products Administration Database](https://www.nmpa.gov.cn/datasearch/home-index.html)<br><br>[China National Veterinary Drug Basic Information Database](http://vdts.ivdc.org.cn:8081/cx/)<br><br>[US FDA Database](https://www.accessdata.fda.gov/scripts/cder/daf/index.cfm?event=BasicSearch.process)<br><br>[European Medicines Agency (EMA) Medicine Query](https://www.ema.europa.eu/en/medicines)<br><br>For details about the controlled ingredients on AliExpress, refer to the [Prohibited Ingredient List](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/164875083) and [List of Ingredients Prohibited for Sale in Specific Countries](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/164875170). |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |
| 1、Prescription Drugs, Hormones, Radiopharmaceuticals, Special Pharmaceutical Products |     |     |     |     |     | General Violation, 12 Points Deduction/Violation |     |     |     |     |     |
| \*\*\*Regulatory Basis\*\*\*<br><br>In accordance with the Drug Administration Law of the People's Republic of China, Measures for the Administration of Internet Drug Information Services, Measures for the Administration of Toxic Drugs for Medical Use, Measures for the Administration of Radiopharmaceuticals, Regulations on the Administration of Narcotic Drugs and Psychotropic Drugs, and Regulations on the Administration of Blood Products, Internet websites are not allowed to publish product information related to narcotic drugs, psychotropic drugs, medicinal toxic drugs, radiopharmaceuticals, detoxification drugs, and medical institution preparations. According to the laws and regulations of the corresponding destination countries, medicinal products are prohibited or not suitable for online cross-border sales. The specific ban list and requirements are subject to the local laws and regulations of each country. Please also refer to the requirements and relevant information from regulatory authorities in the Chinese mainland, Hong Kong, and other countries and regions, such as the US (FDA) and the UK.<br><br>This basis is for reference only and does not guarantee completeness, accuracy, or timeliness. AliExpress reserves the right to modify/update and supplement the content.<br><br>\*\*\*Reminder\*\*\*<br><br>AliExpress strictly prohibits the listing or sale of of any prescription drug information. Prescription drugs refer to drugs regulated or approved by the national health administrative department, which must be prescribed by physicians or other licensed medical professionals and sold with prescriptions. They must be used under the supervision or guidance of physicians, pharmacists, or other medical professionals. These drugs mainly include drugs that may cause dependence, drugs with high toxicity, special drugs for specific diseases, and new drugs that require further observation of drug activity and side effects. Such drugs are subject to approval by medical institutions before use.<br><br>\*\*\*Risk Examples\*\*\*<br><br>Prescription drugs: aspirin, penicillin, lidocaine, Seroxat, etc.<br><br>Prescription veterinary drugs: antiviral drugs; antibiotics and synthetic antimicrobials; antipyretics and analgesics; compound preparations, etc. |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |

| (Ⅶ) Medical Devices |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |
| 【Overview】<br><br>Medical devices refer to instruments, equipment, appliances, materials, or other items intended to be used alone or in combination on the human body, including the necessary software. Their effects on the surface and inside the human body are not obtained by means of pharmacology, immunology, or metabolism, but these means may participate and play a certain auxiliary role. To strengthen the supervision and management of medical devices, ensure their safety and effectiveness, and safeguard human health and safety, China has formulated the Regulations on the Supervision and Administration of Medical Devices and implements classified management of medical devices.<br><br>Class I medical devices refer to medical devices for which conventional management is sufficient to ensure their safety and effectiveness.<br><br>Class II medical devices are those that need to be controlled to ensure their safety and effectiveness.<br><br>Class III medical devices are those that are implanted in the human body, used to support or sustain life, or present potential risks to the human body, for which strict controls are required to ensure their safety and effectiveness. AliExpress restricts the listing or sale of Class III medical device products.<br><br>The following list of control basis is provided by a third party and is for reference only. AliExpress does not guarantee the completeness, accuracy, or timeliness of the content, and reserves the right to modify/update and supplement the list and the specific control scope.<br><br>References:<br><br>[China National Medical Products Administration Database](https://www.nmpa.gov.cn/datasearch/home-index.html)<br><br>[China Medical Device Classification Catalog](https://www.nmpa.gov.cn/wwwroot/gyx02302/flml.htm)<br><br>href="https://www.accessdata.fda.gov/scripts/cdrh/cfdocs/cfpmn/pmn.cfm" U.S. FDA Medical Device Query - 510(k)<br><br>[U.S. FDA Medical Device Query - PMA](https://www.accessdata.fda.gov/scripts/cdrh/cfdocs/cfpma/pma.cfm)<br><br>[Canadian Medical Device Classification Catalog](https://www.canada.ca/en/health-canada/services/drugs-health-products/medical-devices/application-information/guidance-documents/guidance-document-guidance-risk-based-classification-system-non-vitro-diagnostic.html) |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |
| 1、Medical Consultation and Medical Services |     |     |     |     |     | General Violation, 6 Points Deduction/Violation |     |     |     |     |     |
| \*\*\*Regulatory Basis\*\*\*<br><br>The Regulations on the Supervision and Administration of Medical Devices, the Measures for the Administration of Internet Drug Information Services, and the requirements and relevant information from regulatory authorities in the Chinese mainland, Hong Kong, and other countries and regions, such as the US (FDA) and the UK.<br><br>This basis is for reference only and does not guarantee completeness, accuracy, or timeliness. AliExpress reserves the right to modify/update and supplement the content.<br><br>\*\*\*Reminder\*\*\*<br><br>AliExpress prohibits the posting of information related to medical or healthcare services, including medical consultation and medical tourism. The scope of services includes but is not limited to medical treatment, rehabilitation, vaccination, health check-ups, psychological counseling, nutrition, plastic surgery, and massage.<br><br>\*\*\*Risk Examples\*\*\*<br><br>Medical consultation services (e.g., medical treatment, rehabilitation, vaccination, health check-ups, psychological counseling, nutrition, plastic surgery, and massage)<br><br>Medical tourism services (e.g., overseas medical tourism) |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |

| 【Overview】<br><br>AliExpress strictly prohibits users from listing items related to the trade of human organs, live animals and plants protected by law and products, and tools used for illegal hunting and killing of animals. When listing items, users must comply with the Convention on International Trade in Endangered Species of Wild Fauna and Flora (CITES) and other international conventions, relevant laws and regulations of China, laws and regulations of their country/region and jurisdiction, and the website's specific rules.<br><br>【Related Articles and Latest Announcements】<br><br>[AliExpress' Compliance Notice on the Prohibition of the Sale of Animal Fur and Related Fur Products to California, USA](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/124114564) |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |

| \*\*\*Regulatory Basis\*\*\*<br><br>Regulations on Human Organ Transplantation;<br><br>Regulations on the Management of Human Genetic Resources;<br><br>Measures for the Management of Human Sperm Banks;<br><br>Measures for the Management of Human Assisted Reproductive Technology;<br><br>Other domestic and international laws and regulations, and general principles of international law and humanitarianism.<br><br>This basis is for reference only and does not guarantee completeness, accuracy, or timeliness. AliExpress reserves the right to modify and supplement the content.<br><br>\*\*\*Reminder\*\*\*<br><br>Please comply with relevant national laws and regulations and refrain from listing human skeletons, organs and body fluids, plastinated specimens from human bodies, and similar products for any purpose.<br><br>\*\*\*Risk Examples\*\*\*<br><br>Examples include but are not limited to human organs/remains/corpses, sperm/eggs, blood, and plastinated specimens from human bodies.<br><br>\*\*\*FAQs\*\*\*<br><br>Can human specimens used for medical and educational purposes be listed?<br><br>Specimens made of materials such as plastic and silicone for medical and educational purposes can be listed, but specimens from human organs and remains are strictly prohibited. |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |

| \*\*\*Regulatory Basis\*\*\*<br><br>Appendices I, II and III to the CITES (Sale of species listed on the appendices is prohibited.), as well as relevant laws and regulations such as the List of Key Protected Wild Plants and the Regulations on the Protection of Wild Plants of the People's Republic of China.<br><br>This basis is for reference only and does not guarantee completeness, accuracy, or timeliness. AliExpress reserves the right to modify and supplement the content.<br><br>\*\*\*Reminder\*\*\*<br><br>Please comply with the CITES, national laws and regulations, and platform rules. It is prohibited to sell plants protected by the CITES and related logs, sawn timber, timber, and wood chips.<br><br>\*\*\*Risk Examples\*\*\*<br><br>Cathaya argyrophylla, Taxaceae, Nostoc flagelliforme, agarwood, and sandalwood (including their logs, sawn timber, boards, wood chips, etc.).<br><br>【Related Articles and Latest Announcements】<br><br>[Announcement on the Prohibition of the Sale of Sky Lanterns and Seed/Potted Plant Products](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/156165432)<br><br>\*\*\*FAQs\*\*\*<br><br>Are listings of rosewood furniture allowed?<br><br>Rosewood furniture products can be listed, but rosewood lumber, sawn timber, boards, wood chips, etc., are prohibited from being listed. |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |
| Related Links:<br><br>**·** [CITES Official Website](https://cites.org/eng)<br><br>**·** [Endangered Species Scientific Commission of the People's Republic of China](http://cites.org.cn/)<br><br>**·** [Announcement from the Office of Endangered Species Import and Export Management of the People's Republic of China, General Administration of Customs](https://www.forestry.gov.cn/c/www/gsgg/26818.jhtml)<br><br>**·** [Catalog of Goods Prohibited from Export by China Customs](https://www.mee.gov.cn/xxgk2018/xxgk/xxgk10/202306/t20230608_1033209.html) |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |
| 5、Other Regulated Animals, Plants and Their Products |     |     |     |     |     | General Violation, 0 Points Deduction/Violation |     |     |     |     |     |
| \*\*\*Regulatory Basis\*\*\*<br><br>Requirements of major domestic and international regulatory bodies, such as CITES.<br><br>This basis is for reference only and does not guarantee completeness, accuracy, or timeliness. AliExpress reserves the right to modify and supplement the content.<br><br>\*\*\*Risk Examples\*\*\*<br><br>Some live wild animals, such as bats and wild civets, and their products |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |     |

AliExpress

- - -

AliExpress Index of Prohibited and Controlled Items

Release date: July 24, 2023

Revision date: October 21, 2025

**·** [1、Overview](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/127561551#MEl5q)

**·** [2、Index of Prohibited and Controlled Items](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/127561551#tWkUv)

**·** [3、Penalties for Violations](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/127561551#EWlTa)

**·** [4、Response to Reports and Complaints](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/127561551#etuQy)

1、Overview:
-----------

No information that contains or is suggestive of any prohibited or controlled items may be published on the platform. AliExpress has the right to punish any act in violation of these Rules in accordance with the AliExpress Index of Prohibited and Controlled Items.

Users shall not circumvent these Rules, other administrative provisions on prohibited goods published by the platform and the contents specified in the platform announcements by any means; otherwise, they may be subject to heavier penalty.

For principles of penalty and specific standards of point deduction, please refer to Penalties for Violations.

2、Index of Prohibited and Controlled Items
------------------------------------------

Platform users shall not post any products that are in violation of the legal or regulatory requirements of any countries, regions or jurisdictions on AliExpress.

AliExpress Index of Prohibited and Controlled Itemsis an index of certain prohibited or controlled items on the platform for users’ reference only. However, the completeness, timeliness and accuracy of such index is not guaranteed. The platform shall have the right to make any addition, deletion and modification to the following information in accordance with legal provisions, regulatory requirements and its own rules, while platform users shall have the obligation to ensure that the products posted by them do not violate the requirements of any jurisdiction.

Unless otherwise specified, the AliExpress Index of Prohibited and Controlled Items also apply to the publishing of information and the online transaction (“Online Transaction”) provided for in the Transaction Services Agreement.

AliExpress Index of Prohibited and Controlled Items also apply to the AliExpress sites in English and other languages.

For goods prohibited or controlled by the laws of certain countries and goods that are not suitable for cross-border sales due to their nature, please refer to the laws and regulations of such countries and the latest announcements of the platform.

If there is any discrepancy between the Chinese and English versions of any announcement or between the content of any announcement and other rules of AliExpress platforms, or if there is any other matter that is not detailed, AliExpress reserves the right of final explanation.

3、Penalties for Violations
--------------------------

The platform has the right to raise or mitigate the penalties depending on the severity of the violation, i.e., posting prohibited or controlled items, and the member’s acts.

Examples of malicious acts include but are not limited to evading system monitoring utilizing secretive means such as hiding, blocking or blurring product information, utilizing implicit description, or willfully through vague descriptions or deliberate mis-categorization; listing a large number of prohibited items at the same time; repeatedly publishing non-compliant information; maliciously testing the regulations. For malicious violations, the penalty will be raised depending on the severity. For example, the penalty will be doubled for a general violation, or in the case of serious violation, the relevant account will be closed.

Raised penalties for general violations: for a general violation that is identified as a malicious violation, the penalty will be raised (if the same violation occurs again, the penalty points will be doubled for the second time)

|     |     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Basis for Penalties** | **Violation** | **Severity/Frequency of Violation** | **Other Penalties** |
| AliExpress Index of Prohibited and Controlled Items | Listing prohibited and controlled items | Serious violation: 48 penalty points per violation (closure of account) | **·**Removal/deletion of the non-compliant information<br><br>**·**If AliExpress finds any involvement of any prohibited or controlled item in an order, AliExpress will close the order and, where the buyer has made the payment, refund the payment in full to the buyer regardless of the status of the logistics, in which case the seller shall be held solely liable. |
| General violation: 0.5-6 penalty points per violation (up to 12 penalty points within a day) |

The penalty points for violations of the rules on prohibited and controlled items and for general infringements of intellectual property rights will be calculated accumulatively. Penalties against accounts will be implemented once the accumulated points reach a threshold.

|     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Violation** | **Threshold of Penalty Points** | **Penalty** |
| Violations of the rules on intellectual property rights and prohibited and controlled items | 2   | Serious warning |
| 6   | Restriction on product listing for 3 days |
| 12  | Account freezing for 7 days |
| 24  | Account freezing for 14 days |
| 36  | Account freezing for 30 days |
| 48  | Account closure |

**Notes:**

1\. General violation: The cumulative penalty points shall not exceed 12 points within a day (i.e., within 24 hours from the first violation’s penalty);

2\. Serious violation: 48 penalty points per violation and closure of account;

3\. All online products and removed products are within the scope of sampling inspection of the platform. In case of any violation, penalties will be imposed pursuant to relevant rules;

4\. The items listed above which are not suitable for trading on AliExpress are not exhaustive. AliExpress will adjust the scope of such items from time to time.

5\. In case of extremely serious violations such as malicious evasion (including but not limited to evading platform management utilizing secretive means such as hiding, blocking or blurring product information; penalties having been imposed on an account user or other accounts controlled by the user due to serious violations in the reasonable judgment of the platform; investigations having been conducted by domestic or foreign regulatory authorities on any account user or other accounts controlled by the user; or although the violation has not been filed for investigation, the platform reasonably believes that there is major suspect or any other situation that has a serious impact on the management order of the platform or causes certain negative impacts), the platform reserves the right to deduct 48 penalty points and close the account.
