PART 1 GENERAL PROHIBITIONS
---------------------------

1.1 You may not post or sell any item that is restricted or prohibited by a federal, state or local law in any country or jurisdiction. Please be aware that the AliExpress e-commerce platform including but not limited to the web and mobile-optimized versions of the websites identified by the uniform resource locator “www.aliexpress.com”, “www.aliexpress.ru” and “www.tmall.ru”, and the mobile applications of the AliExpress e-commerce platforms (collectively the “AliExpress Sites” or the “AliExpress”), which

functions as a global marketplace; thus the selling or posting of items may be controlled or prohibited because of laws of the relevant jurisdictions. Below, we have listed some categories of prohibited or restricted items. HOWEVER, THIS LIST IS NOT INTENDED TO BE EXHAUSTIVE; YOU, AS THE SELLER, YOU AND YOUR AFFILIATES ARE RESPONSIBLE FOR ENSURING THAT YOU ARE FOLLWING ANY RELATED LAW AND REGULATIONS in any jurisdiction, especially the country of departure and the country of destination and applicable international conventions, including labor laws and standards, such as the Forced Labor Convention, 1930 and the Abolition of Forced Labor Convention, 1957. Your obligations may include but not limited to attaching any license/product certificate/testing report required, APPLlYING FOR any registration needed and NOT POSTING ANY ITEM THAT IS PROHIBITED. Unless otherwise indicated and annotated accordingly below, the list of prohibited or restricted items as listed shall be applicable to the AliExpress.

For the purposes of this Product Listing Policy, transactions which are supported by AliExpress shall be “Relevant Online Transactions”.

1.2 AliExpress has chosen to also prohibit the posting of items which may not be restricted or prohibited by law but are nonetheless controversial including:  
(a) Items that encourage illegal activities (e.g. lock pick tools, synthetic urine for cheating drug tests);  
(b) Items that are racially, religiously or ethnically derogatory, or that promote hatred, violence, racial or religious intolerance;  
(c) Giveaways, lotteries, raffles, or contests;  
(d) Stocks, bonds, investment interests, and other securities;  
(e) Pornographic materials or items that are sexual in nature;  
(f) Items that do not offer a physical product or service for sale, such as digital currencies and advertisements solely for the purpose of collecting user information.  
1.3 AliExpress, in its sole and exclusive discretion, reserves the right to impose additional restrictions and prohibitions.

1.4 In the event of inconsistency, ambiguity or conflict of the contents of this policy with any other terms of the AliExpress Sites, or between the English and other language versions of this policy, the English version and the decision of AliExpress exercised in its absolute discretion shall always prevail.  
Top

PART 2 PROHIBITED AND CONTROLLED ITEMS
--------------------------------------

### 1\. ILLICIT DRUGS, PRECURSORS AND DRUG PARAPHERNALIA

1.1 AliExpress expressly forbids any and all listing or sale of narcotics, tranquilizers, psychotropic drugs, natural drugs, synthetic drugs, steroids and other controlled substances (including all drugs listed in Schedules I, II, III, IV or V of the Uniform Controlled Substances Act, 21 U.S.C. 801 et seq.). Such activity can result in your account being delisted.

1.2 The listing or sale of all drug precursor chemicals (such as those listed in the Convention on Psychotropic Substances of 1971) is strictly prohibited.

1.3 Drug paraphernalia, including all items that are primarily intended or designed for use in manufacturing, concealing, or using a controlled substance, are strictly forbidden on the Site. Such items include, but are not limited to those items used for the ingestion of illicit substances, including pipes such as water pipes, carburetor pipes, chamber pipes, ice pipes, bongs etc.

1.4 The listing or sale of packaging materials which may be utilized to contain controlled substances, materials conducive to smuggling, storing, trafficking, transporting and manufacturing illicit drugs (e.g. marijuana grow lights), publications and other media providing information related to the production of illicit drugs.

### 2\. FLAMMABLE, EXPLOSIVE AND HAZARDOUS CHEMICALS

2.1 The posting of explosives and related ignition and detonation equipment is strictly prohibited. Such activity can result in your account being delisted.

2.2 Radioactive substances, toxic and poisonous chemicals are forbidden on the AliExpress Sites.

2.3 The posting, offering for sale, or offering for purchase of hazardous or dangerous materials (such as the categories of dangerous goods as defined under the International Maritime Dangerous Goods Code) are forbidden on the AliExpress Sites.

2.4 Ozone depleting substances are not permitted to be listed.

2.5 The posting, offering for sale, or offering for purchase of any products containing harmful substances (e.g. items containing asbestos) are forbidden on the AliExpress Sites.

2.6 Listing of fireworks, firecrackers and associated products are forbidden on AliExpress Sites for Relevant Online Transactions. Where the seller is a properly licensed seller of these products in mainland China, and exception can be made where the sale will not amount to a Relevant Online Transaction.

2.7 Automotive airbags are expressly forbidden on the AliExpress due to containing explosive materials.

### 3\. WEAPONS, FIREARMS AND AMMUNITIONS

3.1 AliExpress does not permit the posting, offering for sale, or offering of purchase of weapons that can incapacitate or cause serious physical harm to others (e.g. stun guns, batons, crossbows).

3.2 Any service, instruction, process, or aid for producing any biological, chemical, or nuclear weapons, or other Weapons of Mass Destruction (WMD) or known associated agents is strictly prohibited by international law and accordingly prohibited on the Site. Any violation of this policy will result in the notification of government authorities by AliExpress and your account being delisted.

3.3 The posting of, offering for sale, or offering for purchase of any arms, munitions, military ordnance, weapons (including explosive weapons), and/or any related parts and components (whether integral or otherwise) is strictly prohibited. Such activity can result in your account being delisted.

3.4 AliExpress does not permit the posting, offering for sale, or offering of purchase of replica, "look-alike” or imitation firearms, and/or any related parts and components (whether integral or otherwise). This prohibition covers such products as air guns, BB guns, paintball guns, harpoons, spear guns and other weapons that may discharge a projectile containing any gas, chemical, or explosive substance.

3.5 AliExpress maintains discretion over what items are appropriate and may cause removal of a listing that it deems as a weapon.

### 4\. CONTROLL ITEMS

4.1 While listing of most knives and other cutting instruments is permitted, switchblade knives, gravity knifes, knuckledusters (bladed or not), bladed handheld devices, and disguised knives are prohibited.

4.2 AliExpress does not permit the posting, offering for sale, or offering of purchase of control items that endanger the personal safety of others (e.g. restrained knives).

### 5\. GOVERNMENT, LAW ENFORCEMENT AND MILITARY ISSUED ITEMS

5.1 The following items are not permitted to be listed:

(a) Articles of clothing or identification that claim to be, or appear similar to, official government uniforms.

(b) Law enforcement badges or official law enforcement equipment from any public authority, including badges issued by the government of any country.

(c) Military decorations, medals and awards, in addition to items with substantially similar designs.

5.2 Police uniforms, police insignia and police vehicles may not be posted unless they are obsolete and in no way resemble current issue police uniforms, police insignia and police vehicles. This fact must be clearly stated within the posting description.

5.3 There are some police items that may be listed on the AliExpress Sites, provided they observe the following guidelines:

(a) Authorized general souvenir items, such as hats, mugs, pins, pens, buttons, cuff links, T-shirts, money clips that do not resemble badges, and paperweights that do not contain badges.

(b) Badges that are clearly not genuine or official (e.g. toy badges).

(c) Historical badges that do not resemble modern law enforcement badges, provided that the item description clearly states that the badge is a historical piece at least 75 years old or issued by an organization which no longer exists.

5.4 The following mass-transit related items are not permitted to be listed:

(a) Any article of clothing or identification related to transportation industries, including but not limited to, commercial airline pilots, flight attendants, airport service personnel, railway personnel, mass-transit security personnel. Vintage clothing related to commercial airlines or other mass-transit may be listed provided that the description clearly states that the item is at least 10 years old, is no longer in use and does not resemble any current uniform.

(b) Manuals or other materials related to commercial transportation, including safety manuals published by commercial airlines and entities operating subways, trains or buses. Such items may only be listed if the description clearly states that the material is obsolete and no longer in use.

(c) Any official, internal, classified or non-public documents.

5.5 AliExpress does not permit the posting, offering for sale, or offering of purchase of uniforms, equipment and other products that may be mistaken by the public for military or police supplies. Where the seller is a properly licensed seller of these products in mainland China, and exception can be made where the sale will not amount to a Relevant Online Transaction.

### 6\. MEDICAL DRUGS

6.1 The posting of prescription drugs, psychotropic drugs and narcotics is strictly prohibited.

6.2 The listing or sale of orally administered or ingested sexual enhancement foods and supplements and sexual health products are prohibited.

6.3 Prescription veterinary drugs may not be listed.

6.4 Members may post OTC (over-the-counter) drugs on the AliExpress Sites after provision of appropriate production and sales permits to AliExpress, while transactions of these products are strictly prohibited to be entered into as a Relevant Online Transaction.

### 7\. MEDICAL DEVICES

AliExpress does not permit the posting of unauthorized medical devices. Members may only post authorized medical devices after provision of appropriate production and sales permits/qualification to AliExpress, while transactions of these products are strictly prohibited to be entered into as a Relevant Online Transaction.

### 8\. ADULT AND OBSCENE MATERIALS

8.1 The posting or sale of pornographic materials is strictly prohibited, as it violates laws in many countries. While pornography is difficult to define and standards vary from nation to nation, AliExpress will generally follow guidelines accepted in Hong Kong and the PRC.

8.2 Items depicting or suggestive of bestiality, rape sex, incest or sex with graphic violence or degradation, and any items depicting or suggestive of sex involving minors, are strictly prohibited.

8.3 In determining whether listings or information should be removed from the AliExpress Sites, we consider the overall content of the posting, including images, pictorials, and text.

8.4 While sex toys and related products are permitted to be listed, product descriptions may not include nude or otherwise sexually explicit images.

### 9\. CIRCUMVENTION DEVICES AND OTHER EQUIPMENT USED FOR ILLICT PURPOSES

9.1 Descramblers and other items that can be used to gain unauthorized access to television programming (such as satellite and cable TV), internet access, telephone, data or other protected, restricted, or premium services are prohibited. Stating the item is for educational or test purposes will not legitimize a product that is otherwise inappropriate. Some examples of items which are not permitted include smart cards and card programmers, descramblers, DSS emulators and hacking software.

9.2 Similarly, information on "how to" descramble or gain access to cable or satellite television programming or other services without authorization or payment is prohibited. AliExpress' s policy is to prohibit any encouragement of this type of activity.

9.3 Devices designed to intentionally block, jam or interfere with authorized radio communications, such as cellular and personal communication services, police radar, global positioning systems (GPS) and wireless networking services (Wi-Fi) are prohibited.

9.4 The listing or sale of spy equipment and software used for eavesdropping, stealing privacy or confidentiality and devices used for interception of wire, oral and electronic communications is not permitted on the Site.

9.5 Hidden photographic devices are permitted on the AliExpress Sites, unless used for sexual or illicit purposes.

9.6 Bank card readers 、“skimmers” are prohibited from being listed.

9.7 Any and all unauthorized circumvention devices not included in the above are also strictly prohibited.

### 10\. ILLEGAL SERVICES

10.1 Listings claiming to provide government services and related products are strictly prohibited. Examples include:

(a) Official government-issued identification documents, such as birth certificates, driving licenses, passports and visas;

(b) Completed applications for the abovementioned documents

(c) Any materials, equipment or processes designed for use in the production of government-issued identification documents (e.g. driving license holograms, passport booklets).

(d) The offering for sale or purchase of textile quota is prohibited on the AliExpress Sites.

10.2 The listing or sale of any form of invoices or receipts (including blank, pre-filled, or value added invoices or receipts), is strictly prohibited on the Site.

10.3 AliExpress prohibits listings that offer financial services, including money transfers, issuing bank guarantees and letters of credit, loans, fundraising and funding for person investment purposes, etc.

10.4 AliExpress prohibits listings for the sole purpose of collecting user information or raising money.

10.5 Listings that offer medical or healthcare services, including services for medical treatment, rehabilitation, vaccination, health checks, psychological counseling, dietetics, plastic surgery and massage are prohibited.

10.6 The posting or sale of bulk email or mailing lists that contain personally identifiable information including names, addresses, phone numbers, fax numbers and email addresses, is strictly prohibited. Also prohibited are software or other tools which are designed or used to send unsolicited commercial email (i.e. "spam").

10.7 Job postings from which a factory/company/institute may directly recruit employees are prohibited on the Site.

10.8 AliExpress is an online business to customer information platform; personal and non-business information is prohibited.

10.9 Non-transferable items may not be posted or sold through the AliExpress. Many items including lottery tickets, airline tickets and some event tickets may not be resold or transferred.

### 11\. COLLECTIONS, ARTIFACTS AND PRECIOUS METALS

11.1 AliExpress strictly forbids the sale and purchase of currency, coins, banknotes, stocks, bonds, money orders, credit and debit cards, investment interest, currency, financial warrants in digital or any intangible form (e.g.crypto-currency) or other similar products or products that may be mistaken for such items, as well as the tools, methods, equipment and materials used to produce,counterfeit or modify such items.

11.2 Counterfeits of the identified articles in 11.1, legal tender and stamps are strictly prohibited.

11.3 Reproductions or replicas of coins as collectible items must be clearly marked with the word "COPY", "REPRODUCTION" or "REPLICA" and comply with all relevant local laws.

11.4 Listings that offer the sale or buying of gold, silver and other precious metals (not including jewelry) are prohibited.

11.5 Rough diamonds and “conflict minerals” originating from non-compliant countries may not be listed.

11.6 Artifacts, cultural relics, historical grave markers, and related items are protected under the laws of the PRC, the United States, and other jurisdictions; and may not be posted or sold through the AliExpress Sites.

### 12\. HUMAN PARTS, HUMAN REMAINS AND PROTECTED FLORA AND FAUNA

12.1 AliExpress prohibits the listing of human body parts and remains. Examples of such prohibited items include, but are not limited to: organs, bones, blood, sperm, and eggs. Items made of human hair, such as wigs for commercial uses, are permitted.

12.2 The listing or sale of any species (including any animal parts such as pelts, skins, internal organs, teeth, claws, shells, bones, tusks, ivory，logs, roots and other parts) protected by the Convention on International Trade in Endangered Species of Wild Fauna and Flora (CITES) or any other local law or regulation is strictly forbidden on the AliExpress Sites.

12.3 The listing or sale of products made with any part of and/or containing any ingredient derived from sharks or marine mammals is prohibited on the AliExpress Sites. Products compliant with specific country or regional laws and having valid authorization may be excluded.

12.4 The listing or sale of products made from cats, dogs and bears, as well as any processing equipment, is prohibited on the AliExpress Sites.

12.5 AliExpress prohibits the listing or sale of animal trapping and culling equipment, such as animal traps, leg traps, cat and dog hair plucking machines etc.

12.6 The listing or sale of poultry, livestock and pets is prohibited on the AliExpress Sites. For the avoidance of doubt, live animals are prohibited from being listed on the AliExpress Sites.

### 13\. OFFENSIVE MATERIAL AND INFORMATION DETRIMENTAL TO NATIONAL SECURITY

13.1 Any and all publications and other media containing state secrets or information detrimental to national security or public order are prohibited. Such activity can result in your account being delisted.

13.2 Any information supporting or advocating infringement of national sovereignty, terrorist organizations or discrimination on grounds of race, sex, or religion is strictly prohibited on the AliExpress Sites. Such activity can result in your account being delisted.

13.3 Postings that are ethnically or racially offensive are prohibited on AliExpress. Sellers and purchasers must ensure that any wording used portrays appropriate sensitivity to those who might read it in their postings, and when they are offering or purchasing potentially offensive items or services.

13.4 Occasionally, if materials are of historical value or integral to the item (such as a book title), members may use offensive words and phrases such as "Yang Guizi" in the subject and description of a posting. AliExpress reserves the sole discretion to decide the removal of such items and encourages all members to treat others as they themselves would like to be treated.

13.5 Materials advocating, promoting or otherwise supporting fascism, Nazism and other extreme ideologies are strictly prohibited.

### 14\. TOBACCO PRODUCTS

14.1 The posting of tobacco products, including but not limited to cigars, cigarettes, cigarette tobacco, pipe tobacco, hookah tobacco, chewing tobacco and tobacco leaf is prohibited.

14.2 The posting of nicotine and other liquids (e-liquids) for use in electronic cigarettes is forbidden.

14.3 Members located in mainland China may only list equipment used for tobacco processing and production of tobacco products after provision of appropriate production and sales permits to the AliExpress.

### 15\. GAMBLING EQUIPMENT

The listing or sale of tools, equipment or information specifically used for gambling is prohibited. Products which have other legitimate uses (such as dice and playing cards) will generally be permitted.

### 16\. SANCTIONED AND PROHIBITED ITEMS

16.1 Products prohibited by laws, regulations, sanctions and trade restrictions in any relevant country or jurisdiction worldwide are strictly forbidden on AliExpress Sites.

16.2 The listing or sale of petroleum, petroleum products and petrochemical products originating in the Islamic Republic of Iran is strictly forbidden.

16.3 The listing or sale of coal, iron, iron ore, gold, titanium ore, vanadium ore and rare earth minerals originating in the Democratic People’s Republic of Korea is strictly forbidden.

16.4 The listing or sale of crude oil by sellers and buyers located in mainland China is prohibited.

16.5 The listing for sale into the United States America or other markets of a product that is subject to import prohibition/restriction (including an active U.S. Customs and Border Protection Withhold Release Order) is prohibited on AliExpress Sites.

### 17\. INFERIOR OR RISKY ITEMS THAT VIOLATE LAWS/REGULATIONS/POLICIES OF DOMESTIC AND DESTINATION COUNTRY

17.1.Items identified, warned or recalled as inferior or risky products by authoritative quality inspection institutions, manufacturers or regulators are forbidden on AliExpress Sites

### 18\. PRODUCTS THAT ARE NOT SUITABLE FOR CROSS-BORDER SALES DUE TO THEIR NATURE

18.1 The listing or sale of products that are banned or restricted in specific countries.

18.2 The listing or sale of lucky bag, blind box and other associated products are prohibited.

18.3 The listing or sale of Alcohol, Food and Beverage are prohibited on the AliExpress Sites.

18.4 Goods that should not be sold because their attributes are not suitable for cross-border sales (such as tea, ordinary food (nuts, fast food, pickled food), live plants, live animals, virtual products(except for targeted seller recruitment), etc.)

### 19． CONTROVERSIAL OR SENSITIVE PRODUCTS THAT ARE CONTRARY TO SOCIAL MORALS, PUBLIC ORDER, GOOD CUSTOMS, AND HUMANITARIAN PRINCIPLES

The listing or sale of controversial or sensitive products that may breach lines of morality, humanity; violate any local society's basic norms; or jeopardize any social order are strictly prohibited. Such items include, but are not limited to, abortion tools, genetic related products, products related to animal or organ cloning, products related to animal or human experiments, or products that may cause detrimental harm to the environment or society.

### 20\. OTHER LISTING PROHIBITIONS

20.1 The posting of any products containing harmful substances (e.g.toys containing lead paint) is forbidden on the AliExpress Sites.

20.2 Refurbished products

The sale and purchase of refurbished mobile phones, laptops and computers is prohibited on the AliExpress Sites.

20.3 Used products

(a) Used undergarments may not be listed or sold on the Site. Other used clothing may be listed, so long as the clothing has been thoroughly cleaned. Postings that contain inappropriate or extraneous descriptions will be removed.

(b) The listing or sale of used cosmetics is prohibited on the AliExpress Sites.

20.4 Contracts and tickets

(a) You are responsible for ensuring that your transaction is lawful and not in violation of any contractual obligation. Before posting an item on the Site, you should carefully read any contracts that you have entered into that might limit your right to sell your item on the Site. Some items, such as airline tickets, have terms printed on the item that may limit your ability to sell that item. In other cases, such as when you are distributing a company's products, you may have signed a separate contract restricting your ability to market the product.

(b) AliExpress does not search for items that may raise these types of issues, nor can it

review copies of private contracts, or adjudicate or take sides in private contract disputes. However, we want you to be aware that posting items in violation of your contractual obligations could put you at risk with third parties. AliExpress therefore urges that you not list any item until you have reviewed any relevant contracts or agreements, and are confident you can legally sell it on the Site.

(c) If you have any questions regarding your rights under a contract or agreement, we

strongly recommend that you contact the company with whom you entered into the contract and/or consult with an attorney.

20.5 Event ticket resale policy

AliExpress allows the listing of tickets to performance, sporting and entertainment events to the extent permitted by law. However, as a ticket seller, you are responsible for ensuring that your particular transaction does not violate any applicable law or the terms on the ticket itself.

20.6 Stolen property

(a) The posting or sale of stolen property is strictly forbidden on the Site, and violates international law. Stolen property includes items taken from private individuals, as well as property taken without authorization from companies or governments.

(b) AliExpress supports and cooperates with law enforcement efforts involving the recovery of stolen property and the prosecution of responsible individuals. If you are concerned that the images and/or text in your item description have been used by another Site user without your authorization, or that your intellectual property rights have been violated by such user, please contact our service team at alibaba@service.alibaba.com.

PART 3 INTELLECTUAL PROPERTY RIGHTS (IPR) PROTECTION POLICY
-----------------------------------------------------------

### 1\. FACES, NAMES AND SIGNATURES

Items containing the likeness, image, name, or signature of another person are prohibited, unless the products were made or authorized by the person whose likeness, image, name or signature has been used.

### 2\. REPLICA AND COUNTERFEIT ITEMS

2.1 Listing of counterfeits, non-licensed replicas, or unauthorized items, such as counterfeit designer garments, watches, handbags, sunglasses, or other accessories, is strictly prohibited on the Site.

2.2 If the products sold bear the name or logo of a company, but did not originate from or were not endorsed by that company, such products are prohibited from the Site.

2.3 Postings of branded products are permitted if a certificate of authorization has been issued by the brand owner.

2.4 Postings offering to sell or purchase replicas, counterfeits or other unauthorized items shall be subject to removal by AliExpress. Repeated postings of counterfeit or unauthorized items shall result in the immediate suspension of your membership.

### 3\. SOFTWARE

3.1 Academic Software

(a) Academic software is software sold at discounted prices to students, teachers, and employees of accredited learning institutions.

(b) On the Site, please do not list any academic software unless you are so authorized. Postings violating AliExpress' s academic software policy may be deleted prior to publication.

(c) For postings of academic software on behalf of an authorized educational reseller or an educational institution, such licensure must be stated conspicuously in the listings. A certificate of authorization issued by the authorized educational reseller (or the educational institution) must also be provided to AliExpress.

3.2 OEM Software

(a) Do not list "OEM" or "bundled" copies of software on the AliExpress Sites unless you are selling it with computer hardware. Original Equipment Manufacturer (OEM), or bundled software, is software that is obtained as part of the purchase of a new computer. OEM software licenses usually prohibit the purchaser from reselling the software without the computer or, in some cases, without any computer hardware.

### 4\. UNAUTHORIZED COPIES OF INTELLECTUAL PROPERTY

The listing or sale of unauthorized (pirated, duplicated, backup, bootleg, etc.) copies of software programs, video games, music albums, movies, television programs, photographs or other protected works is forbidden on the Site.

For further information of Intellectual Property Rights (IPR) Protection Policy, please click on: [https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523641](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523641) and [https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647)

**NOTICE:** THIS LIST SHOULD NOT BE CONSIDERED EXHAUSTIVE IN NATURE AND SHALL BE UPDATED ON A CONTINUOUS BASIS. IF YOU ARE UNSURE ABOUT THE PRODUCT YOU WISH TO LIST WITH THE SITE IN REGARD TO ITS APPROPRIATENESS OR LEGALITY, PLEASE CONTACT CUSTOMER SERVICES FOR FURTHER QUERIES.

[https://customerservice.aliexpress.com/home?language=en&from=slr\_common&hcMapRule=aeMapRule](https://customerservice.aliexpress.com/home?language=en&from=slr_common&hcMapRule=aeMapRule)

Rules on Product Safety and Compliance on AliExpress

Release date: /

Revision date: November 11, 2025

  

AliExpress is committed to providing consumers with safe and quality goods, creating a proper business environment for AliExpress users, continuously improving consumers’ shopping experience and safeguarding the rights and interests of honest sellers. As a seller, you are responsible to ensure that the goods you offer comply with the relevant laws and regulations in the countries you are selling to. Before listing the relevant product, please make sure that you understand your responsibilities as seller.

The following are the rules related to product safety and compliance on AliExpress:

\[Beautiful category\]
======================

|     |     |

AliExpress Product Recall Policy

**Why is a product recall implemented?**

Product recall refers to the process where a product sold is found to be defective and needs to be recovered from the end user. When a product has been recalled in certain countries, in order to protect the personal safety and property of consumers, AliExpress will prohibit sellers from selling this product in these countries.

**Where can information about product recalls be obtained?**

1、Recall announcements or directives issued by regulators in various countries, e.g. [Rapid Alert System for Non-Food Products (RAPEX, EU)](https://ec.europa.eu/consumers/consumers_safety/safety_products/rapex/alerts/?event=main.listNotifications&lng=en), [OPSS (UK)](https://www.gov.uk/guidance/product-safety-database-unsafe-products), [EU Rapid Alert System for Food and Feed (RASFF)](https://ec.europa.eu/food/safety/rasff_en), [OECD Global Recalls Portal](https://globalrecalls.oecd.org/#/), [USDA](https://www.fsis.usda.gov/wps/portal/fsis/topics/recalls-and-public-health-alerts), [FDA](https://www.fda.gov/safety/recalls-market-withdrawals-safety-alerts), [CPSC](https://www.cpsc.gov/Recalls), [Health Canada/Transport Canada](https://healthycanadians.gc.ca/recall-alert-rappel-avis/index-eng.php), [Australian Competition and Consumer Commission (ACCC)](https://www.accc.gov.au/topics/recalls?spm=5261.ams_108617.0.0.2b7065252KwsuB). Such recalls are generally announced by these regulators on their websites. The content of these announcements usually includes the name of the product (identification information), risk type, the nature of the problem, the regions of the affected product, and remedial measures for buyers.

2、Recalls initiated by the manufacturer or actual producer. For such recalls, the manufacturer, brand owner, or supplier directly informs retailers and other supply chain partners of the product issues before regulators intervene (or in some cases, without the intervention of regulators at all).

**Measures taken by AliExpress in a product recall**

After receiving relevant information about a product recall, AliExpress will take measures including but not limited to the following:

1、Check the recalled products and, as appropriate, inspect the same type of products sold on the AliExpress platform

2、Block the recalled products or other similar products from displaying in certain countries or remove them directly

3、Contact and notify sellers to recall the products that have been sold, and demand due diligence in the recall and handling process

4、Formulate control measures to prevent recalled products from entering the market again Report the handling of recalled products to overseas regulatory agencies according to laws, regulations or regulatory requirements

5、Demand sellers to tighten quality and safety risk control

6、Strengthen education and legal publicity for sellers to provide guidance on sales that meet compliance requirements

7、Other measures deemed appropriate by the platform

**Obligations of AliExpress sellers during a product recall**

After receiving a product recall request from AliExpress, sellers shall comply with applicable laws and regulations regarding recalls, and take the following measures:

1、Immediately contact all buyers in the region of the recall, and recall relevant products or provide return/refund services; properly dispose of the recalled products

2、Stop selling similar products to these regions or remove these products

3、Intercept affected product in transit or take corresponding recall measures

4、If damage is caused to consumers, they shall be compensated

5、In accordance with corresponding laws, regulations or regulatory requirements, report product recalls to regulatory agencies, cooperate with their investigations, and respond promptly

6、Actively cooperate with the platform in investigations and provide relevant documents or test reports

7、Enhance compliance awareness, and conduct own inspection of other products in the stores to prevent similar incidents in the future

**If a buyer purchased a product marked for recall, what should the buyer do?**

If you have purchased a recalled product, please stop using it immediately, or you can contact the seller to request a return/replacement/refund.

Thank you for your attention and support!

**AliExpress**

January 27, 2021

AliExpress "Abuse Report" Rules

Release date: August 25, 2023

Revision date: October 17, 2024

  

1、Scope of Application
----------------------

AliExpress encourages global users to use the reporting function to report illegal behavior. In order to maintain a healthy and orderly marketplace and to uphold the quality of reports, rules have been established to prevent the abuse of the reporting function.

When users use the reporting function, the reported behavior includes:

(1) Reports initiated by buyers or unregistered users:

1) Intellectual property complaints (limited to rights holders)

2) Intellectual property infringement reports (excluding rights holders)

3) Prohibited or restricted sales

(2) Reports initiated by sellers:

1) Intellectual property complaints (limited to rights holders)

2) Intellectual property infringement reports (excluding rights holders)

3) Prohibited or restricted sales

4) Violation of product listing rules

5) Search manipulation

6) Reporting malicious buyers

The platform has the right to clarify illegal behavior and add new reportable scenarios, and notify through the platform rules center, in-site messages, etc. before execution. Please pay attention.

2、Definition and Presentation
-----------------------------

### (1) The submitted content is illegal

Illegal content refers to information that endangers national and social security according to the laws and regulations of various countries and other illegal speech and illegal content stipulated in the laws and regulations of various countries, including but not limited to:

1) Oppose the basic principles established by the laws of various countries;

2) Endanger the unity, sovereignty and territorial integrity of all countries;

3) Leaking state secrets, endangering national security, or damaging national honor and interests;

4) Incite ethnic hatred and discrimination, undermine ethnic unity, or infringe on ethnic customs and habits;

5) Undermining national religious policies and promoting cults and superstitions;

6) Spread rumors, disrupt social order, and undermine social stability;

7) Promote gambling, violence, murder, terror, drug abuse, pyramid schemes, self-abuse, or instigate crime;

8) Inciting illegal assembly, association, procession, demonstration, or gathering of people to disrupt social order;

9) Obscene and pornographic information, including but not limited to:

**·** Specific depictions of sexual acts or explicit promotion of pornographic and obscene information;

**·** Exposed pictures and videos, audios and texts with pornographic connotations, hints, provocations and arousing similar feelings in others;

**·** Vulgar information, such as: using only a small covering to cover the hidden parts of the human body, wearing revealing clothing, topless, naked children, breastfeeding performances, etc., except for descriptions, instructions and comments related to product functions.

### (2) The submitted content has no obvious basis, including but not limited to the following scenarios:

1) Incorrect or unrelated links to other products;

2) Failure to clearly and accurately express the reasons for the report or the reported reasons clearly do not match the actual situation;

3) Failure to provide valid evidence to support the reported facts;

4) Repeatedly submitting duplicate reports for the same reported content.

### (3) The submitted content does not comply with platform rules.

When your report content is rejected, please prioritize reviewing the rule requirements under the corresponding report category. You can also check the rule details on the report submission page:

1) Intellectual property complaints (limited to rights holders) and intellectual property infringement reports (excluding rights holders): [Update of Enforcement Actions for Intellectual Property Rights (IPR)](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/127561565);

2) Prohibited or restricted sales: [AliExpress Index of Prohibited and Controlled Items](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/127561551);

3) Reporting malicious buyers: [AliExpress "Unfair Competition" Rules](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/137340205).

3、Violation and Penalties
-------------------------

The platform will take measures to warn and restrict the use of the reporting function for users who engage in abusive reporting behavior. The platform has the right to independently determine the severity of the violation based on the frequency of users' reports and impose the following penalties.

For general violations where the number of abuse reports exceeds that of most platform users within a certain period, the platform will issue a warning to the user. For serious violations where users use scripts and other tools to submit reporting information in batches or submit reports far more than the average user within a certain period, the platform will take measures such as freezing the user's reporting function for 3 days or freezing the user's account. After the penalty period expires, the user's reporting function will be restored.

AliExpress

AliExpress "Credit and Sales Manipulation" Rules Supplemental Explanation

Dear Sellers,

In order to help sellers better understand the "Credit and Sales Manipulation" rules and regulate their own business practices accordingly, the platform has provided supplemental explanations on the scope of application, definitions, manifestations of credit and sales manipulation, violation categories, and penalties. The specific rules are as follows:

1、Scope of Application
----------------------

To protect the legitimate rights and interests of consumers, operators, or AliExpress, if the platform discovers any violation by a merchant, the following violation handling measures will be taken during the violation processing period in accordance with the circumstances specified in these rules, until AliExpress confirms that the risks are basically under control and partial or complete lifting of control measures.

2、Definition and Manifestations
-------------------------------

Credit and sales manipulation refers to the behavior of merchants obtaining false benefits such as fake product sales, store ratings, credit scores, product reviews, or transaction amounts through improper methods such as fabricating or concealing transaction facts, and evading or maliciously exploiting credit record rules.

Unfair forms of credit and sales manipulation include but are not limited to:

（1）Using fake shipping tracking numbers or reusing a single tracking number multiple times, or providing logistics information that cannot be queried or does not exist.

（2）Lowering product prices directly or indirectly (such as significantly modifying product prices or transaction prices, etc.) to attract buyers to place orders but not shipping or falsely shipping.

（3）Sellers registering their own accounts or manipulating other accounts (including but not limited to manipulation of team accounts, accounts of relatives and friends, accounts of colleagues in the company, etc.) to purchase their own listed products; or occurrences of repetitive bidding, account, and IP issues by buyers.

（4）Sellers engaging in false transactions using tools, services, or favorable conditions provided by third parties (including other sellers).

（5）Other abnormal trading methods.

3、Violation Categories and Penalty Measures
-------------------------------------------

（1）For sellers who are first identified by the platform as engaging in credit and sales manipulation, the platform will delete the credit scores and sales records of their violating products, refund orders related to credit and sales manipulation, and impose penalties ranging from warnings to account freezes for 7 to 180 days, depending on the severity of the violation. In severe cases, direct account termination may be imposed.

（2）Goods suspected of false transactions will have their platform search ranking lowered for 30 days. In severe cases, the platform will also delist all products in the seller's store.

（3）For sellers who continue to engage in credit and sales manipulation after receiving warnings or account freezes, the platform reserves the right to directly terminate their accounts.

（4）Credit and sales manipulation penalty execution overview:

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| **Violation Category** | **Penalty Measures** |
| Minor Offense | 6 points/times |
| Moderate Offense | 12 points/times |
| Severe Offense | 24 points/times |
| Particularly Severe Violation | 48 points/times |

Offense Penalty Standard Dimension: Based on the number of violating orders within 30 days, the proportion of violating orders to total orders, and the credit and sales manipulation situation on the platform.

AliExpress

[1、Scope of Application](#LLPDc)

[2、Definition and Manifestations](#qW13G)

[3、Violation Categories and Penalty Measures](#P4GR8)

AliExpress "Disclosure of Personal Information" Rule

1、Scope
-------

In order to maintain a healthy and orderly marketplace, protect the privacy and security of platform users, and enhance the user experience, this rule is formulated.

2、Definition and Manifestations
-------------------------------

**"Personal information" includes but is not limited to**:

Buyer's username, platform ID, real name, mobile phone number, shipping address (partial or complete), messages, comments, personal characteristics, preferences, and other order or personal-related information. Disclosure of personal data includes but is not limited to the following cases:

（1）Sellers disclose or transfer information to external parties without the written and explicit permission of the buyer and the platform (permission should be provided by the seller as evidence). The term "external parties" includes but is not limited to unnecessary internal employees, external third-party companies or individuals, and unspecified entities. The term "disclosure or transfer" includes but is not limited to any method, whether online or offline, public or targeted, explicit or implied, written or encrypted. For example, a seller publicly discloses personal information on the platform without permission, and a seller discloses personal information to third-party websites without permission, a seller discloses personal information to third-party companies that are not involved in completing transactions with buyers, or a seller discloses buyer's order information to non-buyers without permission.

（2）Sellers publish products for non-genuine transaction purposes and subsequently disclose buyer information obtained through it.

（3）Sellers' negligence in employee management, account management, system security, etc., leading to the disclosure of personal information. Negligence includes but is not limited to: lack of basic information security measures within the seller's store, poor employee management, obvious risks of information leakage in the system but no effective remedial measures taken by the seller.

3、Violation Categories and Penalty Measures
-------------------------------------------

**"Disclosure of Personal Information" is divided into minor offenses and severe offenses based on severity. Severe violation behaviors include but are not limited to the following situations:**

（1）Disclosure of personal information to third-party websites, companies, or individuals.

（2）Bulk disclosure of personal information through technical means.

（3）Disclosure of personal information with subjective malicious intent, including but not limited to malicious methods or tactics.

（4）Other means of disclosure result in a significant quantity of leaked information.

（5）Cases where the disclosure of personal information may result in civil, administrative, or criminal liability.

（6）Cases where the disclosure of personal information causes serious consequences to users or the platform.

（7）Other severe instances of personal information disclosure.

Penalty Measures:

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| **Violation Category** | **Penalty Measures** |
| Minor Offense | 2 points/time |
| Severe Offense | 12 points/time |
| Extremely Severe | 48 points/time |

In addition to the above rules, the platform reserves all legal rights to hold any user accountable for disclosing personal information, including but not limited to pursuing civil liability or reporting to competent authorities for administrative or criminal responsibilities.

AliExpress

[1、Scope](#NqDQ8)

[2、Definition and Manifestations](#qJuND)

[3、Violation Categories and Penalty Measures](#NwMfM)

AliExpress "Disruption of Platform Order" Rule

Latest Revision Date: September 16, 2022 (Beijing Time)

  

1、Scope
-------

In order to maintain a healthy and orderly marketplace, prevent behaviors that disrupt platform order, and enhance the user experience of members, this rule is formulated. Disruption of platform order refers to behaviors that interfere with platform management, disrupt platform order, and harm the legitimate rights and interests of other users or the platform.

2、Definition and Manifestations
-------------------------------

（1）Behaviors that maliciously evade platform rules or regulatory measures.

（2）Behaviors that interfere with the normal transactions of other users through malicious violations or other means.

（3）Behaviors that cause serious negative experiences for buyers during the shopping process, the trend towards damaging buyer's rights, and have a detrimental impact on the business environment of AliExpress.

（4）Merchants who do not cooperate or fail to timely submit/update compliance qualification documents in accordance with platform rules.

（5）Existence of issues related to product quality or store compliance, which may lead to judicial investigations, administrative supervision, administrative litigation, media coverage, public questioning, or involve goods, information, or behaviors that may be related to current affairs, public opinion events, and can easily trigger inappropriate public opinion.

（6）Other behaviors that disrupt platform order.

3、Violation Categories and Penalty Measures
-------------------------------------------

The platform has the right to independently judge the severity of the circumstances and impose the following penalties on merchants who engage in the above-mentioned disruptive behaviors that violate platform order:

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| **Violation Category** | **Penalty Measures** |
| Minor Offense | 6 points/time |
| Severe Offense | 12 points/time |
| Extremely Severe 48 points per occurrence Offense | 48 points/time |

Meanwhile, the search rankings of shops involved in violations will be downgraded.

Note: The platform has the right to independently determine the severity of circumstances based on factors such as the level of malice in the means adopted, the amount of profits gained, the number of orders involved, the severity of consequences caused, and the impact on consumer experience.

4、Interpretation
----------------

（1）What does "maliciously evading platform rules or regulatory measures" refer to? This includes but is not limited to:

1）Evading the regulation of major categories for platform operations and posting goods that are not allowed to be sold in non-admissible major categories.

2）Evading category regulations of the platform and posting a large number of goods that are not suitable for cross-border sales and should not be sold (such as perfumes; edible health products and food such as tea, powdered animal/plant extracts, etc.).

3）Guiding buyers to modify cancellation or dispute reasons to evade platform assessment.

（2）What does "behaviors that cause serious negative experiences for buyers during the shopping process and have a detrimental impact on the business environment of AliExpress" refer to? This includes long-term selling of poor-quality products, choosing logistics methods with poor timeliness, etc., where the overall operating indicators of the store are significantly lower than the industry average (e.g., high dispute rate, DSR significantly lower than the average level, low positive feedback rate), significantly affecting the consumer experience and causing serious negative experiences for buyers.

（3）How is "extremely severe circumstances" defined? If there are circumstances where means adopted to disrupt platform orders are extremely malicious, involve a large amount of profits, affect a significant number of orders, cause adverse consequences, or severely impact the consumer experience, they are considered as extremely severe circumstances.

AliExpress

[1、Scope](#clN7B)

[2、Definition and Manifestations](#Bvryc)

[3、Violation Categories and Penalty Measures](#Nld9G)

[4、Interpretation](#XS4v7)

AliExpress "fake shipment" Rules

Latest Revision Date: July 8, 2020 Beijing Time

1、Scope
-------

In order to maintain a healthy and orderly marketplace, prevent fake shipment behaviors, and improve the user experience of members, these rules are established.

2、Definitions and Manifestations
--------------------------------

Within the specified shipment period, fake shipment behaviors include using invalid or irrelevant tracking numbers, a prolonged absence of logistics collection information, failure to ship according to the declared tracking number in the system, or failure to fulfill the shipment obligation as declared to the consumer.

**Manifestations of fake shipment:**

（1）Using invalid or irrelevant tracking numbers when declaring shipment (e.g., false tracking numbers, inconsistent recipient information and delivery addresses with the order);

（2）Seller declares shipment but there is a prolonged absence of logistics collection and delivery information, or the tracking number exceeds the time limit and is canceled;

（3）Seller fails to choose the shipping method according to the platform's logistics policy (e.g., inconsistency between the shipping tracking number and the declared shipment, unauthorized use of offline economic logistics for shipment, or using economic logistics to impersonate standard or express logistics);

（4）Seller declares shipment from a country different from the one chosen by the buyer for shipping or where the inventory is located, such as declaring overseas inventory but actually shipping from China.

**Friendly Reminder:**

（1）"Invalid tracking number" refers to a non-existent logistics tracking number (including situations where the logistics information cannot be traced due to using unregistered small packages).

（2）"Irrelevant tracking number" refers to a logistics tracking number that exists but is unrelated to the order, including but not limited to discrepancies in order placement time (e.g., the receipt time is significantly earlier than the order placement time) or the delivery address is different from the one provided by the buyer (e.g., the delivery address and recipient's address are in different countries).

（3）"Logistics collection and delivery information" refers to the first piece of information provided by the logistics provider, where online shipments are generally collected/received by the warehouse, and offline shipments generally have successful collection or delivery information provided by the logistics provider.

（4）If there is a problem with the logistics order declared for the first shipment, please make sure to modify the declared logistics tracking number within 10 working days. The platform does not accept logistics tracking numbers provided in order messages or buyer communications and only recognizes the logistics tracking number declared in the order.

3、Violation Categories and Penalties
------------------------------------

Fake shipment behaviors are categorized as general violations or serious violations based on severity.

Serious violations of fake shipment behaviors include but are not limited to the following situations:

（1）Large order amounts for fake shipments;

（2）Collusion between buyers and sellers to mislead the AliExpress platform in disbursing funds through fake shipment behaviors without actual transactions;

（3）Repeated incidents of general fake shipment behaviors.

**Penalties:**

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| **Violation Category** | **Penalty** |
| General Violation | 2 points/time |
| Serious Violation | 12 points/time |
| Particularly Serious Violation | 48 points/time |
| Note:<br><br>AliExpress will penalize or directly close accounts based on the severity of seller violations. If a fake shipment is determined by the platform, measures such as revoking overseas warehouse shipping privileges, closing fake shipment orders and providing refunds, revoking product publishing privileges, taking down online products, and closing accounts may be implemented. |     |

AliExpress

[1、Scope](#o0xnQ)

[2、Definitions and Manifestations](#sHc8W)

[3、Violation Categories and Penalties](#Ql4mM)

AliExpress "Illegal Profits" Rules

Latest Revision Date: March 6, 2023 (Beijing Time)

1、Scope
-------

In order to maintain a healthy and orderly marketplace, prevent illegal profit-making activities, and enhance the user experience of members, these rules have been formulated.

2、Definitions and Manifestations
--------------------------------

Illegal profits refer to the actions of sellers that fabricate or conceal transaction facts, violate or evade AliExpress rules, and are suspected of infringing upon the property rights or other legitimate rights and interests of others. They include but are not limited to the following situations:

（1）Sellers deceive buyers by publishing or providing false or mismatched goods, services, or logistics information to obtain transaction funds.

（2）Sellers induce their trading counterparts to deviate from the normal AliExpress transaction process and gain unfair advantages.

（3）Sending phishing links or Trojan virus messages to deceive others' property.

（4）Using unfair means, non-genuine transactions, or illegal methods to obtain subsidies from the AliExpress platform, including but not limited to platform After-Sales Compensation, platform coupons, promo codes, platform discounts, deposits, platform compensation funds, commissions, and bounty incentives.

（5）Deceiving others by impersonating AliExpress or its affiliated company employees or AliExpress store customer service.

（6）Using third-party accounts to commit fraud and deceive others of their property.

（7）Sellers illegally profit through means other than violating AliExpress rules.

（8）For the purpose of sales, sellers engage in or assist buyers in various types of tax evasion behaviors in any explicit or implied manner.

3、Violation and Penalties
-------------------------

Based on comprehensive risk investigations conducted by the platform, including data analysis, feedback from buyers or other sellers, and various potential risks, sellers' goods, transactions, etc., are evaluated for risks associated with illegal profit-making behaviors. Illegal profit-making behaviors are categorized as general violations, serious violations, and particularly serious violations based on severity.

General Violation: The platform determines that the seller has engaged in illegal profit-making behavior, but the number of orders involved or the amount of illegal profits is small, and the severity of the situation is minor.

Serious Violation: The platform determines that the seller has engaged in illegal profit-making behavior, and the number of orders involved or the amount of illegal profits is large, or the proportion of illegal profits to the store's total transaction amount is high, or it has caused consumers a negative shopping experience, or the platform has issued a warning but no corrective action has been taken.

Particularly Serious Violation: The platform determines that the seller has engaged in illegal profit-making behavior, using egregious methods, and the number of orders involved or the amount of illegal profits is significantly large, or the proportion of illegal profits to the store's total transaction amount is very high, or it has caused consumers a serious negative shopping experience or damages to the platform, or the platform has issued two or more warnings or penalties, and the store continues to violate the rules.

**Penalties:**

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| **Violation Category** | **Penalty Measures** |
| General Violation | 6 points/time |
| Serious Violation | 12 points/time |
| Particularly Serious Violation | 48 points/time |

Suppose the platform discovers that a seller is suspected of illegal profit-making. In that case, the platform has the right to immediately take restrictive measures against the seller, including but not limited to restricting product listing permissions, removing online products, freezing the seller's account, freezing the seller's Alipay account/AliExpress account, and extending the loan repayment time. The platform also has the right to close orders related to illegal profit-making behaviors (such as orders obtained by taking advantage of coupons) regardless of the order status (even if the seller has shipped the order or the order status is already marked as successful). After closing the order, the payment will be refunded to the buyer, and the platform subsidy will be returned to the platform. At the same time, if the seller has obtained platform subsidies through illegal profit-making behaviors, the platform has the right to demand that the seller bear breach of contract liability and directly deduct an amount equal to the funds involved in the illegal profit-making from the seller's Alipay international account or AliExpress account as liquidated damages. If there is an insufficient amount for a deduction, AliExpress has the right to continue to recover the remaining amount from the seller.

In addition to the penalties mentioned above, if the seller causes damage to the platform through illegal profit-making, the platform has the right to seek compensation from the seller and reserves other remedies permitted by law, including reporting to public security or procuratorial authorities.

Note 1: If you have objections to the related penalties or the orders involved in the violations, please file an online appeal against the punishment for illegal profit-making or serious disruption of platform order on the Merchant Backstage - Violations page. Please be sure to initiate the appeal within the time limit specified on the penalty page and submit supporting materials for each order, including but not limited to authentic and valid delivery orders or delivery certificates provided by the official postal service, logistics in transit proof, and logistics package weight settlement information. Please refer to the penalty notice for specific instructions. If your appeal is rejected or exceeds the appeal deadline during the appeal period, the platform will enforce the penalties and deduct the liquidated damages based on the content of the penalty notice. For clarity, the calculation of liquidated damages will be based on the final details of the violation order.

4、Interpretation
----------------

How should the funds involved in illegal profits be understood?

It refers to the subsidies provided by the AliExpress platform, such as platform coupons or other benefits, that are associated with violation orders committed during the seller's operation. These subsidies are funds provided by the platform to buyers in the form of promotional measures or other entitlements.

Taking platform coupons as an example, they are a type of promotional measure provided by the platform using its own funds. They are a form of preferential treatment that allows buyers to enjoy a certain amount of discount when making purchases. After the buyer uses the platform coupon during the transaction, the seller can directly or indirectly obtain cash from the platform by settling through the system or through manual means. If a seller illegally profits by taking advantage of coupons issued by the platform during their operation on the platform, the funds involved in illegal profits refer to the total sum of the face value of the coupons used by buyers in violation orders associated with the seller.

Note: When deducting the liquidated damages (an amount equal to the funds involved in illegal profits), the platform will convert the face value of the coupons into the currency of the seller's funding account based on the real-time exchange rate provided by the Bank of China. If a buyer requests a refund for a violation order or initiates a dispute process (such as a "dispute") or a chargeback in the system, the order will still be handled based on the platform's dispute rules and chargeback rules. The costs and liabilities associated with resolving disputes or chargebacks caused by disputes or chargebacks are the direct responsibility of the seller.

AliExpress

[2、Definitions and Manifestations](#BjghD)

[3、Violation and Penalties](#Hdjp7)

[4、Interpretation](#DsoQh)

AliExpress "Inducing Early Confirmation of Receipt" Rules

Latest Revision Date: September 16, 2022, Beijing Time

1、Scope
-------

In order to maintain a healthy and orderly marketplace and prevent the practice of inducing early confirmation of receipt, and to enhance the user experience of members, these rules are formulated.

2、Definition and Manifestations
-------------------------------

Refers to the seller's act of inducing the buyer to confirm receipt before receiving the goods.

3、Violation Categories and Penalty Measures
-------------------------------------------

For the above-mentioned behavior of inducing early confirmation of receipt, the platform has the right to independently judge and impose the following penalties: Within one performance year (starting from the date of the first identified act of inducing early confirmation of receipt; the second performance year starts 365 days after the end of the first performance year, and so on):

（1）If identified as inducing early confirmation of receipt for the 1st to 5th times, deduct 1 point per occurrence from the store.

（2）If identified as inducing early confirmation of receipt for the 6th to 10th times, deduct 2 points per occurrence from the store.

（3）If identified as inducing early confirmation of receipt for the 11th time or more, deduct 3 points per occurrence from the store.

AliExpress "Malicious Harassment" Rule

1、Scope
-------

In order to maintain a healthy and orderly marketplace, prevent malicious harassment, and enhance the user experience of members, this rule is formulated.

2、Definition and Manifestations
-------------------------------

It refers to the behavior of sellers frequently or using malicious means to harass members, which affects others' normal lives or impairs their legitimate rights and interests. Examples include demanding buyers to leave positive reviews or using abusive language towards buyers due to disputes. This behavior may include but is not limited to frequently contacting others through methods such as phone calls, text messages, AliWangWang, messages, emails, etc., which disrupts others' normal lives.

Severe malicious harassment behavior includes but is not limited to the following:

（1）The use of abusive language (such as "fuck," "suck," etc.), threats, curses, racial discrimination, religious or personal attacks, or repeated harassment that affects others' physical and mental well-being and normal lives; Extremely severe malicious harassment behavior includes but is not limited to the following:

（2）Harassment on a large scale, with a widespread impact, which may cause or has caused serious consequences to the platform's security and reputation;

（3）Using extreme means or tools to harass users, severely affects others' normal lives and causes significant harm to their physical and mental well-being. This includes but is not limited to mailing offensive or threatening items to members and publicly disclosing a buyer's personal phone number, address, name, purchase records, etc., on the internet.

3、Violation Categories and Penalty Measures
-------------------------------------------

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| **Violation Category** | **Penalty Measures** |
| Minor Offense | 2 points/time |
| Severe Offense | 12 points/time |
| Extremely Severe Violation | 48 points/time |

AliExpress "Mismatched merchandise" Rules

Latest Revision Date: September 16, 2022, Beijing Time

1、Definition and Manifestations
-------------------------------

To promote a fair trading environment, the behavior of selling Mismatched merchandise on the Alibaba Global AliExpress platform is considered a violation.

"Mismatched merchandise" refers to situations where the received product does not match the description or promises made by the seller at the time of the transaction in terms of category, parameters, material, specifications, etc.

**Manifestations of "Mismatched merchandise" include but are not limited to the following:**

（1）Sending empty packages to buyers;

（2）Products in the order are electronic storage devices with capacities that do not match the product description or promises;

（3）Products in the order are computer hardware with configurations that do not match the product description or promises;

（4）Products in the order are precious metals or gemstone jewelry with material contents that do not match the description;

（5）Received goods do not match the order information;

（6）Other situations where the ordered products do not match the shipped products.

2、Violation and Penalties
-------------------------

（1）General violations: There are slight quality or service issues based on buyer feedback, data analysis, or product inspections, but they do not have a substantial impact on the buyer's normal use.

（2）Serious violations: There are apparent quality or service issues based on buyer feedback, data analysis, or product inspections that have affected the buyer's normal use, or have caused harm to the buyer/other individuals' personal or property, or there have been three or more instances of general violations.

（3）Particularly serious violations: There are severe quality or service issues based on buyer feedback, data analysis, or product inspections, including but not limited to buyer disputes/evaluation data significantly lower than the level of similar products in the category, non-compliance with platform testing conducted directly or through third parties, and numerous incidents causing harm to the buyer/other individuals' personal or property; or there have been three or more instances of serious violations.

Violation Category Penalty General Violation 2 points/time.

Violating products cannot be relisted or must be deleted, and the store's search ranking is downgraded. Serious Violation 12 points/time.

Violating products cannot be relisted or must be deleted, and the store's search ranking is downgraded. Particularly Serious Violation 48 points/time. Store closure.

These rules are effective supplements to the "AliExpress Rules". All AliExpress sellers must comply with both the "AliExpress Rules" and the provisions of this standard when listing products. If the "AliExpress Rules" already have provisions, they shall be followed. If there are no provisions or if this standard has special provisions, this standard shall be followed.

AliExpress

[2、Violation and Penalties](#uFgr2)

AliExpress "Guiding Offline Transactions" Rules

Latest Revision Date: September 16, 2022, Beijing Time

1、Scope
-------

In order to maintain a healthy and orderly marketplace and prevent offline transactions, and to enhance the user experience of members, these rules are formulated.

2、Definition and Manifestations
-------------------------------

Refers to the seller's act of guiding the buyer to engage in offline transactions, thereby harming the legitimate interests of the buyer and the platform. Examples of guiding offline transactions include but are not limited to:

（1）Publishing or promoting third-party products or information that may lead to transaction risks, such as publishing the names, logos, QR codes, hyperlinks, contact accounts, etc., of third-party websites or platforms such as social media, shopping guides, group buying, promotions, shopping platforms, etc., except for specific market agreements with certain groups.

（2）Inducing consumers to redirect to third-party websites or platforms through other means, such as using SMS notifications.

（3）Third-party information includes but is not limited to non-AliExpress shopping links, QR codes, third-party website information, non-IM contact information, bank account and other payment methods, non-AliExpress platform identifiers, etc.

3、Violation Categories and Penalty Measures
-------------------------------------------

For the above-mentioned behavior of guiding offline transactions, the platform has the right to independently judge and impose the following penalties: Within one performance year (starting from the date of the first identified act of guiding offline transactions; the second performance year starts 365 days after the end of the first performance year, and so on):

（1）If identified as guiding offline transactions for the 1st to 5th times, deduct 1 point per occurrence from the store.

（2）If identified as guiding offline transactions for the 6th to 10th times, deduct 2 points per occurrence from the store.

（3）If identified as guiding offline transactions for the 11th time or more, deduct 3 points per occurrence from the store.
