AliExpress "Online Assessment" Rules

Latest revision date: May 6, 2022 (Beijing Time)

On April 19, 2022, AliExpress held its annual merchant summit and presented the three most important things for AliExpress in 2022. One of them is to "accelerate the improvement of global logistics fulfillment capabilities, incentivize merchants who fulfill orders quickly, and deliver goods within 72 hours with an online rate >90%." Fulfillment certainty is an important reason for consumers to continue repurchasing. In order to improve the consumer receiving experience and safeguard the rights and interests of more merchants with quality supply chains, one of the key areas for service improvement in 2022 is how to improve the 72-hour online rate and obtain more platform benefits.

This set of rules will introduce the definition of the online rate rule, assessment scope, incentive policies, control policies, and suggestions for improving shipping capabilities to help merchants improve their shipping abilities. These rules were officially released on April 28, 2022 (Beijing Time), and the public notice period for the rules is from April 28, 2022 to May 5, 2022. The rules will officially take effect from May 6, 2022.

1、Updates to the Online Rate Rules
----------------------------------

### （1）Description of the 24-hour/48-hour/72-hour/5-day online rate indicators

1) Numerator: The number of orders in the past 30 days that have been shipped within 24 hours/48 hours/72 hours/5 days after the logistics online time (minus the time for successful payment and risk control review).

2) Denominator: The number of orders that have been successfully paid (after risk control review) in the past 30 days, minus the number of canceled orders that were successfully canceled or expired.

3) The calculation is done based on Pacific Time, with a 7-day buffer for logistics online feedback delay. For example, the data on January 8 is the data from 30 days prior, starting from January 1.

4) All calculations are based on natural days, with the following exceptions:

**·** For orders shipped from mainland China, the effective time for calculation is Monday to Saturday. Sundays, public holidays, National Day holidays, and Spring Festival holidays are not included in the 24-hour/48-hour/72-hour/5-day period.

**·** For orders shipped from Hong Kong warehouses, the effective time for calculation is Monday to Friday. Saturdays, Sundays, public holidays, National Day holidays, and Spring Festival holidays are not included in the 24-hour/48-hour/72-hour/5-day period.

**·** For orders shipped from overseas warehouses, the effective time for calculation is Monday to Friday. Saturdays, Sundays, and holidays in respective countries are not included in the 24-hour/48-hour/72-hour/5-day period.

### （2）Assessment scope of online rate indicators

Taking into account merchants' operations and logistics collection and delivery situations, the following types of orders are temporarily not assessed for the online rate indicators, while all other orders will be included in the calculation of the 24-hour/48-hour/72-hour/5-day online rate indicators:

1) Customized attribute orders: Orders with a delivery period of more than 7 days are not assessed. A notice on the adjustment of customized attribute categories on AliExpress is expected to be released in May 2022. Please pay attention to platform notifications.

2) Links for price adjustment of special categories are not assessed.

3) Orders for special items (such as large items, liquid powders, etc.) that are shipped through custom shipping methods are not assessed.

4) For orders in overseas warehouse routes, orders generated using non-Cainiao official warehouse routes or non-platform direct trajectory data are not assessed.

5) Other situations are not assessed for a long time or temporarily based on platform discretion. For example, during recent global epidemic outbreaks, the platform will actively exempt merchants from responsibility based on the impact of the epidemic, and support for exemption indicators should be based on the latest announcements. For details, click here: 2022 Epidemic-related Shop Assessment Exemption Information Announcement Section, AliExpress and merchants working together during difficult times (constantly updated).

### （3）Querying and downloading details of the online rate indicators

Note: We recommend that you use the relevant pages to check the latest indicator rules after the rules come into effect on May 6. The details displayed on the product page should prevail.

1) You can log in to the seller's backend, and go to \[Store\] - \[My Store\] - \[Seller Service Score\], to check the online rate indicators for your store.

2) You can log in to the seller's backend, go to \[Business Insights\] - \[Logistics Overview\], to check the online rate indicators for your store.

3) You can log in to the seller's backend, go to \[Business Insights\] - \[Product Analysis\], to check the online rate indicators for your products.

### （4）FAQ

Q: What specific time does the logistics online time refer to in the online rate?

A: The logistics online time refers to the first information provided by the logistics provider. For online shipping, it is generally the time when the order is shipped from the warehouse, picked up by the delivery service provider, or delivered to the destination country. The actual shipping method should be used as the reference.

Q: When there are multiple logistics tracking numbers for the same transaction order, which logistics tracking number's time should be considered for the online time?

A: For a transaction order with one or more items, each item should have its corresponding shipping notification tracking number. All tracking numbers should have online logistics information within 24 hours/48 hours/72 hours/5 days in order for the order to be counted as an online order within that time frame. It is recommended to accurately fill in the tracking numbers corresponding to each item.

Q: For products belonging to a category with a set lead time of more than 7 days, is the assessment based on the actual lead time set for the product or the lead time set for the category the product belongs to?

A: The assessment is based on the actual lead time set for the product. If the lead time set for your actual product is ≤7 days, your orders will participate in the assessment as usual, and if they meet the criteria, you will enjoy the benefits.

2、Platform has a series of incentive policies and will implement them gradually for products and merchants with excellent delivery efficiency
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The 72-hour online rate indicator will be applied in search ranking, Gold and Silver Seller Access, marketing enrollment, and grouped order enrollment. Sellers with excellent online rates will have more opportunities to receive search recommendations, Gold and Silver Seller Access, and marketing enrollment opportunities.

（1）Positive impact on search ranking: Preferred warehouses & overseas warehouses > 24-hour online rate > 48-hour online rate > 72-hour online rate. Faster delivery will give your products a higher-ranking advantage on top of the natural search ranking.

（2）Grouped orders/cross-border expedited delivery, etc.: For products that meet the requirements of the 72-hour online rate, the platform will provide additional labeling, exposure, and exclusive marketing benefits. For details, click here to view the Introduction to Upgraded Grouped Orders and the Introduction to 72-hour expedited delivery.

（3）Gold and Silver Seller Access and Exclusion: Starting from July, the 72-hour online rate will be included in the assessment criteria for Gold and Silver Seller Access and Exclusion. The specific implementation details and timing will be announced at a later date. Please pay attention to platform notifications.

3、Platform benefits will be affected for products and merchants with slow delivery efficiency
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

（1）Platform marketing campaign access: The online rate will be included in the threshold for participating in platform marketing campaigns, and products that do not meet the criteria will not be able to participate in platform campaigns.

**·** Currently, the platform uses a 5-day online rate >80% for products in the store as the standard for participating in platform campaigns. For details, click here: \[AliExpress Rules\] - \[Marketing Rules\]. Products that do not meet the criteria will not be able to participate in platform campaigns.

**·** The standard for participating in marketing campaigns will gradually be upgraded to the 72-hour online rate. It is expected that important marketing fields on the platform will prioritize this starting in May. Please refer to the activity enrollment page for specific activities and criteria.

（2）Store service assessment: The indicator will be included in the merchant service score, and the platform will define the online rate assessment criteria in the merchant service score. If it is significantly lower than the industry standard, it may result in a lower search ranking.

4、Platform suggestions for improving the online rate
----------------------------------------------------

（1）We recommend that you maintain a certain level of inventory and manage your inventory well. Ship orders as soon as possible to improve customer satisfaction.

（2）Encourage stocking popular products in preferred warehouses and overseas warehouses to ensure inventory and achieve fast shipping and online rates. For instructions on stocking in preferred warehouses and overseas warehouses, click here to view the Preferred Warehouse System Operation Manual and Overseas Warehouse Introduction, and the Commitment to Reach Introduction.

（3）We recommend using the platform's grouped packaging feature, extending the online time by 12 to 48 hours. For instructions on using the grouped packaging feature, click here to view the Cross-Border Collection Service Online Introduction. If your region is not covered by the collection service, we recommend using the Cainiao Remote Area Collection Service. Click here to view the Cainiao Worry-Free Logistics Standard Route Introduction.

AliExpress

AliExpress reaffirms "seller's obligation to declare truthfully"

Dear Sellers,

According to relevant laws and regulations, sellers should voluntarily fulfill (or urge consumers to fulfill) tax and customs clearance obligations. Sellers must not understate, conceal, or falsely report transaction information at the import and export stages, nor help buyers evade or pay fewer taxes. Such violations include but are not limited to making statements or implications in store pages, product descriptions, or other channels of communication with buyers that various illegal tax avoidance operations can be carried out.

**Examples of violation information include but are not limited to:**

**·** avoid tax

**·** declare lower value

**·** avoid value-added tax

**·** tax evasion

**·** declared the item as a gift

To demonstrate the platform's prohibition attitude towards suspected illegal behavior, the Global AliExpress platform rules will add an item (8) to the "Illegal Profit" rule: For sales purposes, sellers are suspected of engaging in or assisting buyers in various illegal tax avoidance behaviors in any explicit or implicit manner. This modification will take effect from January 20, 2020.

Sellers are requested to thoroughly check and inspect their stores' product information. If there is any violation information mentioned above, please immediately delete and rectify it. The self-rectification period for sellers starts from the date of this announcement until January 20, 2020. After the self-rectification period, the platform will further strengthen the investigation of such violation information. Once discovered, the relevant products will be deleted, and 0.5 points will be deducted. In severe cases, the platform reserves the right to freeze or close the account.

Thank you for your attention and cooperation.

AliExpress

AliExpress "Transaction but Not Selling" Rules

Latest Revision Date: September 16, 2022, Beijing Time

1、Scope
-------

We are committed to making AliExpress the preferred platform for overseas buyers in cross-border shopping. It is the primary obligation of sellers to strictly adhere to the promised price, delivery time, logistics services, and product quality when fulfilling orders placed by buyers. However, the platform has found that some sellers have caused a large number of products to be undelivered due to their own reasons, resulting in the closure of orders due to delivery timeouts. This has caused extremely negative experiences for buyers, leading to disputes and complaints. In order to maintain a healthy and orderly marketplace and enhance the shopping experience for buyers on the platform, these rules are formulated.

2、Definition and Manifestations
-------------------------------

Definition of "Transaction but Not Selling": Refers to the behavior of sellers failing to ship the order after the buyer has made payment. The aforementioned delay refers to the failure to upload the tracking number before the seller's shipping timeout.

Based on the severity, the behavior of "Transaction but Not Selling" is categorized as general violation, severe violation, and particularly severe violation.

Examples of particularly severe violations of "Transaction but Not Selling" include but are not limited to the following situations, with particularly severe circumstances constituting particularly severe violations:

（1）A large number of "Transaction but Not Selling" orders or a significant proportion of "Transaction but Not Selling" orders in the seller's store within the past 7 days or 30 days.

（2）Intentional "Transaction but Not Selling" for improper purposes such as diverting traffic.

（3）Repeated occurrences of general violations of "Transaction but Not Selling".

3、Violation Categories and Penalty Measures
-------------------------------------------

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| **Violation Category** | **Penalty Measures** |
| General violation of "Transaction but Not Selling" | 2 points/times |
| Severe violation of "Transaction but Not Selling" | 12 points/times |
| Particularly severe violation of "Transaction but Not Selling" | 48 points/times |

AliExpress

[1、Scope](#UeBdo)

[2、Definition and Manifestations](#gHEtw)

[3、Violation Categories and Penalty Measures](#g9ldc)

- - -

AliExpress Explanation of the Assessment Criteria for "Transaction but Not Selling"

Effective Date: December 2, 2020, Beijing Time

Dear sellers,

It is the basic obligation of sellers to strictly adhere to the promised price, delivery time, logistics services, and product quality. In order to maintain a healthy and orderly marketplace, enhance the shopping experience of buyers on the platform, and help sellers better provide services to consumers, the following changes are made to the assessment criteria for "Transaction but Not Selling":

"Transaction but Not Selling" refers to the behavior of sellers failing to ship the order after the buyer has made payment. The aforementioned delay refers to the failure to upload the tracking number before the seller's shipping deadline (including cases where partial shipment is made but not all items are confirmed as shipped before the seller's shipping timeout), resulting in the order being closed by the system. Note: If the cancellation of the order is initiated by the buyer, it will not be counted as "Transaction but Not Selling" in the assessment. Please refer to the "Global AliExpress Transaction but Not Selling Rules" for more details.

**FAQ:**

Q: What is the current cancellation process in general?

A: If a consumer requests to cancel an order, the seller should respond within 72 hours. If there is no response from the seller within 72 hours, the order will be closed due to timeout, and the payment will be refunded to the buyer. The order status will be displayed as "Order Closed." Note: Buyer-initiated cancellations before payment do not require seller confirmation and will be automatically closed by the system.

  

Q: Will agreeing to a buyer's cancellation request have any impact on my store?

A: If the cancellation of the order is initiated by the buyer, any reasons for canceling the order will not have any impact on your store (it will not be counted as "Transaction but Not Selling"). Note: You do not need to guide the consumer to modify the cancellation reason. On the contrary, you can identify the shortcomings in store management through the reasons for order cancellations provided by consumers, which can help you better operate your store.

Q: Why was the order automatically closed even though I did not agree to the buyer's cancellation request?

A:

（1）If you do not respond within 72 hours, the order is affected by the cancellation rules and will be automatically closed.

（2）If you have engaged in some violations, the platform may close the order. For example, if the consumer complains about your lack of stock, price increase, refusal to ship, etc., and the platform verifies the evidence and finds the situation to be true, the order will be closed.

（3）For unpaid orders, buyer cancellations do not require your confirmation and will be automatically closed by the system.

Q: Does this apply to all orders or only to new orders?

A: This applies to all orders.

AliExpress

- - -

AliExpress "Unfair Competition" Rules

Latest Revision Date: September 16, 2022, Beijing Time

Alibaba's Global AliExpress platform has always been committed to maintaining an honest, fair, and just trading environment and continues to supervise and crack down on behaviors that affect the legitimate rights and interests of other users or the platform.

1、Definition and Manifestations
-------------------------------

（1）The product information, store decoration, or other information published by a seller creates confusion or misleads consumers and other sellers into believing that there is a specific connection with other sellers' normal operations.

（2）A seller engages in malicious behaviors such as intentionally placing orders, leaving malicious reviews, or making malicious complaints against other sellers, which affect the reputation and normal operations of other sellers.

Malicious Orders: Refers to a seller using an overseas member account to place orders against other sellers, which adversely affect their normal operations, such as placing orders for inventory without payment.

Malicious Reviews: Refers to a seller using an overseas member account to place orders against other sellers, intentionally leaving negative reviews or reviews that do not reflect the facts.

Malicious Complaints: Refers to a seller making complaints against other sellers through themselves or using other member accounts, with complaints lacking relevant evidence or improper complaint purposes, intending to damage the reputation of fellow sellers, extort legitimate sellers, or deliberately undermine the legitimate operations of fellow sellers.

Behaviors with particularly severe circumstances of unfair competition include but are not limited to the following situations:

（1）Causing severe negative impacts on the normal operations of other sellers.

（2）Causing serious misunderstandings, confusion, and significantly affecting the shopping experience of buyers.

（3）Making false statements or providing false supporting documents during the platform investigation process.

（4）Sellers who refuse platform reminders or rectification requests while knowingly and intentionally committing violations.

2、Violation and Penalties
-------------------------

Regarding the aforementioned unfair competition behaviors, the platform has the right to independently judge the severity of the violations and impose the following penalties:

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| **Violation Category** | **Penalty Measures** |     |
| General Violation | Being identified as engaging in "unfair competition" behavior for the first time, deduct 3 points from the store, and delete the products and store decoration information causing unfair competition. |     |
| Severe Violation | Being identified as engaging in "unfair competition" behavior for the second time, deduct 12 points from the store, freeze the account for 7 days, and delete the products and store decoration information causing unfair competition. |     |
| Particularly Severe Violation | Engaging in behaviors with particularly severe circumstances or being identified as engaging in "unfair competition" behavior three times or more, deduct 48 points from the store and close the store. |     |

AliExpress

[1、Definition and Manifestations](#x4OB2)

[2、Violation and Penalties](#xV65v)

- - -

AliExpress "Violation of Commitment Penalty" Rules

Latest Revision Date: September 16, 2022, Beijing Time

  

1、Definition and Manifestations
-------------------------------

Violation of commitment refers to the seller's failure to provide services to the buyer in accordance with the following commitments, thereby harming the legitimate rights of the buyer:

**（1）Commitments related to transactions and after-sales services, including but not limited to：**

1) The seller refuses to trade at the price agreed upon by the buyer (except for offline agreements between the two parties), or the seller promises discounts on the product price but fails to fulfill them.

2) The seller promises to provide the buyer with gifts or invoices, or other items beyond the transaction goods but fails to deliver or provide them.

3) The seller promises to provide after-sales services such as returns, exchanges, or repairs to the buyer but fails to fulfill them.

**（2）Commitments related to logistics, including but not limited to:**

1) The seller promises free shipping in the product title or content, but the buyer discovers that there is a shipping fee when placing the actual order.

2) The seller makes self-commitments or agrees with the buyer on specific shipping methods, logistics companies, etc., during the transaction process but fails to fulfill the relevant commitments or agreements.

3) The seller promises to bear the return shipping fee but fails to fulfill it.

**（3）Violation of established platform rules or requirements, including but not limited to:**

1) The platform requires both buyers and sellers to conduct transactions online, but the seller guides the buyer to not make payments and transactions through the AliExpress platform in various ways.

2) The seller participates in official AliExpress activities but fails to provide services according to the activity requirements (except for delivery time).

**（4）Sellers violating other commitments made by themselves.**

2、Violation Behaviors and Penalty Measures
------------------------------------------

For the aforementioned violation of commitment behaviors, the platform has the right to independently judge and impose the following penalties: Within one performance year (starting from the date of the first identified violation of commitment; the second performance year starts 365 days after the end of the first performance year, and so on):

（1）If identified as violating commitment behavior for the 1st to 5th times, deduct 1 point per occurrence from the store.

（2）If identified as violating commitment behavior for the 6th to 10th times, deduct 2 points per occurrence from the store.

（3）If identified as violating commitment behavior for the 11th time or more, deduct 3 points per occurrence from the store.

AliExpress

[2、Violation Behaviors and Penalty Measures](#e107o)

全球速卖通针对商品信息中包含marijuana禁限词的商品整治公告

发布日期：北京时间2015/10/12

尊敬的速卖通平台卖家：  
根据相关部门紧急通知，即日起速卖通平台全面整治信息中包含marijuana（中文释义：大麻）禁限词的商品，请卖家做好自查，本周内（10.12-10.19）尽快将相关包含marijuana禁限词的商品进行修改调整或删除操作，包含但不限于图片，标题文字，详细描述等。  
平台将于**2015年10月19日**针对已发布上线的产品信息中包含marijuana禁限词的商品做统一删除处理，此次调整暂不作扣分处罚处理，平台禁限售相关规则了解请[点击](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647)。

Legislative Decree no. 101 of 2020

**LEGISLATIVE DECREE NO 101 OF 31 JULY 2020**

Implementation of Directive 2013/59/Euratom, concerning the establishment of basic safety standards for protection against the dangers arising from exposure to ionising radiation and repealing Directives 89/618/Euratom, 90/641/Euratom, 96/29/Euratom, 97/43/Euratom and 2003/122/Euratom and reordering of sector legislation in implementation of Article 20(1)(a) of Law No 117 of 4 October 2019.

_(Official Gazette General Series No. 201, 12.08.2020 - Ordinary Supplement No. 29)_

Entry into force of the measure: 27/08/2020

**Article 39 - Prohibition of practices** _(Directive 2013/59/Euratom, Articles 20 and 21; Legislative Decree No. 230 of 17 March 1995, Article 98)_

1、The intentional addition of radioactive substances, directly or by activation, in the production of:

（1）hygiene and cosmetic products

（2）objects for domestic or personal use

（3）toys;

（4）food and beverages;

（5）animal feed;

（6）lightning protection devices.

2、Also prohibited are:

（1）the import, acquisition by means of electronic commerce, export, trade, distribution, use, handling of products referred to in paragraph 1 to which radioactive materials are deliberately added, either directly or by activation;

（2）practices involving the activation of materials resulting in increased activity in consumer products;

（3）practices involving the activation of materials used in toys and articles for personal use, and the import and export of such products or materials

（4）the use on persons of sources of ionising radiation which is not carried out for diagnostic, therapeutic or clinical scientific research purposes, except as provided for in Article 169;

（5）the production, import, use or, in any event, the placing on the market of electronic apparatus for remote viewing or in any case suitable for the electronic reproduction of images, which emit ionising radiation at levels exceeding those established by decree of the Minister of Health, in agreement with the Ministers of Economic Development and of the Environment and Protection of Land and Sea, after consulting ISIN.

\------------------------------------------------------------------

GENERAL DIRECTORATE FOR HEALTH PREVENTION

OFFICE IV - PREVENTION OF PHYSICAL CHEMICAL,

BIOLOGICAL RISK AND ENVIRONMENTAL HEALTH PROMOTION,

PROTECTION OF HEALTH AND SAFETY IN THE WORKPLACE

To the Command of the NAS for the Protection of Health in Milan

To the company Alibaba Italy S.r.l.

  

**Object:** Request for clarification regarding the Health Ministry note: Reporting household and personal items containing radioactive material for sale on e-commerce channels. Ban on the sale and blackout of products from sales sites.

With reference to the inspection carried out by the Milan NAS on 16 December at the registered office of Alibaba Italy S.r.l. and to the latter's requests, the following is reported.

Thanking for your cooperation, it is considered that the blackout of online sales should concern products containing the word ‘_tritium’_ or ‘_trizio’_ in the search bar and/or product description.

As for Italy, it should be noted that Article 39(1) of Legislative Decree No. 101/2020 contains the following punctual list of products for which the ban on the sale of articles with intentionally added tritium is in force:

_（1）hygiene and cosmetic products;_

_（2）household or personal items;_

_（3）toys;_

_（4）food and drink;_

_（5）animal feed._

Well, the blackout of online sales should, in general, concern all the above-mentioned product categories.

Finally, in order to ensure correct information to users, is permitted the publication of this explanatory note sent to this company.

With regard to withdrawal from the market and disposal, these will be ordered by the competent offices, as soon as the detection and quantification of the problem has been completed.

The Director of Office IV

Dr. Pasqualino Rossi

全球速卖通关于禁止销售含Nitrous Oxide商品的公告

发布日期：北京时间2019/9/5

亲爱的速卖通卖家：

依据中国 《危险化学品安全管理条例》 、危险化学品目录（2015版）的相关规定，速卖通平台禁止销售含Nitrous Oxide 商品。即日起到9月30日（清理期时间），请所有卖家对店铺内商品进行自检自查，立即停止销售并删除相关商品。自10月1日起，平台将对此类商品进行删除及扣分处置（每次2分）；情节严重的，平台有权进行账号冻结或关闭。

AliExpress Ban on the Sale of Mercury-containing Products

  

**Dear sellers:**

AliExpress is always committed to maintaining an orderly marketplace in compliance with all local laws, regulations and providing consumers with safe and high-quality goods. On January 19, 2013, the United Nations Environment Programme (UNEP) adopted the Minamata Convention, an international treaty aimed at controlling and reducing global mercury emissions. As of now, 137 countries have joined the Minamata Convention and have committed to gradually phasing out and restricting the production and import/export of mercury-containing products to reduce mercury emissions and exposure. Due to the requirements of the relevant international conventions, laws and regulations and regulatory requirements of various countries, in order to protect the rights and interests of users and the ecological environment, and maintain the sustainable and healthy development of the AliExpress, AliExpress prohibits the listing and sale of Mercury-containing products.

Based on the above conventions and related regulations, AliExpress has banned the sale of liquid mercury and mercury-containing products and closed related categories from May 1, 2022.

【Products Scope】
----------------

1、Prohibited products include, but are not limited:

**·** Mercury-containing switches, mercury-containing lamps, mercury-containing batteries;

**·** Mercury measuring instruments;

**·** Mercury thermometers, mercury sphygmomanometers, and other mercury-containing medical devices;

**·** Consumer novelty products with added mercury, such as toys, games, cards, jewelry, clothing, and shoes;

**·** Thermostats;

**·** Wheel balancing weights;

**·** Cosmetics containing mercury or mercury compounds, including mercury-containing creams;

**·** Mercury Lamps;

**·** Mercury-based pesticides, insecticides, preservatives, etc.

【Controlled Area】
-----------------

**Global**

【Control measures】
------------------

AliExpress has banned the sale of mercury-containing commodities on May 1, 2022, and closed the category of mercury-containing lighting lamps. **From Beijing time on December 1, 2023, the platform will upgrade the control measure. If the above-mentioned illegal products are found, the platform will follow the AliExpress platform rule to delete the products and deduct 2 points for each violation.**

AliExpress members shall list and sell products in accordance with applicable rules and abide by applicable laws and regulations of any country of origin and any country of destination. Where any member is found to be listing products or releasing information in violation of the rules, AliExpress will delist or delete the related products or information and punish the violator in accordance with relevant rules. For a member that knowingly circumvents the rules, provides information about prohibited products in any interaction scenarios (e.g., chats, live-streaming), violates the rules repeatedly, is criticized in any form of media circulated by a regulator, receives negative publicity published by media, or commits any other serious violation, AliExpress will impose penalties, including but not limited to deleting product information, deducting points, blocking stores, restricting access to the website's product features, and freezing or even closing the account, in accordance with the platform's relevant rules.

【Reference】
-----------

[The Minamata Convention on Mercury](https://www.mercuryconvention.org/en)

[Regulation (EU) 2017/852 of the European Parliament and of the Council of 17 May 2017 on mercury, and repealing Regulation (EC) No 1102/2008](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/legal-content/EN/TXT/?uri=CELEX%3A32017R0852&qid=1648885378666)

[The Control of Mercury (Enforcement) Regulations 2017](https://www.mee.gov.cn/gkml/hbb/bgg/201708/t20170816_419736.htm)

[中国《关于汞的水俣公约》生效公告](https://www.mee.gov.cn/gkml/hbb/bgg/201708/t20170816_419736.htm)

Note: The above information does not constitute any legal advice and shall not be deemed or represent the legal opinion or conclusion of the regulatory body. Further, we do not undertake or warrant that the information represents the latest laws and regulations. For specific information, please consult the competent authority, law firms, or third-party certification/testing/consulting companies in the target country or region.

AliExpress.com will continue to monitor the changes in laws and related policies of countries worldwide, and adjust our platform rules accordingly. Please contact our online customer service for any further queries.

AliExpress

全球速卖通关于枪支及零配件产品禁限售规则解读及发品规范

生效日期：北京时间2022/7/26

  

一、管控背景
------

根据**《**中华人民共和国枪支管理法》，国家严格管制枪支。禁止任何单位或者个人违反法律规定持有、制造（包括变造、装配）、买卖、运输、出租、出借枪支。

全球速卖通平台（以下简称为“平台”或“速卖通”）禁止发布、许诺销售或许诺购买任何可能对他人造成危害的枪类商品，包含国内外法律规定的任何真枪、仿真枪、以及真枪或仿真枪的零部件等商品。

二、禁止发布商品范围
----------

1、平台禁止发布枪支商品：

枪支主要是指以火药或者压缩气体等为动力，利用管状器具发射金属弹丸或者其他物质，足以致人伤亡或者丧失知觉的各种枪支。枪⽀分为两⼤类，制式枪⽀和⾮制式枪⽀。

根据用途分为军用枪支/公务用枪支/民用枪支，包含但不限于猎枪、手枪、步枪、冲锋枪、发令枪、改制射钉枪、电磁线圈枪及任何形式的伪装枪等。

包括但不限于以下示例：

2、平台禁止发布仿真枪：

凡符合以下条件之一的，可以认定为仿真枪：

（1）符合《中华人民共和国枪支管理法》规定的枪支构成要件，所发射金属弹丸或其他物质的枪口比动能小于1.8焦耳/平方厘米（不含本数）、大于0.16焦耳/平方厘米（不含本数）的；（枪口比动能的计算，按照《枪支致伤力的法庭科学鉴定判据》规定的计算方法执行）

（2）具备枪支外形特征，并且具有与制式枪支材质和功能相似的枪管、枪机、机匣或者击发等机构之一的；

（3）外形、颜色与制式枪支相同或者近似，并且外形长度尺寸介于相应制式枪支全枪长度尺寸的二分之一与一倍之间的。

\*制式枪支：国内制造的制式枪支是指已完成定型试验，并且经军队或国家有关主管部门批准投入装备、使用(含外贸出口)的各类枪支。国外制造的制式枪支是指制造商已完成定型试验，并且装备、使用或投入市场销售的各类枪支。

\*全枪长：是指从枪管口部至枪托或枪机框(适用于无枪托的枪支)底部的长度。

根据以上标准，仿真枪可包含但不限于气枪、BB枪、彩弹枪、钢珠枪、鱼枪、钢笔枪、火柴枪、迷你大炮等。

包括但不限于以下示例：

3、平台禁止发布枪支零部件：

真枪及仿真枪支的零部件（包括枪支内部部件及外部部件），枪支零部件一般为可用于或描述用于组装枪支或者替换任何枪支组成部分的产品，包含但不限于枪托、握把、枪支架、子弹匣、扳机、扳机护圈、消音器、闪光抑制器、改制射钉枪散件、秃鹰气枪内部散件、pcp气枪内部散件、气枪枪机、气瓶、气枪用阀体、枪支气体及其他具备枪支零部件相同功能的装置等。

包括但不限于以下示例：

4、平台禁止发布枪支专用工具：

本处枪支专用工具主要指用于组装或拆卸枪支的专用工具，包含但不限于军用扳手、冲孔器、快速装弹器、弹匣装弹器等。发布枪支专用工具，参照枪支零部件处置措施。

包括但不限于以下示例：

三、平台允许发布产品及发品规范
---------------

1、儿童玩具枪及其零附件：

允许发布不具备危害性的儿童玩具枪及其零附件（但对符合《仿真枪认定标准》的玩具枪及其零附件，视同仿真枪禁售）。

2、枪支周边产品（非枪支组成部件）：

允许发布枪支周边产品（非枪支组成部件），如保养工具、包装工具、光学仪具等

2.1 保养工具：清洗工具、润滑油等

2.2 包装工具：枪套、枪背带、枪盒等

2.3 光学仪具：非枪械专用的光学仪具等

3、发布规范要求

3.1 商品信息展示要求：

3.1 玩具枪产品信息应当使用合规展示(包含商品描述/图片/视频等)：

3.1.1 标明儿童玩具用途、玩具枪尺寸、玩具枪材质、玩具子弹材质等。

AliExpress Announcement on Banning the Sale of Automobile and Motorcycle Parts Products Suspected of Refitting as Gun Silencers

Release date: July 30, 2024

Revision date: /

**Dear Sellers:**

AliExpress is always committed to maintaining an orderly marketplace in compliance with all local laws, regulations and providing consumers with safe and high-quality goods. In order to protect the rights and interests of platform users, AliExpress (hereinafter referred to as "AliExpress" or "Platform") prohibits the listing and sale of the following products.

\[Prohibited Products\]
-----------------------

AliExpress prohibits the listing and sale of gun silencers and automobile oil filters and/or other automobile and motorcycle parts that are suspected of being refitted as gun silencers. Gun silencer related products are strictly prohibited in virous countries around the world.

Prohibited products include but are not limited to the following types:

\[Control measures\]
--------------------

If the above-mentioned products are found, AliExpress will implement corresponding penalties in accordance with the Prohibited and Restricted Sales Rules of the Platform：

1、Platform will delete the product with 2 points deducted.

2、If serious violations, and it will be regarded as not obeying the ban on the sale of gun accessories, Platform will delete the product with 6 points deducted.

Sellers shall list and sell products in accordance with applicable rules and abide by applicable laws and regulations of any country of origin and any country of destination. Where any Seller is found to be listing products or releasing information in violation of the rules, AliExpress will delist or delete the related products or information and punish the violator in accordance with relevant rules. For a Seller that knowingly circumvents the rules, provides information about prohibited products in any interaction scenarios (e.g., chats, live-streaming), violates the rules repeatedly, is criticized in any form of media circulated by a regulator, receives negative publicity published by media, or commits any other serious violation, AliExpress will impose penalties, including but not limited to deleting product information, deducting points, blocking stores, restricting access to the website's product features, and freezing or even closing the account, in accordance with the platform's relevant rules.

\[References\]
--------------

1、[U.S.: National Firearms Act of 1934](https://homicide.northwestern.edu/docs_fk/homicide/laws/national_firearms_act_of_1934.pdf)

2、[Australia: Customs (Prohibited Imports) Regulations 1956](https://www.legislation.gov.au/F1996B03651/2016-08-07/text)

Note: The above information does not constitute any legal advice and shall not be deemed or represent the legal opinion or conclusion of the regulatory body. Further, we do not undertake or warrant that the information represents the latest laws and regulations. For specific information, please consult the competent authority, law firms, or third-party certification/testing/consulting companies in the target country or region. AliExpress.com will continue to monitor the changes in laws and related policies of countries worldwide, and adjust our platform rules accordingly. Please contact our online customer service for any further queries.

Thank you for your support and attention.

AliExpress

全球速卖通枪型玩具发品规范

发布日期：北京时间2023/12/12

本文涉及Aliexpress平台对枪型玩具及相关商品的管控标准，请商家在发品时加以注意，以免违规而触发商品扣分删除。

一、符合《仿真枪认定标准》的枪型玩具及其零附件，视同仿真枪全球禁售
---------------------------------

仿真枪定义：

凡符合以下条件之一的，可以认定为仿真枪：

（1）符合《中华人民共和国枪支管理法》规定的枪支构成要件，所发射金属弹丸或其他物质的枪口比动能小于1.8焦耳/平方厘米（不含本数）、大于0.16焦耳/平方厘米（不含本数）的；（枪口比动能的计算，按照《枪支致伤力的法庭科学鉴定判据》规定的计算方法执行）

（2）具备枪支外形特征，并且具有与制式枪支材质和功能相似的枪管、枪机、机匣或者击发等机构之一的；

（3）外形、颜色与制式枪支相同或者近似，并且外形长度尺寸介于相应制式枪支全枪长度尺寸的二分之一与一倍之间的。

\*制式枪支：国内制造的制式枪支是指已完成定型试验，并且经军队或国家有关主管部门批准投入装备、使用(含外贸出口)的各类枪支。国外制造的制式枪支是指制造商已完成定型试验，并且装备、使用或投入市场销售的各类枪支。

\*全枪长：是指从枪管口部至枪托或枪机框(适用于无枪托的枪支)底部的长度。

\*颜色：不可发布主颜色为黑色、灰色、银色、沙色、迷彩色、军绿色、棕色等非明亮色系（或这几种颜色的混合）。

禁止发布示例（包括但不限于）：

二、使用图片模糊或者全文字描述进行规避行为视同仿真枪禁售
----------------------------

在商品主图、营销图、sku图、商详页使用模糊图片或者文字描述管控颜色的行为均视同为仿真枪管控，全球禁售

禁止发布包括但不限于以下示例：

------------

**1、主颜色为明亮色系的仿真外观枪型玩具（明亮色主要包括：白色、亮红色、亮橙色、亮黄色、亮绿色、亮蓝色、亮粉色或亮紫色单独或作为主要颜色与其他颜色组合）**

允许发布包括但不限于以下示例：

**2、尺寸小于制式枪支二分之一的仿真外观枪型玩具**

允许发布包括但不限于以下示例：

**3、积木枪（拼装完成后外观明显能看出与仿真枪无关的）**

允许发布包括但不限于以下示例：

全球速卖通刀具类商品发布规范

一、总则
----

为了进一步规范全球速卖通平台（以下称“平台”）刀具商品的发布行为，维护平台有序的市场秩序，提升会员的用户体验，特依据[《全球速卖通平台规则(卖家规则)》](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/?tocUuid=zWSCDsWL57obW4AZ)，制订《全球速卖通刀具类商品发布规范》（以下称“本规则”）。平台禁止发布管制器具类相关商品，请会员发布商品前先阅读下方的“参考范例”，了解并遵守平台发布的禁售及产品发布规则。

三、特定用途刀具发布规范
------------

#### 1、厨房超规刀具范围及发布要求：

**范围定义：**厨房刀具，包含但不限于屠宰刀、放血刀、剥皮刀、分骨刀、剔骨刀、砍骨刀、切肉刀、料理刀、刺身刀、主厨刀、面包刀、西瓜刀等。

厨房超规刀具，包含以上刀具种类且刀尖角度大于60度，刀身长（刃长）超过220mm，刀柄长超过160mm，全刀长最大值不超过400mm（物流限制）。平台已于2025年4月21日开放厨房超规刀具POP模式售卖，首期已开放美国地区，本次将新增开放欧洲地区（除英国外）；商家需在商品信息处上传承诺函及盖章备案，资质审核通过后选择3PL物流线路。请会员发布商品前先阅读下方的“发布范例”，了解并遵守平台发布的禁售及产品发布规则。

**（1）发布规范图示：**

商品详情和属性展示刀尖角度、刃身长（刃长）、刀柄长、全刀长最大值，厨用尖刀（刀尖角度小于70度）需在商品副图展示标尺量刃长和量角器量刀尖角度（刀刃与刀背上距离刀尖顶点10mm的两点与刀尖顶点形成的角度），刀具平行摆放对齐0刻度。

**（2）叶子类目：**

**家居用品>厨房吧台用品>厨房刀具及附件>厨师刀（特殊厨房刀具），**必须发布至该叶子类目**，否则将无法发品。**

**（5）物流线路选择：**

选择3PL线路→仅美国/欧洲（除英国外）可见可售→选择**HUAHAN\_SSG\_STANDARD （华翰特敏标准专线）**

**（6）相关资料模版：**

**1）卖家自我承诺声明模版：**[**点此下载**](https://files.alicdn.com/tpsservice/31142b88511884fd582345174e916906.docx)

**2）刀具生产/销售备案证：**根据法律法规要求，目前《特种刀具生产许可证》已取消，生产管制刀具的企业向公安机关备案后可以生产，生产备案表样式：（若非刀具生产方 即中间采购商，需补充提交刀具备案证、与刀具生产方的采购协议）

**· 管制刀具生产企业，公安机关进行备案表样式（需盖章），具体以公安机关备案格式为准：**

**· 管制刀具销售企业，公安机关进行备案表样式（需盖章），具体以公安机关备案格式为准：**

#### 2、文具类刀具范围及发布要求：

**（1）****范围定义：**文具类刀具，包含但不限于裁纸刀、切纸刀、美工刀、壁纸刀、削笔刀等。

**（2）****禁售范围：**文具刀具刀尖角度小于60度，刀身长（刃长）不得超过150mm，刀柄长不得超过140mm，全刀长最大值不得超过290mm；刀尖角度大于60度，刀身长（刃长）不得超过220mm，刀柄长不得超过160mm，全刀长最大值不得超过380mm。

**（3）****发布规范：**商品详情和属性展示刀尖角度、刃身长（刃长）、刀柄长、全刀长最大值，文具类刀具（刀尖角度小于70度）需在商品副图展示标尺量刃长和量角器量刀尖角度（刀刃与刀背上距离刀尖顶点10mm的两点与刀尖顶点形成的角度），刀具平行摆放对齐0刻度。

#### 3、户外刀具范围及发布规范

**（1）****范围定义：**户外刀具，包含但不限于户外类的直刀、折刀以及刀刃弯曲的爪刀。

**（2）****禁售范围：**户外刀具刀身（刃长）不得超过100mm；其他折叠刀具，刀身展开后，可被弹簧或卡锁固定自锁的折叠刀具（弹簧刀、蝴蝶刀、重力刀等），以及其他刀身（刃长）超过100毫米。

**（3）****发布规范：**商品详情和属性中展示刀尖角度、刃身长（刃长）、刀柄长、全刀长、刀具是否带自锁或弹簧力；商品附图展示带有清晰刻度标尺的托，与刀刃平行摆放，刀尖对准尺子的0刻度；多功能刀具展示多功能部分或按标尺规范展示。

#### 4、农用刀具范围及发布规范

**（1）****范围定义：**农用刀具，包含但不限于砍柴刀、篾竹刀。

**（2）****禁售范围：**农用刀具刀尖角度小于60度，刀身（刃长）不得超过150mm；刀尖角度大于60度，刀身（刃长）不得超过220mm。

**（3）****发布规范：**商品详情和属性中展示刀尖角度、刀身长（刃长）。

#### 5、工艺刀剑范围及发布规范

**（1）****范围定义：**工艺刀剑包含但不限于武士刀、武士剑、汉刀、唐刀、清刀等。

**（2）****禁售范围：**工艺刀剑不得发布开刃刀剑及相关服务，不得发布金属材质的武士刀、武士剑、汉刀、唐刀、清刀等。

**（3）****发布规范：**刀剑类工艺冷兵器，需在商品标题写明未开刃；木质或塑料等非金属刀剑（包含玩具、模型等刀类商品）需在商品标题里明示材质、注明未开刃。商品详情和属性里需展示刀尖角度、刀身长（刃长）、刀身材质以及是否开刃。

四、管制刀具商品禁限售规则
-------------

依据中华人民共和国《对部分刀具实行管制的暂行规定》、《人民警察使用警械和武器条例》、《武器、警械管理制度》、《管制刀具认定标准》，香港特别行政区《武器條例》，英国《攻击性武器限制法》等相关法律法规的规定，全球速卖通平台禁止发布管制刀具商品。如存在以下情形，平台将依据[《全球速卖通禁限售规则(含违禁信息列表)》](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647)第（四）项 “管制器具” 执行管理。

**（一）管制刀具禁止销售**，包括但不限于以下情形：

1、刃长大于等于100mm的超长刀具（不包括厨房专用刀、美工刀等特殊用途刀具）；

2、带有血槽的刀具；

3、刀身展开后，可被弹簧或卡锁固定自锁的折叠刀具（弹簧刀、蝴蝶刀、重力刀等），以及其他刀身（刃长）超过100毫米；

4、开刃的武术及工艺礼品刀具；

5、少数民族用刀，如藏刀、腰刀、靴刀、马刀等；

6、三棱刀具以及三棱军刺、刺刀、拳刺、手刺（机械用三棱刮刀、三棱刺刀等）；

7、双刃刀，具有2个及以上刀刃的刀具；

8、特定用途刀具如屠宰类刀具、厨房类刀具、文具类刀具、农用类刀具等，需遵循特定用途刀具发布规范；

9、平台已禁售的其他管制刀具类型。

**（二）****禁售管制刀具产品图例（包括但不限于以下）**

1、匕首：带有刀柄、刀格和血槽，刀尖角度小于60度的单刃、双刃或多刃尖刀（见图一）。

（图一）

2、三棱刮刀：具有三个刀刃的机械加工用刀具（见图二）。

（图二）

3、带有自锁装置的弹簧刀（跳刀）：刀身展开或弹出后，可被刀柄内的弹簧或卡锁固定自锁的折叠刀具（见图三）。

（图三）

4、其他相类似的单刃、双刃、三棱尖刀：刀尖角度小于60度，刀身长度超过150毫米的各类单刃、双刃和多刃刀具（见图四）。

（图四）

5、其他刀尖角度大于60度，刀身长度超过220毫米的各类单刃、双刃和多刃刀具（见图五）。

（图五）

五、违规处理
------

平台禁止发布相关商品及服务，请各卖家对店铺和商品进行自查，按照本规则进行商品发布，删除并停止出售以上相关违规商品及服务，避免产生违规处置。

对于违反本规则的行为，平台将根据[《全球速卖通卖家基础规则（违规及处罚规则）》](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523039)[《全球速卖通禁限售规则（含违禁信息列表）》](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647)的规定，对违规商品信息予以下架或删除，相关订单如买家已付款，无论物流状况如何，均全额退款给买家，卖家承担全部责任，并根据违规行为的严重程度，对卖家给予冻结账户或关闭账户的处罚。

普通刀具依据本规则需要在特定类目下销售，如错放类目针对相关商品第一次进行下架，第二次进行一般违规扣分，2分/次；一般违规，一天内（即首次违规处罚时间起24小时内）累计扣分不超过12分；严重违规每次扣48分，关闭账号；针对恶意规避等情节特别严重行为（包含但不限于采用对商品信息隐藏、遮挡、模糊处理等隐匿的手段规避平台管理），平台保留直接扣除48分，关闭账号的权利。

六、相关问题解答
--------

1、自锁刀可以发布吗？

刀具的自锁装置，是指折刀在使用过程中，为了防止因为用力而产生刀刃回折，对使用者的手部造成伤害而设置的一种锁闭机构，通常见到的有线锁、轴锁、背锁和弹簧刀的锁定装置，由于对人体有伤害，因此在平台上也是禁止发布的。

2、Cosplay用的动漫刀可以发布么？

除了刀刃为金属材质的武士刀，其他的动漫刀可以发布，须按相应类目要求发布。

3、少数民族刀可以发布么？

少数民族刀具只允许在自治区销售，而网络销售势必存在跨地域情况，所以少数民族藏刀、腰刀、靴刀、马刀等都是不可以发布的。其他的少数民族刀具则沿用管制刀具的判断标准，是否自锁、有血槽或者超长等。

4、陶瓷材质的刀具可以发布么？

陶瓷类刀具须符合上述管控要求和商品发布要求。

由于陶瓷类刀具具有超高硬度、超高耐磨、刃口锋利等特点，其技术特性已达到或超过了部分金属刀具的性能，对符合管制刀具认定标准规定的刀具类型、刀刃长度和刀尖角度等条件的陶瓷类刀具，应当作为管制刀具管理。

七、附则
----

1、本规则自2022年8月15日起生效，请商家对照规则详情自行整改属性和发布类目。

2、2022年9月1日起，平台将依据规则对违规商品下架或删除处理。

3、平台享有对本规则的解释权，并有权依据业务发展及法律法规要求，对本规则进行修改。最新规则修订请关注平台通知。

历史公告内容：[速卖通刀具整改通知](https://sale.aliexpress.com/seller/forbiddennotice.htm?spm=5261.170.0.1.YT6N9o)

全球速卖通关于禁售伪装刀具的公告

发布日期：北京时间2024/4/9

最新版本修订日期：/

尊敬的速卖通商家：

根据相关法律法规和监管要求，结合[全球速卖通平台禁限售规则](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647)，为保护消费者安全，更好地保证平台商品符合国内外相关法律法规规定，保障平台用户权益以及促进全球速卖通平台（以下简称为“AliExpress”或“平台”）的持续健康发展，AliExpress特此强调禁止平台商家销售以下商品。

【商品管控范围】
--------

**全球速卖通禁止商家发布并销售**伪装刀，即一切伪装成非刀具、实则是刀具的商品。伪装刀属于平台禁止销售的危害他人生命安全的商品，风险点在于其伪装性，不易被人发觉，而不在于刀具长度，故不存在刀长短及角度的要求，一切伪装成非刀具实则是刀具的商品，对此，为保障消费者安全，平台将定义相关产品为伪装刀具，并进行相应管控。

管控商品包括且不仅限于下示例：

皮带刀

  
梳子刀

  
手表手链式伪装刀

钥匙刀

  
手电筒伪装刀

笔刀

【管控地区】
------

**全球范围**

【管控措施】
------

全球速卖通禁止商家销售伪装刀，若发现上述违规商品，平台将按照全球速卖通平台禁限售规则执行对应处罚：商品删除，并扣6分。  
平台提醒广大商家合规发品及合规交易，商家有责任遵守任何本国及销售目的地适用的商品合规法律，发布违规商品及信息的商家，平台将依照相关平台规则进行处罚。对恶意绕过规则、在任何场景（如沟通、直播等交互场景）发布违规信息、重复违规、被监管部门通告、被重要媒体曝光以及存在其他严重违规情节的会员，依据平台相关规则，平台将采取包括但不限于对相关产品及信息执行对应国家屏蔽、删除产品信息、扣分、屏蔽店铺、限制使用网站产品功能、冻结账号直至关闭账号的处罚。

**我们将会持续关注各国的相关政策和外部风险情况变化，并据此进行平台管控政策和管控范围的相应调整。**

【法规依据】
------

1、Australia: Austrian Arms Act of 1996 (Waffengesetz 1996) https://www.ris.bka.gv.at/GeltendeFassung.wxe?Abfrage=Bundesnormen&Gesetzesnummer=10006016  
2、UK: The Criminal Justice Act 1988 (Offensive Weapons) https://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1988/2019  
3、Australia: Customs (Prohibited Imports) Regulations 1956

https://www.legislation.gov.au/F1996B03651/latest/text  
4、Netherlands: Weapons and Ammunition Act (Wet wapens en munitie)  
[https://wetten.overheid.nl/BWBR0008804/2017-09-01](https://wetten.overheid.nl/BWBR0008804/2017-09-01)

全球速卖通严禁利用VR眼镜销售和传播低俗、色情、淫秽电子信息的公告

发布日期：北京时间2017/3/2

尊敬的全球速卖通卖家：  
为了规范虚拟眼镜市场，依据《中华人民共和国刑法》、《中华人民共和国治安管理处罚法》、《全国人民代表大会常务委员会关于维护互联网安全的决定》等相关法律法规以及平台规则，速卖通平台严禁出售或传播低俗、色情、淫秽物品。现对平台上virtual reality glasses(VR眼镜)产品进行管控，卖家不得利用在销售VR眼镜时搭售或传播低俗、色情和淫秽电子信息。具体的商品发布规范如下：  
1、商品需要发布在正确的类目: ConsumerElectronics> VR Devices > 3D Glasses/ Virtual Reality Glasses  
2、商品图片不得使用低俗、色情淫秽或带有快播标识的图片，图片中的文字及商品信息不得出现蕴含低俗、色情淫秽内容的文字或图片， 包括但不限于“sex”、“adult”、“porn”、“pussy”等明示或者暗示低俗、色情淫秽信息的用语，提供以下案例供各位卖家参考：

  
【正确案例】:  

全球速卖通

- - -

AliExpress Notice on the Prohibition of Adult/Sex Product Listings Suspected to Involve Minors

Release date: July 16, 2020

Revision date: /

  

Dear AliExpress Sellers:

It is emphasized that posting or selling any listings or content related to or suspected of being related to child and minor pornography is a serious violation on AliExpress (hereinafter referred to as the "Platform" or "AliExpress"). The Platform will strengthen its efforts to control and address such violations. For any violations, the offending products will be immediately removed from the Platform, and the corresponding punishment will be implemented to the seller/store until seller account closure in accordance the applicable rules. Please ensure compliance with the following requirements.

The sale of sex dolls is subject to the following requirements:

1) The sale of sex dolls shorter than 140cm is strictly prohibited;

2) Packaging, advertising, product names, or descriptions must not directly or indirectly involve minors, including text and image descriptions. Product images must not depict minors’ features or show the features of minors. Any textual or image violation will result in a penalty;

3) Any seller who may attempt to circumvent the Platform’s control by ways like miscategorizing, deliberately obscuring, or blurring images will be severely punished.

Textual violations include, but are not limited to, the following:

1) Words that directly have the meaning that the product represents a minor, such as child, kid, infant, underage, school girl, loli, Lolita, teenager, maiden, virgin, and words for children under 17, young girls, and lolis;

2) Words that indirectly imply the meaning that the product represents a minor, such as little, teen, baby, young, small, mini, minor, petty, etc. Using words like "minute" or "young" to describe girls or boys, implying an age group.

The platform identifies image violations by considering the following criteria, including but not limited to:

1) The features or characteristics of minors: face shape, figure, body type, etc.

2) The appearance of minors: hairstyles (e.g., pigtails, cartoon hair clips), accessories (e.g., red scarves, green scarves, etc., children's identification markers), clothing (e.g., school uniforms, cartoon-patterned clothes, princess dresses, children's shoes, princess stockings, etc.);

3) The setting of scenes that suggest minors: props (e.g., plush toys, backpacks, Barbie dolls, etc.), scenes (e.g., schools, children's playgrounds, etc.);

4) Other settings that may imply minors or emphasize the concepts of "small" or "young".

Example of prohibited images:

AliExpress

- - -

全球速卖通关于平台上窃听窃照设备风险的处理

发布日期：北京时间2016/1/7

尊敬的速卖通平台卖家：

根据国家关于《禁止非法生产销售使用窃听窃照专用器材和“伪基站”设备的规定》及平台《[禁限售规则](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647)》，速卖通平台一直禁止销售用于非法摄像、录音、取证等用途的设备（如隐蔽伪装式录音或摄像设备），若平台核实为该类禁限产品，将执行严格的处罚措施。

同时，近期平台排查发现部分产品存在较为严重的关键词滥用现象，包括但不限于spy、spy camera、hidden camera、spy audio、hidden audio等类似禁限词的电子商品。请卖家即日起开展自查，若您销售的商品符合国家及平台规则，但误用了上述禁限词，请即日起进行修改调整，包含但不限于图片，标题文字，详细描述等。

平台将于2016年1月25日针对已发布上线的产品信息中包含spy、spy camera、hidden camera、spy audio、hidden audio及类似禁限词的商品做统一删除处理。

相关规则了解：  
禁限售规则：[https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647)  

  
全球速卖通

- - -

全球速卖通平台卖家如实申报义务的规则重申

发布日期：-

  

亲爱的速卖通卖家：

根据[全球速卖通"不法获利"规则](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523667)中第（8）项：为销售目的，卖家以任何明示或暗示的方式涉嫌进行或协助买家进行各类违规避税行为，平台再次重申卖家如实申报义务的规则。按照相关法律法规，卖家应自主履行（或敦促消费者履行）纳税、清关义务，卖家不得以任何方式在进出口环节低报、瞒报、虚报交易信息，或帮助买家规避或者少缴税费，包括但不限于，在店铺页面、商品标题、商品SKU、商品描述或其他与买家沟通渠道中说明、提供各类规避税收的信息或服务。

违规信息举例**包含但不限于**：

1、avoid tax/VAT

2、declare lower value

3、No tax/VAT

4、Zero tax/VAT

5、Free of VAT

6、Don’t pay VAT

请卖家务必对店铺内商品进行自纠自查。若存在上述违规信息，请立即进行整改或删除商品。平台会持续对该类违规信息进行排查，对存在类似违规描述的商品进行删除并扣分；如情节严重，平台有权对卖家的账号、店铺实施处罚。

请您知悉。

附：

1、[关于卖家如实申报义务的规则更新](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/156187105?spm=a2g3p.rule_index.0.0.4b21rVqsrVqsZN)

2、[关于卖家如实申报义务的再次重申](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/156186716?spm=a2g3p.rule_index.0.0.4b219eG89eG88f)

全球速卖通关于卖家如实申报义务的再次重申

**发布日期：北京时间2019/12/23**

**最新版本修订日期：北京时间2020/1/20**

**注：****红字部分****为本次修改或增加部分**

亲爱的速卖通卖家：

按照相关法律法规，卖家应自主履行（或敦促消费者履行）纳税、清关义务，卖家不得以任何方式在进出口环节低报、瞒报、虚报交易信息，或帮助买家规避或者少缴税费。该违规行为包括但不限于，在店铺页面、商品描述或其他与买家沟通之渠道中说明、暗示可以进行各类违规避税操作。

违规信息举例包含但不限于：

**·** avoid tax

**·** declare lower value

**·** avoid value added tax

**·** tax evasion

**·** declared the item as a gift

为显示平台对涉嫌违法行为的禁止态度，平台将在全球速卖通平台规则"不法获利"规则中增加第（8）项举例：为销售目的，卖家以任何明示或暗示的方式涉嫌进行或协助买家进行各类违规避税行为。本修改自2020年1月20日起生效。

请卖家务必对店铺内产品信息进行自检自查。若存在上述违规信息，请立即做删除整改。卖家自主整改期为本公告起至2020年1月20日。自主整改期后，平台将再次加强对该类违规信息的排查，一旦发现将删除相关产品并扣2分；情节严重的，平台有权进行账号冻结或关闭。

全球速卖通

全球速卖通关于禁止销售孔明灯及种子/植物盆栽产品的公告

发布日期：北京时间2017/12/20

尊敬的速卖通卖家：  
速卖通一直致力于为消费者提供安全，品质的商品，为广大速卖通会员创造良好的交易环境，持续改善消费者购物体验，维护品质商家的权益。  
根据各国物流及国家的进口要求，孔明灯及种子/植物盆栽产品已被绝大部分国家法律规定不允许进口。为了更好的维护广大速卖通会员的利益，为避免卖家的损失和相关法律责任，自本日起请卖家停止销售孔明灯及种子/植物盆栽产品。  
1、自北京时间2017年12月20日起，平台将关闭中国卖家Home & Garden>Garden Supplies>plant seeds类目，仅境外本地卖家可销售**种子/植物盆栽产品。**  
2、自北京时间2017年12月27日起，平台将进行排查，若发现有**孔明灯、种子/植物盆栽产品**，平台将按照禁限售规则执行商品退回并扣分：

**·** 孔明灯，根据禁限售（二）危险化学品 第8点：烟花爆竹、点火器及配件； 执行每次0.5分并退回商品处理；  
**·** 种子/植物盆栽，根据禁限售违 (十二)人体器官、保护动植物及捕杀工具 第4点：重点和濒危保护植物、制品，执行每次1分并退还商品处理；  
**·** 若卖家通过类目错放等方式规避发布，平台将根据严重程度，按严重扰乱市场秩序规则对账号执行冻结甚至关闭的处理。

建议卖家关注各国物流及国家的进口要求，共同营造安全，品质的交易环境。  
感谢您对速卖通的关注和支持！  

  
全球速卖通

全球速卖通关于规范管理地图及其相关制品的公告

**发布日期：北京时间2017/9/29**

**最新版本修订日期：北京时间2022/10/9**

亲爱的卖家：  
地图直接体现国家领土完整与民族尊严，具有很强的严肃性与科学性。为落实地图制品的规范、科学、严谨管理，我国《地图管理条例》明确规定，向社会公开的地图，应当报送有审核权的测绘地理信息行政主管部门审核，依法执行地图审核制度，获取“地图审图号”。

平台自2022年10月10日起，将加强地图相关商品管控：

**1、地图商品必须发布在以下类目：**

办公、文化及教育用品>>地图和地图集

办公、文化及教育用品>>教学设备及用品>>教学用具>>地球仪

办公、文化及教育用品>>教学设备及用品>>教学用具>>磁性地球仪

**2、在商品资质模块填写商品的“地图审图号”。**

国务院测绘行政主管部门审图号为：GS（××××年）××××号〔如：GS（2004）001号〕

省级测绘行政主管部门审图号为：省（自治区、直辖市）简称S（××××年）××××号〔如：京S（2004）006号〕

**3、地图上禁止出现危害国家主权统一、领土完整的错绘漏绘，包括错误表示台湾省、错绘藏南地区和阿克赛钦地区国界线，漏绘钓鱼岛、赤尾屿、南海诸岛、南海十段线等。**

对于不合格商品，速卖通将依照平台规则对“宣传国家分裂及其他各国禁止传播发布的敏感信息”相关商品或信息进行删除、下架或严重违规处理。  
**特别注意**：请勿**随意填写伪造或错误的审图号或冒用他人所持有的审图号**，此类行为属于《地图管理条例》第五十二条规定的“伪造、冒用地图审核批准文件和审图号”的严重违法行为，将承担严厉的法律责任。请卖家务必做好自检自查工作，若存在此类行为，请尽快修正或撤回错填、伪造、冒用的审图号信息。

**若您的商品还未获得“地图审图号”，您可以访问zwfw.ch.mnr.gov.cn/approval 免费申请：**

注：如果为省、市等地方性地图，需到各省市对应的测绘局申请。

**常见问题FAQ：**

1、怎么判断商品是否需要地图审图号？

答：检查商品上是否含有地图LOGO、地图图形。如果有，通常均需要地图审图号。

2、去哪审批？

答：可网上申请办理，网址：zwfw.ch.mnr.gov.cn/approval，（网址下滑到底）“行政审批>>地图审核”。如果您的商品为省、市等中国地方性地图，请向区域当地有审核权的测绘局进行申请。

3、地图审图号审批时长？申请费用？

答：常规地图，自受理地图审核申请之日起20个工作日内作出审核决定；无收费。具体可咨询国家测绘地理信息局地图技术审查中心。

4、地图审批需提供的资料有哪些？

答：相关资料见：zwfw.ch.mnr.gov.cn/result/matterdetial?appId=4028fb8351193e4e0151194302a50001

5、怎么判断地图有没有错绘漏绘

答：详细说明见：https://www.zrzyst.cn/gjbtdtzs/730.jhtml

注：有下列情形之一的，可以不提供地图编制单位的测绘资质证书：

（1）进口不属于出版物的地图和附着地图图形的产品；

（2）直接引用古地图；

（3）使用示意性世界地图、中国地图和地方地图；

全球速卖通

全球速卖通关于禁止销售彩票的公告

发布日期：-

亲爱的速卖通商家：

根据国内外各国家及地区对于彩票类商品管控的相关法律法规及监管机构的相关规定，经综合考量，全球速卖通禁止商家销售彩票。

【管控范围】
------

彩票类商品，包括但不限于乐透、刮刮乐、大百万乐透、威力球乐透等各类实体或虚拟彩票。

【管控地区】
------

全球

【处置措施】
------

平台一旦发现商家有相关产品发布或销售行为，将对商品立即下架，对商家进行如下处罚：违规扣分2分/次。

平台提醒广大商家合规发品及合规交易，商家有责任遵守任何本国及销售目的国适用的产品合规法律，发布违规产品及信息的商家，平台将对相关产品及信息进行下架或删除，同时对存在违规情况的商家，依照相关平台规则进行处罚。对恶意绕过规则、在任何场景发布违规信息、重复违规、被监管部门通告、被重要媒体曝光以及存在其他严重违规情节的会员，依据平台相关规则，平台将采取包括但不限于删除产品信息、扣分、屏蔽店铺、限制使用网站产品功能、冻结账号直至关闭账号的处罚。我们将会持续关注各国的相关政策变化，并据此进行平台管控政策的相应调整。

【相关法规】
------

[美国彩票法案 18 U.S.C.](https://www.govinfo.gov/content/pkg/USCODE-2009-title18/html/USCODE-2009-title18-partI-chap61.htm)

[英国赌博法案](https://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2005/19/contents)

[荷兰赌博与彩票法规](https://wetten.overheid.nl/BWBR0002469/2018-07-28)

《彩票管理条例》

《彩票管理条例实施细则》

Dear Sellers:

Pursuant to the relevant requirements of laws and regulations all around the world for the control of lottery tickets, Aliexpress.com will ban the sale of Lottery tickets.

\[Prohibited Product Scope\]
----------------------------

Lottery tickets, including but not limited to Lotto, Instant win tickets or scratch-cards, Powerball, Mega Millions, etc. whether in physical or virtual form.

\[Countries of Control\]
------------------------

Global

\[Violations and penalties\]
----------------------------

Once the platform discovers that the merchant has any relevant product release or sales behavior, related products or information will immediately be deleted and AliExpress will deduct 2 points for each violation.

AliExpress members shall list and sell products in accordance with applicable rules and abide by applicable laws and regulations of any country of origin and any country of destination. Where any member is found to be listing products or releasing information in violation of the rules, AliExpress will delist or delete the related products or information and punish the violator in accordance with relevant rules. For a member that knowingly circumvents the rules, provides information about prohibited products in any interaction scenarios, violates the rules repeatedly, is criticized in any form of media circulated by a regulator, receives negative publicity published by media, or commits any other serious violation, AliExpress will impose penalties, including but not limited to deleting product information, deducting points, blocking stores, restricting access to the website's product features, and freezing or even closing the account, in accordance with the platform's relevant rules.

\[Reference\]
-------------

[USA -CHAPTER 61—LOTTERIES 18 U.S.C.](https://www.govinfo.gov/content/pkg/USCODE-2009-title18/html/USCODE-2009-title18-partI-chap61.htm)

[UK Gambling Act 2005](http://www.legislation.gov.uk/ukpga/2005/19/contents)

[Netherland Law and Regulations on Lottery and Gambling](https://wetten.overheid.nl/BWBR0002469/2018-07-28)

《彩票管理条例》

《彩票管理条例实施细则》

Note: The above information does not constitute any legal advice and shall not be deemed or represent the legal opinion or conclusion of the regulatory body. Further, we do not undertake or warrant that the information represents the latest laws and regulations. For specific information, please consult the competent authority, law firms, or third-party certification/testing/consulting companies in the target country or region.

AliExpress.com will continue to monitor the changes in laws and related policies of countries worldwide, and adjust our platform rules accordingly. Please contact our online customer service for any further queries.

Thank you for your support and attention.

Aliexpress

全球速卖通关于出口管制两用物项合规销售的公告（无人驾驶航空飞行器及其相关物项）

发布日期：北京时间2023/08/18

最新版本修订日期：北京时间2024/08/29

注：红字部分为本次修改或新增部分

尊敬的速卖通商家，

根据商务部海关总署中央军委装备发展部公告2024年第31号关于优化调整无人机出口管制措施的公告，根据《中华人民共和国出口管制法》《中华人民共和国对外贸易法》《中华人民共和国海关法》有关规定，调整特定无人驾驶航空飞行器及其相关物项的出口管制措施，新规将于2024年9月1日起正式实施。据此，速卖通禁止平台上的任何商品被用于大规模杀伤性武器扩散、恐怖主义活动或者军事目的，并禁止销售受出口管制的无人驾驶航空飞行器相关物项。

【商品管控范围】
--------

根据调整后的出口管制措施，具体包括：

（一）最大持续功率超过16千瓦（kW）的专门用于特定无人驾驶航空飞行器或无人驾驶飞艇的航空发动机（参考海关商品编号：8501200010、8501320010、8501330010、8501340010、8501400010、8501520010、8501530010、8407101010、8407102010、8408909230、8408909320、8411111010、8411119010、8411121010、8411129020、8411210010、8411221010、8411222010、8411223010、8411810002）。

（二）满足一定技术指标的专门用于特定无人驾驶航空飞行器或无人驾驶飞艇的载荷，包括红外成像设备、合成孔径雷达、用于目标指示的激光器和惯性测量设备。

1、具有以下所有特性的红外成像设备（参考海关商品编号：8525891110、8525892110、8525893110）：

（1）波长范围在780纳米（nm）至30000纳米（nm）之间；

（2）瞬时视场角（IFOV）小于2.5毫弧度（mrad）。

2、作用距离大于5千米（km），且具有以下任一特性的合成孔径雷达（SAR）（参考海关商品编号：8526109011）：

（1）条带模式分辨率优于0.3米（m）；

（2）聚束模式分辨率优于0.1米（m）。

3、可在高于55摄氏度（℃）环境中稳定工作，且具有以下所有特性的用于目标指示的激光器（参考海关商品编号：9013200093）：

（1）免温控型；

（2）能量大于80毫焦（mJ）；

（3）稳定度优于15%；

（4）光束发散角小于0.3毫弧度（mrad）。

4、具有以下所有特性的惯性测量设备（参考海关商品编号：9014209014）：

（1）航向精度小于2度（°）；

（2）姿态精度小于0.5度（°）；

（3）分辨率小于0.1度（°）。

（三）专门用于特定无人驾驶航空飞行器或无人驾驶飞艇，且具有下述任一特性的无线电通信设备（参考海关商品编号：8517629910、8517691002、8526920010）：

1、无线电视距传输距离大于50千米（km）；

2、一站控多机能力大于10架。

（四）民用反无人机系统：

1、干扰范围大于5千米（km）的反无人机电子干扰设备（参考海关商品编号：8543709960）；

2、专门用于反无人机系统的输出功率大于1.5千瓦（kW）的高功率激光器（参考海关商品编号：9013200093）。

技术说明：“特定无人驾驶航空飞行器或无人驾驶飞艇”是指满足商务部、海关总署公告2015年第31号（《关于加强部分两用物项出口管制的公告》）中1.1款所列条件的无人驾驶航空飞行器或无人驾驶飞艇。

**管控商品示例（包括但不限于以下产品）：**

惯性测量设备，通常指的是惯性导航系统（INS, Inertial Navigation System）或惯性测量单元（IMU, Inertial Measurement Unit）,它们用于测量和控制飞行器的姿态和运动，简要描述如下：

**1、惯性测量单元（IMU）**：通常包括加速度计、陀螺仪和有时包括磁力计，用于测量无人机的加速度、角速度和方向。

**2、惯性导航系统（INS）**：INS结合了IMU的数据并通过算法计算出无人机的位置、速度和姿态。INS通常还会集成GPS等其他传感器来提高精度。

【管控地区】
------

全球

【管控措施】
------

禁售规则自有关政府机关的公告实施之日起开始实行。违反中国出口管制相关法律法规的，有可能被处以罚款、责令停业及吊销经营资格，情节严重的，还可能被追究刑事责任。请商家对其在售商品进行自检自查，确认是否属于受管制物项，并主动下架属于受管制物项的商品。对于公告实施前的在途订单，请商家及时按照相关规定办理出口许可手续。如果商家未及时获得出口许可证，请立刻终止交易并联系买家退款，避免违反相关法规及速卖通规则。

【参考依据】
------

1、[商务部 海关总署 中央军委装备发展部公告2024年第31号 关于优化调整无人机出口管制措施的公告](https://www.mofcom.gov.cn/zwgk/zcfb/art/2024/art_db6e21907d69404fb473ddb0b248d3d7.html)

2、[《两用物项和技术进出口许可证管理目录》](http://exportcontrol.mofcom.gov.cn/article/zcfg/gnzcfg/zcfggzqd/202312/941.html)

注意：以上信息仅供参考，不保证完整性、准确性、及时性，速卖通保留对此内容修改、补充的权利。

如您有任何疑问可咨询小何在线，感谢您对全球速卖通的关注和支持！

全球速卖通关于新增出口管制两用物项合规销售的公告（镓及锗相关物项）

发布日期：北京时间2023/8/18

最新版本修订日期：北京时间2023/8/22

根据商务部、海关总署近期发布的公告，根据《中华人民共和国出口管制法》《中华人民共和国对外贸易法》《中华人民共和国海关法》有关规定，对镓、锗相关物项实施出口管制。 据此，禁止通过速卖通销售受出口管制的镓及锗相关物项，具体包括满足以下特性的物项 ：

（一）镓相关物项
--------

1、金属镓（单质）（参考海关商品编号：8112929010、8112929090、8112999000）；

2、氮化镓（包括但不限于晶片、粉末、碎料等形态）（参考海关商品编号：2850001901、3818009001、3825690001）；

3、氧化镓（包括但不限于多晶、单晶、晶片、外延片、粉末、碎料等形态）（参考海关商品编号：2825909001、3818009002、3825690002）；

4、磷化镓（包括但不限于多晶、单晶、晶片、外延片等形态）（参考海关商品编号：2853904030、3818009003、3825690003）；

5、砷化镓（包括但不限于多晶、单晶、晶片、外延片、粉末、碎料等形态）（参考海关商品编号：2853909026、3818009004、3825690004）；

6、铟镓砷（参考海关商品编号：2853909028、3818009005、3825690005）；

7、硒化镓（包括但不限于多晶、单晶、晶片、外延片、粉末、碎料等形态）（参考海关商品编号：2842909024、3818009006、3825690006）；

8、锑化镓（包括但不限于多晶、单晶、晶片、外延片、粉末、碎料等形态）（参考海关商品编号：2853909029、3818009007、3825690007）。

（二）锗相关物项
--------

1、金属锗（单质，包括但不限于晶体、粉末、碎料等形态）（参考海关商品编号：8112921010、8112921090、8112991000）；

2、区熔锗锭（参考海关商品编号：8112921090）；

3、磷锗锌（包括但不限于晶体、粉末、碎料等形态）（参考海关商品编号：2853904040、3818009008、3825690008）；

4、锗外延生长衬底（参考海关商品编号：8112921090）；

5、二氧化锗（参考海关商品编号：2825600002、3818009009、3825690009）；

6、四氯化锗（参考海关商品编号：2827399001、3818009010、3825690010）。

禁售规则自有关政府机关的公告实施之日起开始实行。违反中国出口管制相关法律法规的，有可能被处以罚款、责令停业及吊销经营资格，情节严重的，还可能被追究刑事责任。请商家对其在售商品进行自检自查，确认是否属于受管制物项，并主动下架属于受管制物项的商品。对于公告实施前的在途订单，请商家及时按照相关规定办理出口许可手续。如果商家未及时获得出口许可证，请立刻终止交易并联系买家退款，避免违反相关法规及速卖通规则。

请参见政府官方公告：[商务部 海关总署公告2023年第23号 关于对镓、锗相关物项实施出口管制的公告](http://www.mofcom.gov.cn/article/zwgk/gkzcfb/202307/20230703419666.shtml)。

全球速卖通关于小颗粒强力磁铁产品的整改通知

发布日期：北京时间2020/6/16

各位卖家：

小颗粒强力磁铁已在全世界范围内多个地区进行严格管控。该产品可能对接触到的儿童产生危害性，严重时可能危及生命。各国相关机构已发布了关于这类产品的消费者警示。

基于此，速卖通已严格管控该类小颗粒强力磁铁，对于最长边小于31.7mm的强力磁铁玩具全面禁售并依据《全球速卖通禁限售商品目录》(十七)条，经权威质检部门或生产商认定、公布或召回的商品或违反其他商品相关规则的商品，将违规商品进行退回并扣除2分/次的处理。

目前平台发现部分卖家仍在售卖该类违规商品导致被扣分处罚，请卖家朋友务必进行店铺的自检自查，及时清理违规商品避免更严重的处罚。

参照图片：

  

各地区的商品召回/禁售规则:

澳大利亚ACCC官网：https://www.productsafety.gov.au/bans/small-high-powered-magnets

新西兰政府官网: http://www.beehive.govt.nz/release/ban-sale-high-powered-magnet-sets

加拿大卫生部官网: http://healthycanadians.gc.ca/recall-alert-rappel-avis/hc-sc/2013/31619a-eng.php

欧盟(28个国家)法律官网: http://eur-lex.europa.eu/legal-content/EN/TXT/?qid=1434350124231&uri=CELEX:32008D0329

巴西(南方共同市场)法律官网: http://www.inmetro.gov.br/qualidade/iaac/pdf/seguranca-brinquedo.pdf

国内相关新闻：

东方网：http://news.eastday.com/eastday/13news/auto/news/china/u7ai3947291\_K4.html?spm=5261.8513437.0.0.6e63267eM8h7un

英文版规则(English version):[Announcement of Prohibit Selling for Magnetic Ball/CubesAnnouncement of Prohibit Selling for Magnetic Ball/Cubes](https://sell.aliexpress.com/zh/__pc/0H2tQvcpem.htm)

AliExpress Announcement on Strengthening Control of Laser Products

Release date: July 30, 2024

Revision date: /

**Dear Sellers:**

AliExpress is always committed to maintaining an orderly marketplace in compliance with all local laws, regulations and providing consumers with safe and high-quality goods. In order to protect the rights and interests of platform users, AliExpress (hereinafter referred to as "AliExpress" or "Platform") will strengthen control over the following products:

\[Prohibited Products\]
-----------------------

Laser products have been strictly controlled in many countries and regions around the world. Laser products may be hazardous to people who contact with such products and may be life-threatening in severe cases. Authorities in various countries have issued warnings to consumers about such products, and some high-power laser products are even recognized as weapons in some countries.

Prohibited products include but are not limited to the following types:

\[Control measures\]
--------------------

AliExpress will strictly control laser products (including laser pens, laser toys, laser sights, etc.). Except for the penalty under the existing prohibited and restricted sales rules (prohibition on the sale of laser pen products with a transmitting power greater than 5 mw: general violation, 1 point/time; serious violation, 6 points/time) , AliExpress requests the Sellers that:

1、All products involving lasers should contain the maximum output power of the product in the product title and/or attributes (such as the maximum output power (Max. Output Power) under the category Computers and Offices > Office Electronics > Administrative and Financial Equipment > Laser Pens)., otherwise it may be punished by being removed from the shelves for the first time and editable, and being deleted twice after February 24 2024;

2、For laser products with a transmission power greater than 1 mw and less than or equal to 5 mw, such products are prohibited in the EU, the United Kingdom, Australia, New Zealand, Brazil, the Kingdom of Saudi Arabia, the United Arab Emirates and other countries.

Sellers shall list and sell products in accordance with applicable rules and abide by applicable laws and regulations of any country of origin and any country of destination. Where any Seller is found to be listing products or releasing information in violation of the rules, AliExpress will delist or delete the related products or information and punish the violator in accordance with relevant rules. For a Seller that knowingly circumvents the rules, provides information about prohibited products in any interaction scenarios (e.g., chats, live-streaming), violates the rules repeatedly, is criticized in any form of media circulated by a regulator, receives negative publicity published by media, or commits any other serious violation, AliExpress will impose penalties, including but not limited to deleting product information, deducting points, blocking stores, restricting access to the website's product features, and freezing or even closing the account, in accordance with the platform's relevant rules.

\[References\]
--------------

1、[EU: European union General Product Safety Directive (GPSD)](https://commission.europa.eu/business-economy-euro/product-safety-and-requirements/product-safety/general-product-safety-regulation_en)

2、[EU: EN 60825-1 (Safety of laser products)](https://standards.iteh.ai/catalog/standards/clc/69b32a43-0ed4-44bd-8b07-03e08e64e963/en-60825-1-2014)

3、[UK: BS EN 60825-1](https://knowledge.bsigroup.com/products/safety-of-laser-products-equipment-classification-and-requirements-1?version=standard)

4、[Canada: CSA E60825-1:15 (R2020)](https://store.accuristech.com/standards/csa-e60825-1-15-r2020?product_id=1907911)

5、[Australia: AS/NZS IEC 60825.1:2014](https://www.standards.org.au/standards-catalogue/standard-details?designation=as-nzs-iec-60825-1-2014)

6、[New Zealand: Health (High-power Laser Pointers) Regulations 2013](https://www.legislation.govt.nz/regulation/public/2013/0478/latest/DLM5714621.html)

7、[Brazil: International Electrotechnical Commission (IEC) 60825-1:2014](https://webstore.iec.ch/publication/3587)

8、[USA: IEC 60825-1](https://webstore.iec.ch/publication/3587)

Note: The above information does not constitute any legal advice and shall not be deemed or represent the legal opinion or conclusion of the regulatory body. Further, we do not undertake or warrant that the information represents the latest laws and regulations. For specific information, please consult the competent authority, law firms, or third-party certification/testing/consulting companies in the target country or region.

AliExpress.com will continue to monitor the changes in laws and related policies of countries worldwide, and adjust our platform rules accordingly. Please contact our online customer service for any further queries.

Thank you for your support and attention.

AliExpress

全球速卖通指尖陀螺商品整改通知

发布日期：北京时间2017/06/28

最新版本修订日期：北京时间2025/09/25

注：红字部分为本次修改或新增部分

尊敬的速卖通商家：  
今年在全球市场指尖陀螺商品畅销，很多消费者购买指尖陀螺作为儿童玩具，指尖陀螺商品的不安全外观设计可能对接触到的儿童产生危害，严重时可能危及生命。目前，境外已发生多起因指尖陀螺引发的伤害事件。为避免潜在的人身伤害风险，请商家注意所销售商品的外观设计的安全性。  
请商家对已上架商品及时调整整改，速卖通平台将依据[《全球速卖通禁限售违禁信息列表》](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647)第十七条高风险及安全隐患类商品管控规则，对存在安全隐患的指尖陀螺商品进行退回并扣除2分/次的处理。  
同时，对于指尖陀螺商品，速卖通平台会依据法律法规的调整、经营环境的变化等因素及时地提升管控标准，例如校验欧盟的CE认证等。敬请关注相关管控变化。

全球速卖通禁限售规则(含违禁信息列表)

发布日期：/

最新版本修订日期：北京时间2025/10/21

注：红字部分为本次修改或增加部分

  

**·** [一、概述](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647#pRLeA)

**·** [二、违禁信息列表](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647#q5y5F)

**·** [三、故意或恶意的违规行为](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647#ooR2W)

**·** [四、违规分类及处罚措施](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647#H04wp)

**·** [五、举报处理](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647#gFm2v)

一、概述：
=====

速卖通（以下简称为“速卖通”或“平台”）全球禁止发布任何含有或指向性描述禁限售信息。任何违反本规则的行为，平台有权依据全球速卖通禁限售规则进行处罚。

用户不得通过任何方式规避本规定、平台发布的其他禁售商品管理规定及公告规定的内容，否则可能将被加重处罚。

二、违禁信息列表
========

平台用户不得在全球速卖通平台发布任何违反任何国家、地区及司法管辖区的法律规定或监管要求的商品。

[《全球速卖通禁限售信息列表》](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647)是平台禁止发布或限制发布的部分信息列表，仅供用户参考。但不能保证完整性、及时性和准确性。平台有权利根据法律规定、监管要求及平台自身规定对下列信息做增删和修改。同时，平台用户有义务确保自己发布的商品没有违反任何司法管辖区的要求。

除非特殊说明，全球速卖通的禁限售规则同时适用于信息发布及《交易服务协议》中规定的线上交易（“线上交易”）行为。

全球速卖通的禁限售规则同时适用于速卖通英文主站及其他多语言站点。

如部分国家法律规定禁限售商品及因商品属性不适合跨境销售而不应售卖的商品，请以部分国家法律规定及平台最新公告为准。

若中文版与英文版公告、公告内容与速卖通平台其他规则存在差异，或有其他不尽详细事宜，速卖通拥有最终解释权。

| 6、追讨服务、代加粉丝或听众服务，签证服务； | 一般违规，0.5分/次 |
| [（十一）收藏  详解类](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523650) |     |
| 1、货币、金融票证，明示或暗示用于伪造、变造货币、金融票证的主要材料、工具及方法； | 严重违规，最高扣除48分 |
| 2、虚拟货币（如比特币）； | 一般违规，6分/次 |
| 3、金、银和其他贵重金属； | 一般违规，2分/次 |
| 4、国家保护的文物、化石及其他收藏品； | 一般违规，2分/次 |
| [（十二）人体器官、捕杀工具、活体动植物及一切形态的保护动植物  详解](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523650) |     |
| 1、用于任何目的的人体骨架、器官及体液，塑化人体标本等商品，包括但不限于人体器官/遗体/遗骸/精子/卵子/血液，塑化人体标本等以及人体器官及遗体制作的标本等； | 严重违规，最高扣除48分 |
| 2、重点和濒危保护动物活体、身体部分；公益保护动物（鲨鱼、熊、猫、狗等）；动物捕杀设备（塑化、剥皮服务；电捕机；捕兽夹；猫狗强制脱毛机等）；及以上动物制品；（鲨鱼软骨素在韩国，若符合合规要求，可在境内销售，合规要求详见如下：[《全球速卖通关于保健食品行业商品加强管控的公告》](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/137686209)） | 一般违规，2分/次 |
| 3、重点和濒危保护植物、地域性保护植物、保护植物标本及以上植物制品； | 一般违规，1分/次 |
| 4、植物种子（波兰、德国、法国、意大利、西班牙本地卖家，若符合合规要求，可在境内销售，合规要求详见如下：[《AliExpress Announcement on the Sales Control over Seeds In Poland, France, Germany, Italy, Spain》](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/240465709)）； | 一般违规，1分/次 |
| 5、活体动植物及其制品； | 一般违规，0分/次 |
| [（十三）危害国家安全及侮辱性信息  详解](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523650) |     |
| 1、宣扬恐怖组织和极端组织信息； | 严重违规，最高扣除48分 |
| 2、宣传国家分裂及其他各国禁止传播发布的敏感信息； | 严重违规，最高扣除48分 |
| 3、涉及种族、性别、宗教、地域等歧视性或侮辱性信息； | 一般违规，2分/次 |
| 4、其他含有政治色彩的信息； | 一般违规，0分/次 |
| [（十四）烟草  详解](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523650) |     |
| 1、成品烟及烟草制品 ； | 一般违规，6分/次 |
| 2、电子烟液； | 一般违规，6分/次 |
| 3、电子烟器具、部件及配件； | 需要类目准入，若错放类目，2分/次 |
| 4、制烟材料及烟草专用机械； | 一般违规，0.5分/次 |
| 5、烟草图片禁售（使用含有烟液的图片或图片中有烟液展示）； | 一般违规，1分/次 |
| [（十五）赌博  详解](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523650) |     |
| 1、在线赌博信息； | 一般违规，2分/次 |
| 2、赌博工具； | 一般违规，2分/次 |
| [（十六）制裁及其他管制商品  详解](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523650) |     |
| 1、禁运物； | 一般违规，1分/次<br><br>平台有权按照禁限售违禁信息列表中已约定类别处理，包括不限于扣分、商品屏蔽、删除等处置。 |
| 2、其他制裁商品； | 一般违规，1分/次 |
| [（十七）违反目的国/本国产品质量技术法规/法令/标准的、劣质的、存在风险的商品  详解](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523650) |     |
| 1、经权威质检部门或生产商认定、公布或召回的商品；各国明令淘汰或停止销售的商品；过期、失效、变质的商品、无生产日期、无保质期、无生产厂家的商品； | 一般违规，2分/次 |
| 严重违规，6分/次 |
| 2、高风险及安全隐患类商品； | 一般违规，2分/次 |
| 严重违规，6分/次 |
| [（十八）部分国家法律规定禁限售商品及因商品属性不适合跨境销售而不应售卖的商品  详解](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523650) |     |
| 1、部分国家法律规定不允许或限制售卖的商品； | 根据不允许售卖商品的类别，平台有权按照禁限售违禁信息列表中已约定类别处理，包括扣分、商品屏蔽、删除等处置。 |
| 2、因商品属性不适合跨境销售而不应售卖的商品（如茶叶、普通食品（坚果、速食品、腌制食品）、活体植物、活体动物、虚拟商品（特定市场定向招商除外）等）； | 根据发布的此类商品禁售清单，卖家不应通过类目错放等方式发布任何平台不许售卖的产品，一经发现，平台有权采取退回、下架、冻结或关闭账号的处置。 |
| 3、不允许发布的盲盒/福袋商品（平台针对特定目的国另有规定除外）； | 一般违规，2分/次<br><br>严重违规，最高扣除48分 |
| 4、因具有高人身安全风险不允许发布和销售的农药类产品（如应用于大规模或专业农田、花园、果园等作物的除草剂、杀虫剂、杀虫喷雾等）； | 一般违规，2分/次<br><br>严重违规，最高扣除48分 |
| （十九）违背社会道德、公序良俗和人道主义精神的争议性或敏感性产品 |     |
| 严禁上架或销售可能违背道德或人性底线、违反地方社会基本规范或危害任何社会秩序的争议性或敏感性产品，包括但不限于堕胎工具、基因相关产品、与动物或器官克隆相关的产品、与动物或人体实验相关的产品或者可能危害环境或社会的产品。 | 一般违规，2分/次<br><br>严重违规，最高扣除48分 |
| （二十）其他禁售商品 |     |
| 详见[《全球速卖通产品发布政策》](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523648)。 | 根据不允许售卖商品的类别，平台有权按照禁限售违禁信息列表中已约定类别处理，包括扣分、商品屏蔽、删除等处置。 |

三、**故意或恶意的违规行为**
================

以下故意或恶意规避平台规则的行为亦属于违规：

1、采用对商品信息、评论、问大家等隐藏、遮挡、模糊处理、隐晦等隐匿的手段；

2、采用暗示性描述或故意通过模糊描述、错放类目等方式规避平台监控规则；

3、平台通过消费者评价中可判断、推断商家销售商品为平台禁售商品等类似违规情况；

4、同时发布大量违禁商品，重复上传违规信息，恶意测试规则或不配合平台对商品进行各类抽检测试等行为。

四、**违规分类及处罚措施**
===============

1、平台有权根据发布商品信息本身、消费者对商品评论及问大家等交互场景及线索判断存在违规行为及情况而对商家进行加重处罚处理，同时平台将对商家在线商品及下架商品进行抽样检查，判定商家是否构成禁限售违规行为。若核查到订单中涉及禁限售商品，速卖通有权关闭订单，如买家已付款，无论状况均全额退款给买家，卖家承担全部责任。

2、**商品信息违规加重处罚**：对于重复、故意或恶意违规行为，平台将加重处罚，包括处罚分数翻倍、直接关闭账户等措施。

3、**其他信息违规加重处罚**：即使商品信息表述无异常，但平台通过评论区、问大家等交互场景发现或认定商家可能以任何形式规避平台规则或存在其他违规行为，则平台有权对商家加重处罚，包括处罚分数翻倍、直接关闭账户等措施。

4、被处罚商家有权对平台处罚进行申诉。对于商家申诉，平台将积极甄别并核实，对于有效申诉将撤销处罚。

5、禁限售违规和知识产权一般侵权，将累计积分，积分累计到一定分值，将执行账号处罚。更多违规处罚措施规则请参考[《全球速卖通卖家基础规则（违规及处罚规则）》](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523039)。

|     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **计分类型** | **扣分节点** | **处罚措施** |
| 知识产权禁限售违规 | 2分  | 警告  |
| 6分  | 限制商品操作3天 |
| 12分 | 冻结账号7天 |
| 24分 | 冻结账号14天 |
| 36分 | 冻结账号30天 |
| 48分 | 关闭  |

**备注：**

1、全部在线商品及下架商品均在“平台抽样检查”范围之内，平台抽样检查范围包括但不限于仓内抽检、寄样抽检、上门实地抽检、第三方质检机构检测等，如抽检不通过或抽检判定存在违规行为，平台将按照相关规则执行处罚；

（1）平台上门实地抽检将按照以下标准执行：

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| **上门实地抽检不通过场景** | **执行标准** |     |
| 检查时发现实物标签瑕疵、错误、违规等 | 1、给予7天整改期，整改结果需在7天内上传至资质系统；<br><br>2、如逾期未整改或整改不通过，对应商品将执行对应国家向屏蔽管控。 |     |
| 检查时发现假证冒证情形 | 平台将对全店商品进行资质复查，同时删除问题商品并扣6分/次。 |     |
| 不配合检查<br><br>（包括但不限于无法联系、拒绝上门实地检查、临时爽约等） | 1、首次不配合检查将记录在名单中；<br><br>2、需在平台首次通知起2个月内配合完成检查，如逾期无法配合，对应国家强管控类目商品执行屏蔽。 |     |
| 其他干扰检查的情形或严重违背平台要求场景 | 依据平台相应规则进行管控。 |     |

（2）经第三方质检机构检测，如存在商品抽检结果存在违规行为，速卖通将采取包括但不限于以下违规管理措施进行处理：

1）删除商品链接；

2）屏蔽或下架可编辑商品链接；

3）店铺扣分1/次。

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| **第三方质检机构检测不通过场景** | **违规处罚** |     |
| 商品本身或最小销售包装上合规信息缺失 | 速卖通将采取包括但不限于以下违规管理措施进行处理：<br><br>1、相关商品执行删除或屏蔽或下架可编辑处罚；<br><br>2、对店铺将执行扣分。 |     |
| 商品属于不符合适用的商品合规安全标准且对人身或其他物品产生潜在伤害（如，造成儿童窒息，电池易短路，赫兹超标等） | 速卖通将采取包括但不限于以下违规管理措施进行处理：<br><br>1、相关商品执行删除或屏蔽处罚；<br><br>2、对店铺将执行扣分。 |     |

2、以上“违禁信息列表”中商品列举并没有尽录全部不适宜在全球速卖通平台交易的商品，全球速卖通亦将不时的予以调整。

3、针对恶意规避等情节特别严重行为（包括但不限于采用对商品信息隐藏、遮挡、模糊处理等隐匿的手段规避平台管理，经平台合理判断账号使用人本人或其控制的其他账号已因严重违规事件被处罚，账号使用人本人或其控制的其他账号被国内外监管部门立案调查、或虽未立案但平台有理由认为有重大嫌疑等严重影响平台管理秩序或造成一定负面影响的情况），平台保留直接扣除48分，关闭账号的权利。

全球速卖通禁止销售便携式壁炉的商家通知

发布日期：北京时间2023/7/5

**尊敬的速卖通商家：**

基于多个国家和地区（如欧盟、澳大利亚、加拿大等）当地法律规定，因便携式壁炉具有很高的火灾风险，为保障消费者的安全，全球速卖通禁止商家向全球销售便携式壁炉。

【商品管控范围】
--------

便携式壁炉：一种可以携带和移动的小型壁炉，使用易燃液体燃料或煤炭等燃料产生热量的一种发热工具。

便携式壁炉包括但不限于如下类型：

【管控措施】
------

**全球速卖通禁止发布、销售便携式壁炉**。平台发现商家店铺发布、销售便携式壁炉，将按照全球速卖通禁限售规则，对发布的违规商品，执行2分删除。  

平台提醒广大商家合规发品及合规交易，商家有责任遵守任何本国及销售目的国适用的产品合规法律，发布违规产品及信息的商家，平台将依照相关平台规则进行处罚。对恶意绕过规则、在任何场景（如沟通、直播等交互场景）发布违规信息、重复违规、被监管部门通告、被重要媒体曝光以及存在其他严重违规情节的会员，依据平台相关规则，平台将采取包括但不限于对相关产品及信息执行对应国家屏蔽、删除产品信息、扣分、屏蔽店铺、限制使用网站产品功能、冻结账号直至关闭账号的处罚。

【参考依据】
------

Australia: Consumer Goods (Decorative Alcohol Fuelled Devices) Safety Standard 2017

Canada: Consumer Chemicals and Containers Regulations 2001 and  
ASTM F3429 / F3429M-20 or ASTM F3363-19

European Union: National legislation transposing the“Commission Decision 2015/547 on the safety requirements for alcohol-powered flueless fireplaces” and EN16647:2015

注意：以上信息仅供参考，不保证完整性、准确性、及时性，AliExpress保留对此内容修改、补充的权利。

感谢您对全球速卖通的关注和支持！

  

**全球速卖通**

  

**AliExpress Ban on the Sales of Tabletop Ethanol Burners**

**Dear sellers**

Tabletop ethanol burners pose a very high risk of severe injury to consumers and property damage from uncontrolled fires due to their size and design. According to the requirements of several districts and countries’ laws and regulations (e.g. the European Union，Australia, Canada, etc.), and in order to protect the safety of consumers and reduce the fire risk associated with tabletop ethanol burners(also known as ‘tabletop fire pits’ or ‘tabletop fireplaces’), AliExpress prohibits the sales of tabletop ethanol burners.

\[Prohibited Products\]
-----------------------

Tabletop ethanol burners: a small fireplace that can be carried and moved, a heating tool that uses fuel such as flammable liquid fuel or coal to generate heat.

Prohibited Tabletop Ethanol Burners include but are not limited to the following types:

\[Control measures\]
--------------------

If sellers are found to list or trade the preceding prohibited Tabletop ethanol burners, AliExpress shall delete the products with 2 points punishment.

AliExpress members shall list and sell products in accordance with applicable rules and abide by applicable laws and regulations of any country of origin and any country of destination. Where any member is found to be listing products or releasing information in violation of the rules, AliExpress will delist or delete the related products or information and punish the violator in accordance with relevant rules. For a member that knowingly circumvents the rules, provides information about prohibited products in any interaction scenarios (e.g., chats, live-streaming), violates the rules repeatedly, is criticized in any form of media circulated by a regulator, receives negative publicity published by media, or commits any other serious violation, AliExpress will impose penalties, including but not limited to deleting product information, deducting points, blocking stores, restricting access to the website's product features, and freezing or even closing the account, in accordance with the platform's relevant rules.

\[References\]
--------------

Australia: Consumer Goods (Decorative Alcohol Fuelled Devices) Safety Standard 2017

Canada: Consumer Chemicals and Containers Regulations 2001 and ASTM F3429 / F3429M-20 or ASTM F3363-19

European Union: National legislation transposing the“Commission Decision 2015/547 on the safety requirements for alcohol-powered flueless fireplaces” and EN16647:2015  

Note: The above information does not constitute any legal advice and shall not be deemed or represent the legal opinion or conclusion of the regulatory body. Further, we do not undertake or warrant that the information represents the latest laws and regulations. For specific information, please consult the competent authority, law firms, or third-party certification/testing/consulting companies in the target country or region.

AliExpress.com will continue to monitor the changes in laws and related policies of countries worldwide, and adjust our platform rules accordingly.  
Thank you for your support and attention.

**AliExpress**

全球速卖通关于禁止向比利时销售食物垃圾处理器的合规公告

发布日期：北京时间2023/5/30

**尊敬的速卖通商家：**

根据比利时皇家法令要求，为保护环境及公众健康，禁止在比利时市场销售可将废弃物排入污水处理系统的食物垃圾处理设备。全球速卖通始终致力于保证平台商品符合国内外相关法律法规规定，保障平台用户权益，考虑当地法律要求，平台对比利时市场禁售食物垃圾处理器。

【商品管控范围】
--------

食物垃圾处理器（kitchen food waste grinders/food waste disposers/ kitchen residue garbage processors）：指无论是否需要同其他设备结合使用，目的在于研磨固体残留物最终排放到水生环境或水收集和废水处理系统中的相关设备。

【管控措施】
------

**全球速卖通禁止商家向比利时销售食物垃圾处理器，**若发现上述违规商品，平台将按照全球速卖通平台禁限售规则执行对应国家屏蔽。

平台提醒广大商家合规发品及合规交易，商家有责任遵守任何本国及销售目的国适用的产品合规法律，发布违规产品及信息的商家，平台将依照相关平台规则进行处罚。对恶意绕过规则、在任何场景（如沟通、直播等交互场景）发布违规信息、重复违规、被监管部门通告、被重要媒体曝光以及存在其他严重违规情节的会员，依据平台相关规则，平台将采取包括但不限于对相关产品及信息执行对应国家屏蔽、删除产品信息、扣分、屏蔽店铺、限制使用网站产品功能、冻结账号直至关闭账号的处罚。

【参考依据】
------

Art 2 §1 of the Belgian Royal Decree of August 10, 2015

AliExpress Ban on kitchen food waste grinders sold to Belgium
=============================================================

**Dear sellers**

AliExpress is always committed to maintaining an orderly marketplace in compliance with all local laws, regulations and providing consumers with safe and high-quality goods. According to Art 2 §1 of the Belgian Royal Decree of August 10, 2015，**AliExpress prohibits the sale of such products to Belgium market.**

\[Prohibited Products\]
-----------------------

Grinders whose grinding is intended to be disposed of through wastewater disposal systems, including any equipment or component, whether integrated into another equipment or not, whose purpose is to grind solid residues for ultimate discharge into aquatic environments or into a water collection and treatment network.

Prohibited products include but are not limited to the following types:

Kitchen food waste grinders/ food waste disposers /kitchen residue garbage processors

\[Control measures\]
--------------------

**AliExpress prohibits the sale of kitchen food waste grinders to Belgium market.**

AliExpress members shall list and sell products in accordance with applicable rules and abide by applicable laws and regulations of any country of origin and any country of destination. Where any member is found to be listing products or releasing information in violation of the rules, AliExpress will delist or delete the related products or information and punish the violator in accordance with relevant rules. For a member that knowingly circumvents the rules, provides information about prohibited products in any interaction scenarios (e.g., chats, live-streaming), violates the rules repeatedly, is criticized in any form of media circulated by a regulator, receives negative publicity published by media, or commits any other serious violation, AliExpress will impose penalties, including but not limited to deleting product information, deducting points, blocking stores, restricting access to the website's product features, and freezing or even closing the account, in accordance with the platform's relevant rules.

\[References\]
--------------
