AliExpress Bans the Sale of angle grinder chain saw disc attachment to EU,UK,Turkey and Kingdom of Saudi Arabia

Release date: January 30, 2024 Beijing time

**Dear sellers**

AliExpress is always committed to maintaining an orderly marketplace in compliance with all local laws, regulations and providing consumers with safe and high-quality goods. In order to providing consumers with safe services, AliExpress prohibits the listings and sale of angle grinder chain saw disc attachment to EU, UK, Turkey and Kingdom of Saudi Arabia.

\[Product Scope\]
-----------------

Angle grinder chain saw **attachments** are upgrade kits (generally consisting of a guide bar, a handle, and a chain) to transform an angle grinder into a chainsaw and a disc, which have a chain (like in a chainsaw) attached to them. These products enable a normal angle grinder to perform as a chainsaw.

Controlled example (including but not limited to the following type):

\[Controlled Areas\]
--------------------

EU, UK, Turkey and Kingdom of Saudi Arabia

\[Controlled measures\]
-----------------------

AliExpress prohibits the listings and sales of angle grinder chain saw disc attachment to EU, UK, Turkey and Kingdom of Saudi Arabia. If sellers have in-transit orders for the above-mentioned products, sellers are requested to handle them properly. The Platform recommends sellers to contact the buyer to cancel the order and prohibit related products from entering these markets.

Sellers shall list and sell products in accordance with applicable rules and abide by applicable laws and regulations of any country of origin and any country of destination. Where any seller is found to be listing products or releasing information in violation of the rules, AliExpress will delist or delete the related products or information and take action against the violator in accordance with relevant rules. For any seller that knowingly circumvents the rules, provides information about prohibited products in any scenario (e.g., chats, live-streaming), violates the rules repeatedly, is mentioned or suspected to be non-compliance by the media or regulator, receives negative publicity published by media, or commits any other serious violation, AliExpress will impose penalties, including but not limited to deleting product information, deducting points, blocking stores, restricting access to the website's product features, and freezing, suspend or even closing the account, in accordance with the platform's relevant rules.

Announcement on Tightening Control of Pesticide Products to EU on AliExpress

Release date: August 5, 2022

Revision date: July 18, 2024

Dear AliExpress sellers:

According to the relevant EU laws and regulations and the regulatory requirements for the control of pesticide products, combined with the prohibition and restriction rules of the AliExpress platform, in order to better ensure that the products on the platform comply with relevant domestic and foreign laws and regulations, protect the rights and interests of users on the platform and promote AliExpress In order to ensure the sustainable and healthy development of the AliExpress platform (hereinafter referred to as "AliExpress" or "Platform"), AliExpress hereby emphasizes that platform sellers are prohibited from selling pesticide products to EU consumers. We will also continue to pay attention to relevant policy changes in various countries and accordingly adjust the platform control policy accordingly.

\[Scope\]
---------

1、Plant protection products (PPP) generally refer to pesticide commodities used to protect crops. The main categories refer to herbicides, pesticides, insecticide sprays, etc. used on crops in large-scale or professional farmland, gardens, orchards, etc.

2、Biocidal product (BP) means any substance or mixture, in the form in which it is supplied to the user, consisting of, containing or generating one or more active substances, with the intention of destroying, deterring, rendering harmless, preventing the action of, or otherwise exerting a controlling effect on, any harmful organism by any means other than mere physical or mechanical action. Such products are generally highly regulated for product performance and human health considerations. The main categories include rodenticides and beehive mite removal strips.

\[Control Area\]
----------------

EU

\[Control Method\]
------------------

From August 8, 2022, the platform will be closed to the EU market for field-use pesticide products (including plant protection products and biological disinfection products). Sellers on the platform are prohibited from selling pesticide products to EU consumers. If sellers have in-transit orders for the above-mentioned products to EU consumers, are requested to handle them properly. The platform recommends sellers to contact buyers to cancel the orders. If you cannot cancel, please do so at your own risk.

The above information is for reference only and does not guarantee completeness, accuracy, and timeliness. AliExpress reserves the right to modify and supplement this content.

Thank you for your continued understanding and support!

  

Appendix:

1、EU Plant Protection Products Regulation (PPP): [https://eur-lex.europa.eu/legal-content/EN/TXT/?uri=celex%3A32009R1107](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/legal-content/EN/TXT/?uri=celex%3A32009R1107)

2、EU biocidal product regulations (BPR): [https://eur-lex.europa.eu/legal-content/EN/TXT/?uri=celex%3A32012R0528](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/legal-content/EN/TXT/?uri=celex%3A32012R0528)

3、Notes on Regulations Governing the Export of Biocide Products:

[https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/131630255](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/131630255)

AliExpress

[\[Control Method\]](#GseXO)

AliExpress Ban on the Sale of Farmland-use Pesticide Products

**Dear sellers，**

Pesticide products pose very high safety risks to consumers, according to the requirements of relevant districts and countries’ laws and regulations (e.g. the European Union，United States, etc.), and in order to protect the safety of consumers, AliExpress prohibits the sales of farmland-use pesticide products.

【Scope of application】
----------------------

Global

【Controlled Product Scope】
--------------------------

Farmland-use pesticide products are used for protecting plants or plant products against all harmful organisms or preventing the action of such organisms. Products are used for large-scale farmland, garden, orchards and other crops for professional use. Product type include but not limited to Herbicides, Insecticides，Sprays，etc.

【Control Measures】
------------------

**Merchants are prohibited from selling relevant products on the platform.** If merchants have in-transit orders for the above-mentioned products, merchant members are requested to handle them properly. The platform recommends merchants to contact the buyer to cancel the order. If cancellation failed, please bear the corresponding consequences at your own risk.

If sellers are found to list or trade the preceding prohibited farmland-use pesticide products, AliExpress shall delete the products with 2 points punishment.

AliExpress members shall list and sell products in accordance with applicable rules and abide by applicable laws and regulations of any country of origin and any country of destination. Where any member is found to be listing products or releasing information in violation of the rules, AliExpress will delist or delete the related products or information and punish the violator in accordance with relevant rules. For a member that knowingly circumvents the rules, provides information about prohibited products in any interaction scenarios (e.g., chats, live-streaming), violates the rules repeatedly, is criticized in any form of media circulated by a regulator, receives negative publicity published by media, or commits any other serious violation, AliExpress will impose penalties, including but not limited to deleting product information, deducting points, blocking stores, restricting access to the website's product features, and freezing or even closing the account, in accordance with the platform's relevant rules.

Thank you for your support and attention.

**AliExpress**

Marking/Labeling Requirements of Beauty and Personal Care Product

Base on the Cosmetic Product Enforcement Regs 2013 Art 19a, all beauty & personal care products sold to the EU, including but not limited to cosmetics, skin care products, nail products, etc., must have information labels that meet the following requirements on the product packaging.

Sellers must provide the following information on the package or the label of product:

\-Product identity/ Function

\-Manufacturer information

\-Country of Origin

\-Name and address of responsible person

\-Batch number or lot code

\-Date of minimum durability

\-Net Content

\-Ingredient declaration

\-Direction for safe use / Particular precautions

Explaination of required information:
-------------------------------------

### 1.Name and address of responsible person

During the two-year transition period from 1 January 2021, the name and address of the responsible person in the EU or UK must be affixed to the container (such as a tube, bottle or jar) and packaging (such as a box or carton) superior. If the product is manufactured outside Europe, the country of origin must be provided. The name, address and other information of the manufacturer's EU authorized representative must be clearly printed on product packaging, labels and instruction manuals. Its information must be on the product or in particular on its packaging (e.g. by printing or engraving) on an easily identifiable, durable and difficult-to-remove label.

### 2.Date of minimum durability

If a cosmetic product has a minimum shelf life of 30 months or less, it must be marked with the latest date or the following symbol on the container and packaging.

The shelf life indication must show "Best used before the end of", following with the date(date/month/year or month/year). If there are other specific conditions to ensure the durability of its products, the seller needs to explain it additionally.

### 3.Batch number or lot code

The manufacturing lot number of the product or the number used for identify product.

### 4.Additional information

If certain ingredients are present, such as preservatives and UV filters, additional information must be provided.

### 5.Product introduction

All the required information must visible on the package or the label of product, the it must be easily identifiable, durable and difficult-to-remove. The ingredient declaration must be given in a language easily understood by consumers. All other information must be in English and may be supplemented in other languages.

a.Ingredient declaration

The ingredient declaration must appear on the packaging or, if there is no packaging, on the container. If the product is sold in bulk, the ingredient declaration may be given on the container exposed to the product supply or on a notice.

If it hard be shown on the outer packaging or container, the declaration may be given on a leaflet, label, tape or card accompanying or attached to the product with instructions instructing consumers (either by an abbreviated message or a book symbol on it ). For smaller products like soaps and bath poms, "posts" can be used in place of leaflets, labels, etc.

b.Other information

Other information must normally showed on the container and packaging along with the ingredient list. If the batch code cannot appear on the container at the same time, it can only be reflected on the packaging. Also, where there are practical limitations, the conditions of use may appear on a leaflet, label, tape or card that accompanies or is attached to the product, again with directions to the consumer.

For "unpackaged" bulk cosmetics such as soaps, bath pods, and other small products, it may not be practical to affix the ingredient list on a label, tape, or card. In such cases, all relevant information required on the packaging (as described above) must be on a notice in the vicinity of the exposed container.

Example of information be included on the packaging label
---------------------------------------------------------

Note: The uploaded packaging label information must be a photograph of the actual product, and the platform does not accept the upload of outer packaging design drawings. If there are product information on multiple packaging planes, please take multiple clear packaging pictures and upload them as collages. Please describe all the key information below in English.

  

  

AliExpress

[1.Name and address of responsible person](#CvYnW)

[2.Date of minimum durability](#eUrSe)

[3.Batch number or lot code](#TgwE5)

[4.Additional information](#vpGAm)

[5.Product introduction](#m6ty9)

AliExpress Ban on the Sale of TCA in cosmetics and skincare products to the EU and USA

Release date: September 4, 2025

Revision date: /

  

**Dear AliExpress Sellers:**

In accordance with relevant laws of EU and USA, regulations, and regulatory requirements, and in conjunction with the AliExpress (“the Platform”) sales restrictions, in order to protect consumer safety, to better ensure that products listed on the Platform comply with relevant domestic and international laws and regulations, to safeguard the rights and interests of Platform users, and to promote the continued healthy development of the Platform, AliExpress hereby prohibits Platform merchants from selling the following products to the EU and USA.

【Product Scope】
---------------

Cosmetics or skin care products containing Trichloroacetic acid (TCA). Examples of regulated goods include, but are not limited to:

【Controlled Area】
-----------------

The European Union, USA.

【Control Measures】
------------------

AliExpress prohibits merchants from selling cosmetics or skin care products containing Trichloroacetic acid (TCA) to the EU and USA, and will block such products from being made available to EU and USA consumers on the Platform. Merchants with existing orders that are already in transit or pending fulfillment for these products, are requested to handle them appropriately. The Platform asks merchants to proactively contact buyers to cancel orders, in order to prevent these products from entering the EU and USA market.

AliExpress merchants shall list and sell products in accordance with applicable rules and abide by applicable laws and regulations of any country of origin and any country of destination. Where any merchant is found to be listing products or releasing information in violation of the rules, AliExpress will delist or delete the related products or information and punish the violator in accordance with relevant rules. For a merchant that knowingly circumvents the rules, provides information about prohibited products in any interaction scenarios (e.g., chats, live-streaming), violates the rules repeatedly, is criticized in any form of media circulated by a regulator, receives negative publicity published by media, or commits any other serious violation, AliExpress will impose penalties, including but not limited to deleting product information, deducting points, blocking stores, restricting access to the website's product features, and freezing or even closing the account, in accordance with the Platform's relevant rules.

【Reference】
-----------

**1\. EU:**

(1) [REGULATION (EC) No 1223/2009 OF THE EUROPEAN PARLIAMENT AND OF THE COUNCIL of 30 November 2009 on cosmetic products](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/legal-content/EN/TXT/PDF/?uri=CELEX:32009R1223);

(2) [Commission Regulation (EU) 2025/877 of 12 May 2025 amending Regulation (EC) No 1223/2009 of the European Parliament and of the Council as regards the use in cosmetic products of certain substances classified as carcinogenic, mutagenic or toxic for reproduction](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/legal-content/EN/TXT/PDF/?uri=OJ:L_202500877);

(3) [Regulation (EC) No 1272/2008 of the European Parliament and of the Council on classification, labelling and packaging of substances and mixtures](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/legal-content/EN/TXT/PDF/?uri=CELEX:32008R1272).

**2\. USA:**

(1) [Federal Food, Drug, and Cosmetic Act (FD&C Act)](https://www.govinfo.gov/content/pkg/COMPS-973/pdf/COMPS-973.pdf);

(2) [U.S. FDA Consumer Safety Notification: “FDA warns against purchasing or using chemical peel skin products without professional supervision”](https://www.fda.gov/drugs/drug-safety-and-availability/fda-warns-against-purchasing-or-using-chemical-peel-skin-products-without-professional-supervision) .

Note: The above information does not constitute any legal advice and shall not be deemed or represent the legal opinion or conclusion of the regulatory body. Further, we do not undertake or warrant that the information represents the latest laws and regulations. For specific information, please consult the competent authority, law firms, or third-party certification/testing/consulting companies in the target country or region.

AliExpress will continue to monitor the changes in laws and related policies of countries worldwide, and adjust our Platform's rules accordingly. Please contact our online customer service for any further queries.

Thank you for your support and attention.

  

  

AliExpress

AliExpress Ban on the Sale of Cosmetics Products Containing TPO to the EU

Release date: September 16, 2025

Revision date: /

  

**Dear AliExpress Sellers:**

In accordance with relevant laws of EU, regulations, and regulatory requirements, and in conjunction with the AliExpress ( "the Platform" ) sales restrictions, in order to protect consumer safety, to better ensure that products listed on the Platform comply with relevant domestic and international laws and regulations, to safeguard the rights and interests of Platform users, and to promote the continued healthy development of the Platform, AliExpress hereby prohibits Platform merchants from selling the following products to the EU.

【Product Scope】
---------------

Cosmetics products containing TPO（Trimethylbenzoyl Diphenylphosphine Oxide）.Examples of regulated goods include, but are not limited to:

【Controlled Area】
-----------------

The European Union

【Control Measures】
------------------

AliExpress prohibits merchants from selling cosmetics products containing TPO（Trimethylbenzoyl Diphenylphosphine Oxide）to the EU, and will block such products from being made available to EU consumers on the Platform. Merchants with existing orders that are already in transit or pending fulfillment for these products, are requested to handle them appropriately. The Platform asks merchants to proactively contact buyers to cancel orders, in order to prevent these products from entering the EU market.

AliExpress merchants shall list and sell products in accordance with applicable rules and abide by applicable laws and regulations of any country of origin and any country of destination. Where any merchant is found to be listing products or releasing information in violation of the rules, AliExpress will delist or delete the related products or information and punish the violator in accordance with relevant rules. For a merchant that knowingly circumvents the rules, provides information about prohibited products in any interaction scenarios (e.g., chats, live-streaming), violates the rules repeatedly, is criticized in any form of media circulated by a regulator, receives negative publicity published by media, or commits any other serious violation, AliExpress will impose penalties, including but not limited to deleting product information, deducting points, blocking stores, restricting access to the website's product features, and freezing or even closing the account, in accordance with the Platform's relevant rules.

AliExpress Announcement Regarding Prohibit Sale of Class III Medical Device, Medical Consultation & Healthcare Service

Release date: November 6, 2025

Revision date: /

Dear Sellers:

In accordance with relevant laws, regulations and requirements by various regulatory bodies in the relevant jurisdictions in conjunction with [AliExpress's Prohibited and Restricted Items Policy](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523647), as well as a comprehensive consideration of the trading environment and merchant risks, AliExpress (hereinafter referred to as "AliExpress" or "the Platform") prohibits the sale of Class III medical devices, medical consultation and healthcare services globally. This measure is taken to better safeguard consumer safety, protect the rights and interests of platform users, and promote the continued healthy development of AliExpress.

**【****Control Scope】**
-----------------------

The medical devices referred to in this announcement as Class III medical devices are those categorized in relevant countries/regions as posing a higher risk to human health, thereby necessitating stringent control over their safety and efficacy.

Examples of Class III Medical Devices:

1\. Common Class III Medical Devices:  
(1) Cardiac pacemakers;  
(2) Bone plates;  
(3) Artificial cardiopulmonary machines (heart-lung machines);  
(4) Ultrasound color Doppler machines;  
(5) Implantable hearing aids.

2\. Dental Instruments:  
(1) Synthetic resin teeth;  
(2) Gutta-percha points.

3\. Aesthetic Injectables:  
(3) Subcutaneous hyaluronic acid injections;  
(4) Breast augmentation fillers.

Note: Given the significant differences in classification criteria among relevant countries/regions, this announcement uniformly refers to Class III medical devices as those posing a higher risk to human health and requiring stringent control over their safety and efficacy.

Examples of medical consultation and healthcare services:

1. Medical consultation services: including rehabilitation, immunization, health examinations, psychological counseling, nutrition/dietetics, plastic surgery, and massage therapy.

2\. Medical tourism services: including overseas medical travel.

**【****Control Area】**
----------------------

Global

**【****Control Measures****】**
------------------------------

The Platform prohibits merchants from selling Class III medical devices,medical consultation and healthcare services and blocks such product listings globally. Merchants are required to comply with the regulations of their respective destination markets and relevant platform policies to ensure smooth market trade.

**【****Violations and punishments】**
------------------------------------

Sellers shall list and sell products in accordance with applicable rules and abide by applicable laws and regulations of any country of origin and any country of destination. If any Seller is found to be listing products or releasing information in violation of the rules, the Platform will delist or delete the related products or information and punish the violator in accordance with relevant rules. For a seller that knowingly circumvents the rules, provides information about prohibited products in any interaction scenarios (e.g., chats, live-streaming), violates the rules repeatedly, is criticized or admonished in any form of media circulated by a regulator, receives negative publicity published by media, or commits any other serious violation, the Platform will impose penalties, including but not limited to deleting product information, deducting points, blocking stores, restricting access to the website's product features, and freezing or even closing the account, in accordance with the Platform's relevant rules.

AliExpress.com will continue to monitor the changes in laws and related policies, and may adjust our rules and policies accordingly.

AliExpress

Announcement on Tightening Control of Health Food Products on AliExpress

Release date: August 5, 2022

Revision date: July 10, 2025

**Dear AliExpress sellers:**

To regulate the development of the health food industry on AliExpress, raise the quality of health food products, and thus safeguard lives and property of consumers, AliExpress will release standards for product posting and impose quality control requirements for this industry. These efforts aim to further tighten control over the health food industry.

**I. Applicable Scope**
-----------------------

All subcategories under Beauty & Health>> Health Care>> Health Food (Vitamins & Supplements);

All subcategories under Mother & Kids>> Baby Food >> Health Food;

All subcategories under Mother & Kids>>Pregnancy & Maternity >>Maternal Nutrition.

**II. Requirements for Merchant Inclusion**
-------------------------------------------

1、The health food industry has launched its merchant onboarding and is open to all legitimate brands.

2、Merchants shall firstly provide qualification documents that comply with the platform requirements. Merchants are allowed to post their products in the health food category only if the qualification has been approved.

3、See Requirements for Cross-Border Merchant Inclusion at: [https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523099](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523099)

Italian merchants shall provide the SCIA Certificate for onboarding.

Spanish merchants shall provide the Food Health Registration Certificate (or RGSEAA Notification No.) for onboarding.

**III. Standards for Posting Products**
---------------------------------------

1、Mandatory product attributes: Merchants are required to truthfully fill in the following required attributes when publishing their products in the category of health food:

（1）Brand;

（2）Product Name;

（3）Product Specifications;

（4）Ingredients;

（5）Nutritional Information;

（6）Usage & Dosage;

（7）Target Population;

（8）Storage Method;

（9）Shelf Life;

（10）Precautions;

（11）Manufacturer Name;

（12）Manufacturer Address;

（13）Allergen Information;

（14）Place of Origin.

Merchants shall fill in the information based on the product label. The filling requirements of the attributes are as follows:

（1）Place of origin refers to the place where health food is produced or manufactured. This information shall be in consistent with that on the label;

（2）Ingredients refers to all material components of the product, or at least the main functional ingredients;

（3）Shelf life refers to before the product is unsealed, the period during which the quality of the product maintains under the storage conditions as specified on the label;

（4）Usage and dosage refers to the eating method, the number of times, dosage per day, a warning that exceeds the recommended daily intake;

（5）Product specification refers to the product packaging specifications of the smallest package being sold, for example, 100 pieces/bottle.

（6）Precautions highlight safety instructions for consumers regarding consumption, storage, or other relevant aspects.

（7）Allergen Information indicates whether the product contains allergenic substances such as dairy, eggs, fish, shellfish, etc. If present, it must be clearly noted.

2、Products with invalid brand information such as "other" or "None" are no longer allowed to be published in the category of health food.

3、Under the health food category, it is not allowed to publish ordinary foods other than health foods, as well as powdered or sliced foods that have only undergone primary processing and unrestricted dose packaging. Common prohibited food products are as follows:

4、Health food does not allow adding ingredients prohibited in the country of sale. Those ingredients include some prohibited and restricted herbal ingredients or medicinal ingredients (including those approved for use in traditional herbal medicine), such as ephedra and kava, aloe-emodin and its preparation, emodin and its preparation, danthron and its preparation, sibutramine, phenolphthalein, DMAA, DMHA, steroid, dinitrophenol, etc. See the attachment for the details.

5、Health food must be sold under the name of health product, shall not contain any claim below:

（1）Information suggesting that the product has features such as preventing, or aiding therapy, or curing human diseases in terms of enhancing sexual functions, treating high blood pressure, improving hearing, and killing bacteria or germs, can replace normal diet, etc.;

（2）Information that is false, ambiguous or misleading;

（3）Information that implies health may be affected if not using the product;

（4）Information that mentions the speed or specific kilograms in losing weight;

（5）Information that mentions the advice given by certain doctors or health professionals;

（6）Information that advise or encourage excessive consumption of a certain type of food;

（7）Information that implies balanced diet can't provide necessary nutrients;

（8）Information that makes consumers doubt the safety and/or nutritional adequacy of other foods;

（9）Information that mentions potential changes to bodily functions, leading to potential customer panic or being used for profits;

（10）Any other descriptions that violate laws, administrative regulations, or market regulatory requirements.

**IV. Requirements for Product Qualifications**
-----------------------------------------------

Merchants shall upload the following information on the Qualification Information module of the product posting page when publishing products under health food related categories:

1、United States:FDA Food Facility Registration Certificate + Self-Declaration Statement executed by the Seller + Pictures of Actual Packaging/Label + (if applicable) FDA Approval for New Dietary Ingredients

2、South Korea: COA (Certificate of Analysis) Test Report + Actual Packaging/Label Photo

3、BrazilCOA (Certificate of Analysis) Test ReportActual Packaging/Label Photo

4、MexicoNOM Certification CertificateNOM Certification NumberActual Packaging/Label Photo

COA (Certificate of Analysis) Test Report Requirements：Test Items: Must include ingredients, heavy metals, and microbial testing.Heavy Metal Testing: Must cover lead, arsenic, mercury, and cadmium at a minimum.Microbial Testing: Must include:Total Aerobic Bacterial CountStaphylococcus aureusEscherichia coliTotal Molds and YeastsEnterobacteriaceaeSalmonella

Product Packaging Label Requirements：The actual product packaging label must include the following information:

BrandProduct NameProduct Specifications (e.g., "100 tablets/bottle")IngredientsPlace of OriginNutritional InformationDosage InstructionsShelf LifeFor domestically produced health foods in China, the label must also include the health food registration or filing number.

**V. Timeline and Penalties for Violations**
--------------------------------------------

1、Existing products whose brand attributes are "Other" or "None" will be taken down but can be edited (For the new categories on August 5, 2022, it will be implemented from August 31, 2022).

2、Any above-mentioned prohibited food products published in the category of health food will be deleted. This will go into effect as of the issue date of this announcement.

3、Any addition of illegally prohibited ingredients to health food products will be deleted and two points will be deducted from the seller's account. This will go into effect as of the issue date of this announcement. Any products that contain above mentioned prohibited claims will be removed (editable for re-uploading) for the first time; and will be deleted for the second violation. This will go into effect as of the issue date of this announcement.

4、Penalties for any attempts to evade control by intentionally misplacing category and wrong filling origin will be imposed as follows:

For the first-time violation, the products will be removed with no points deducted, and will be removed from the platform for the second-time violation. For a merchant who evades the controls maliciously more than once, its commodities will be removed from the platform with two points deducted.

5、In the event where the merchant submits false label, or falsely use another merchant's label information or health food registration number, their products will be deleted and 6 points will be deducted from their account once verified.For accounts with severe violations, the platform will impose penalties in accordance with [AliExpress Rules on Handling Severe Disruption of Platform Order](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/137260610):Serious violation: 12 points/time, freezing the AliExpress account for seven days;Extremely serious violation: 48 points/time, closing the AliExpress account.

VI. Appendix
------------

See **FAQ about Qualification Submission on AliExpress** at: [https://sell.aliexpress.com/\_\_pc/LfHYeAD1WC.htm](https://sell.aliexpress.com/__pc/LfHYeAD1WC.htm)

Some Countries Prohibited to Add Ingredients Query Reference：

1、South Korea list of ingredients prohibited to be added in food/health products: [https://www.foodsafetykorea.go.kr/portal/fooddanger/foodDirectImportBlock.do?menu\_grp=MENU\_NEW02&menu\_no=3594&search\_put=](https://www.foodsafetykorea.go.kr/portal/fooddanger/foodDirectImportBlock.do?menu_grp=MENU_NEW02&menu_no=3594&search_put=).

2、Examples of major commodity compliance requirements related to ingredients in the United States:

（1）New dietary ingredient (I. e., dietary ingredient in a dietary supplement sold on the market after October 15, 1994): Manufacturers or distributors must submit premarket safety notices (New dietary ingredient Ingredient Notifications ,NDINs) to FDA at least 75 days prior to the introduction or delivery of a dietary supplement containing the Dietary ingredient into interstate commerce. There is no authoritative list of such ingredients, so it is the responsibility of manufacturers and distributors to determine whether an ingredient is a "new dietary ingredient" and, if not, to ensure that the dietary supplement containing the dietary ingredient was marketed before October 15, 1994, or that the dietary ingredient was marketed for use in dietary supplements before that date. For more information on the FDA's New Dietary Ingredient (NDI) Notice, please visit [https://www.fda.gov/food/dietary-supplements/new-dietary-ingredients-ndi-notification-process](https://www.fda.gov/food/dietary-supplements/new-dietary-ingredients-ndi-notification-process)

（2）Any non-dietary ingredients (excipients, preservatives, color additives, etc.) and product packaging materials in dietary supplements are subject to the Food Additive Provisions of the FDCA and require prior approval by the FDA as a food additive.

（3）Drug Ingredients: Dietary supplement products should not contain the listed drug ingredients, otherwise they will be defined as drugs and require prior FDA marketing approval. The active ingredient in a product can be checked on the [https://www.accessdata.fda.gov/scripts/cder/daf/](https://www.accessdata.fda.gov/scripts/cder/daf/) to determine if an FDA-approved drug contains the ingredient.

（4）Does not contain unauthorized color additives (artificial colorants) : [21 CFR 74](https://www.law.cornell.edu/cfr/text/21/part-74/subpart-A)

（5）Prohibited Ingredients in 21 CFR 189: [https://www.law.cornell.edu/cfr/text/21/part-189/subpart-C](https://www.law.cornell.edu/cfr/text/21/part-189/subpart-C)

3、Brazil prohibits the addition of ingredient queries: [https://www.gov.br/anvisa/pt-br/assuntos/medicamentos/controlados/lista-substancias](https://www.gov.br/anvisa/pt-br/assuntos/medicamentos/controlados/lista-substancias)

Thank you for your attention and support!

AliExpress

Notes on Regulations Governing the Export of Biocide Products

Background
----------

Biocide products refer to products that kill pathogenic microorganisms among humans and in the environment we live, or inhibit their growth, or counteract their pathogenic action. Biocide products imported into the US are divided into two categories: antimicrobial pesticides for disinfecting ordinary environmental and hard surfaces, which are regulated by the US Environmental Protection Agency (EPA) and falling within the scope of the Federal Insecticide, Fungicide, and Rodenticide Act (FIFRA); and antiseptics for disinfecting critical medical devices and different parts of the body (like skin and hand), which are regulated by the US Food and Drug Administration (FDA). This page mainly describes the regulatory requirements for the **second category**.

Biocide products imported into the EU are subject to the Biocidal Products Regulation (BPR) which sets out explicit rules for Biocide products and their active substances. Biocide products are allowed to be placed on the EU market only if they comply with applicable requirements.

Scope
-----

Biocide products on this page mainly refer to hand sanitizers and wet wipes regulated by the FDA. Only three active ingredients, **benzalkonium chloride, alcohol (ethyl alcohol or ethanol, 60%-95%) and isopropanol (70%-91.3%)**, are eligible for usage.

Biocide products marketed the EU market refer to biocides for human health falling within the scope of the Biocidal Products Regulation (BPR) (Regulation (EU) 528/2012), such as **hand sanitizers, gel hand sanitizers and disinfectants for private and public spaces**.

Regulations
-----------

In the US, Biocide products are over-the-counter (OTC) topical antimicrobial drug products that are regulated by the US Food and Drug Administration (FDA) as OTC drugs, which shall be subject to establishment registration, National Drug Code (NDC) number assignment and drug listing requirements before they are placed on the market. Furthermore, Biocide products shall be manufactured according to the current Good Manufacturing Practices (cGMPs) and conform to the requirements on content and format of labeling under 21 CFR Part 201 Subpart C.

According to the EU BPR, all biocidal products require an authorization before they can be placed on the market, and the active substances contained in a biocidal product must have been approved previously. There are, however, certain exceptions to this principle. There are associated labeling requirements, covering the name and address of the authorization holder, authorized use, authorization number and categories of users to which a biocidal product is restricted. You should also ensure the labels are written in the official language(s) of the Member State(s) in which you offer the product for sale or supply. It is your responsibility to provide accurate and complete product information about biocidal products. In addition to compliance with the BPR, a registration under the EU Registration, Evaluation, Authorization and Restriction of Chemicals (REACH) Regulation is required for biocidal products if the non-active substances contained reach the threshold of 1 ton per year and are not included in the Exemption List. Manufacturers shall comply with the Classification, Labeling and Packaging (CLP) Regulation for the classification, labeling and packaging of biocidal products and prepare Safety Data Sheets (SDS) under EU regulations.

Legal Basis
-----------

For more information about the US regulations on Biocide products, please refer to:

· [Federal Food, Drug, and Cosmetic Act (FD&C Act)](https://www.fda.gov/regulatory-information/laws-enforced-fda/federal-food-drug-and-cosmetic-act-fdc-act)

· [Regulatory Mechanisms for Marketing OTC Drug Products](https://www.fda.gov/about-fda/center-drug-evaluation-and-research-cder/regulatory-mechanisms-marketing-otc-drug-products#monograph)

· [National Drug Code Directory](https://www.fda.gov/drugs/drug-approvals-and-databases/national-drug-code-directory)

For more information about the EU regulations on biocidal products, please refer to:

· [Biocides - Frequently asked questions](http://www.hse.gov.uk/biocides/faq.htm)

· [National helpdesks under the BPR](https://echa.europa.eu/support/helpdesks)

· [Understanding BPR - ECHA](https://echa.europa.eu/regulations/biocidal-products-regulation)

**Note: The above information does not constitute any legal advice and shall not be deemed or represent the legal opinion or conclusion of the regulatory body. Further, we do not undertake or warrant that the information represents the latest laws and regulations. For specific information, please consult the competent authority, law firms, or third-party certification/testing/consulting companies in the target country or region.**  

  
**AliExpress**  
August 31, 2020

Notice on Strengthening Control of Biocide Products

  

**Dear AliExpress sellers,**

The world is now at a critical stage of fighting against the novel coronavirus COVID-19. Biocide products are playing a positive and key role in curbing the spread of the virus, which results in huge public demand for biocide products. To address the rising demand for biocide products globally and provide high-quality and safe products for consumers, the platform will strengthen its control of the biocide products sold on AliExpress to the EU, UK, and US markets, starting in mid-October 2020. The specific requirements are as follows:

**I. Scope**

1.In the US: Biocide products refer to hand sanitizers (including instant hand sanitizers, hand gels, etc.) and wipes subject to the regulation of the FDA that are used on skin and hands for sterilization and anti-bacterial purposes;

2\. In the EU and the UK: Biocide products refer to biocidal products subject to the Biocidal Product Regulation (BPR) \[Regulation (EU) 528/2012\] that are used for human hygiene purposes in private and public areas, such as hand sanitizers, instant hand gel and other disinfectants.

The eight sub-categories involved in initial control include:

1）Home & Garden >> Household Merchandises >> Household Cleaning Chemicals >> All-Purpose Cleaner

2）Home & Garden >> Household Merchandises >> Household Cleaning Tools & Accessories >> Disinfectant Wipes

3）Home & Garden >> Household Merchandises >> Household Cleaning Tools & Accessories >> Paper Towels

4）Beauty & Health >> Skin Care >> Hands & Nails >> Hand Soaps

5）Beauty & Health >> Bath & Shower >> Soap

6）Beauty & Health >> Sanitary Paper>> Wet Wipes

7）Mother & Kids >> Baby Care >> Baby Care Tools>> Baby Wet Wipes

8）Mother & Kids >> Baby Care >> Baby Skin Care >> Baby Hand Soaps

Note: When posting a product in any of the above sub-categories, the merchant shall first clarify the specific functions of the product and tick the checkboxes for the corresponding functional attributes, e.g., Kill Germs/Disinfection/Remove Germs/Antimicrobial/Bacteriostatic/Cleaning (multiple choice), according to the product's actual characteristics. Product functional attributes are expected to become available in mid-October 2020. As from the date of availability, merchants will be required to select functional attributes for their products before posting any products in the aforementioned sub-categories; otherwise, product posting will not be allowed. Selecting any functional attributes other than cleaning shall comply with the following control requirements.

**II. Requirements**

Upon launch of the product functional attributes, the platform will start to control newly published and edited biocide products from mid-October 2020. For biocide products for export to the EU and the UK, the merchants shall submit qualified label images in relevant foreign languages, and shall not claim their products have efficacy in treating or preventing specific pathogens. The platform will review and clear the inventory of goods starting from mid-November 2020. The goods that fail to pass the review will be banned from the UK market first. Please upload the label images in foreign languages in time. Specific requirements are as follows:

Products marketed in the EU and the UK must bear the label image in the local language (English for the UK), which contains at least the content of the active ingredients, instructions and warnings. For more information about the labeling for biocide products, refer to: https://www.hse.gov.uk/biocide/eu-bpr/packaging-labelling-requirements.htm.

The labels of biocide products are not allowed to indicate "low-risk", "non-toxic", "harmless", "natural", "environmental-friendly", "animal friendly" and other similar terms. In addition, the labels shall not contain statements about surgical and medical uses or efficacy in treating certain pathogen-related infections, for example killing escherichia coli, candida albicans, staphylococcus aureus, novel coronavirus, SAS virus, SARS-COV-2, etc.

Furthermore, the platform prohibits the sale of biocide products recalled by the US FDA and Health Canada. The merchants should pay close attention to the list of biocide products recalled by the FDA and Health Canada for any updates and avoid selling the recalled products:

1）[List of biocide products recalled by the US FDA](https://www.fda.gov/drugs/drug-safety-and-availability/fda-updates-hand-sanitizers-consumers-should-not-use#products)

2）[List of biocide products recalled by Health Canada](https://healthycanadians.gc.ca/recall-alert-rappel-avis/hc-sc/2020/73385a-eng.php)

**III. Violations and punishments**

1.Commodities that fail to meet the above requirements will be banned from the US and/or UK markets on the platform.

2.For commodities that are miscategorized and/or assigned incorrect functional attributes to evade controls, corresponding punishments will be imposed as follows:

For the first-time violation, the commodities will be pulled off the shelf with no points deducted. The commodities will be removed from the platform for the second-time violation. For a merchant who evades the controls maliciously more than once, its commodities will be removed from the platform with two points deducted.

3.Merchants who sell recalled goods will have their commodities removed from the platform with two points deducted.

4.For merchants who have submitted false label information or used others' label information as verified by investigation, their commodities will be removed from the platform with six points deducted.  

Stores engaged in severe violations of the platform regulations will be penalized in accordance with the [AliExpress Rules on Handling Severe Disruption of Platform Order](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/36963666/122523665):  
Serious violation: 12 points/time, freezing the AliExpress account for seven days  
Extremely Serious violation: 48 points/time, closing the AliExpress account

Thank you for your attention and support.

For more information about the export regulations for biocide products, refer to:  
[Notes on Regulations Governing the Export of Biocide Products](https://rule.aliexpress.com/rule-channels/37978936/131630255)

**AliExpress**

September 27, 2020

- - -

AliExpress Announcement on Strengthening Qualification Control over Mosquito Killer Lamps Sold to United States of America

Release date: September 26, 2024

Revision date: /

Dear AliExpress Sellers,

AliExpress (the “Platform”) is always committed to maintaining an orderly marketplace in compliance with all local laws, regulations and providing consumers with safe and high-quality goods. In accordance with the requirements set forth by the United States Environmental Protection Agency (EPA)， AliExpress will strengthen the certification control over mosquito killer lamps sold to the United States of America.

【Control Scope】
---------------

|     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Level 1 Category** | **Level 2 Category** | **Leaf Category** |
| Lights & Lighting | Outdoor Lighting | Mosquito Killer Lamps |

【Control Area】
--------------

United States of America

【Qualification Requirements】
----------------------------

The manufacturer of mosquito killer lamps needs to register with the U.S. Environmental Protection Agency (EPA) and obtain an EPA Establishment Number. At the same time, the EPA establishment number must be visible on the outer packaging of the mosquito killer lamps.

Sellers of mosquito killer lamps need to meet the following requirements:

**1、EPA certification**

The EPA registration certificate must include manufacturer information and EPA Establishment Number.If a mosquito killer lamp product does not work in a purely physical way (including through electricity, light, and mechanical parts), but relies on chemical substances or mixed substances to kill mosquitos, the product must be registered with the EPA in addition to obtaining an EPA registration number. However, such products which rely on chemical substances or mixed substances to kill mosquitos, which whether or not have met the registration requirements, are currently prohibited from being sold in the United States.

**2、Photos of product packaging/labels**

The physical packaging/labels of the product must contain at least the following information:

（1）Product name;

（2）Manufacturer name and address;

（3）EPA Establishment Number.

In addition, this information must be consistent with the information on the EPA registration certificate.

【Control Measures】
------------------

The Platform will remove any products sold to the United States that have not obtained the relevant certification. Sellers are urged to swiftly ensure that their product certifications in the listing categories meet the required standards, in order to facilitate smooth trade in the United States market.

【Violation and Penalty】
-----------------------

The following violations and penalties will apply after the start of the control measures:

1、If a product does not meet the above control requirements: the Platform will remove the product from the U.S. market.

2、If the uploaded certification materials seriously do not match the product, the Platform will treat it as a case of false certification and will delete the product and deduct 6 points per occurrence.

3、If a product is not listed under the correct category, for the first violation, the product will be removed by the Platform (editable); for the second violation, the product will be deleted by the Platform; for repeated violations, the Platform will escalate the penalty to product deletion and deduct 2 points per occurrence.

4、Selling recalled products and violating restriction and prohibition rules will result in product deletion and a deduction of 2 points.

5、For false certification, the following penalties will apply: Upon verification of submitted false label information or misappropriation of another's label information, the product will be deleted and 6 points will be deducted.

For accounts with serious violations, the following penalties will be applied in accordance with the AliExpress "Disruption of Platform Order" rules:

Malicious evasion: deletion and deduction of 6 points per occurrence

Serious: 12 points per occurrence (account frozen for 7 days)

Particularly serious: 48 points per occurrence (account closure)

The Platform reminds all Sellers to comply with product listings and transactions requirements. Sellers shall list and sell products in accordance with applicable rules and abide by applicable Platform policies/laws and regulations of any country of origin and any country of destination. For Sellers who list prohibited products and information, the Platform will remove or delete the related products and information, and will penalize sellers with violations according to the relevant Platform rules. For Sellers who maliciously circumvent rules, post prohibited information in any scenario (e.g., chats, live-streaming), repeatedly violate rules, receive notice from regulatory authorities, get exposed by significant media, or other serious violations, the Platform will take actions including but not limited to product information deletion, point deduction, shop blocking, restriction of website product features, account freezing, or closure. AliExpress will continue to monitor changes in relevant policies and make appropriate adjustments to our Platform control policies accordingly.

【References】
------------

1、[EPA:Pesticide Devices: A Guide for Consumers](https://www.epa.gov/pesticides/pesticide-devices-guide-consumers#1)

2、[EPA: Pesticide Registration Manual](https://www.epa.gov/pesticide-registration/pesticide-registration-manual)

3、[EPA registration information List](https://www.epa.gov/compliance/national-list-active-epa-registered-foreign-and-domestic-pesticide-andor-device)

Note: The above information does not constitute any legal advice and shall not be deemed or represent the legal opinion or conclusion of the regulatory body. Further, we do not undertake or warrant that the information represents the latest laws and regulations. For specific information, please consult the competent authority, law firms, or third-party certification/testing/consulting companies in the target country or region.

AliExpress will continue to monitor the changes in laws and related policies of countries worldwide, and adjust our platform rules accordingly.

Please contact our online customer service for any further queries.

Thank you for your support and attention.

AliExpress

Announcement on Strengthening Control of Novelty Lighters

  

Dear AliExpress sellers,

According to several countries’ regulation and laws(including the United States、The European Union, the United Kingdom、Australia, etc.), also it could be easily misused by children causing injury or even death. In view of these risks, the platform has decided to prohibit the sales of Novelty Lighters.

\[Prohibited Products\]
-----------------------

Platform prohibits the listing and sales of Novelty Lighters. Novelty Lighters usually be a child-appealing lighter, with child-appealing defined as: lighters or their holders, the shape of which resembles cartoon characters, toys, guns, watches, telephones, musical instruments, vehicles, human body or parts of the human body, animals, food or beverages, or that play musical notes, or have flashing lights or moving objects or other entertaining features. This excludes lighters that are printed or decorated with logos, labels, decals, artwork or heat shrinkable sleeves.

\[Regions for Prohibition\]
---------------------------

Global

\[Control measures\]
--------------------

If sellers are found to list or trade the preceding prohibited Novelty Lighters, AliExpress shall delete the products. If sellers are found to relist the products or deliberately avoid the management, AliExpress shall delete the products with 2 points punishment.

AliExpress members shall list and sell products in accordance with applicable rules and abide by applicable laws and regulations of any country of origin and any country of destination. Where any member is found to be listing products or releasing information in violation of the rules, AliExpress will delist or delete the related products or information and punish the violator in accordance with relevant rules. For a member that knowingly circumvents the rules, provides information about prohibited products in any interaction scenarios (e.g., chats, live-streaming), violates the rules repeatedly, is criticized in any form of media circulated by a regulator, receives negative publicity published by media, or commits any other serious violation, AliExpress will impose penalties, including but not limited to deleting product information, deducting points, blocking stores, restricting access to the website's product features, and freezing or even closing the account, in accordance with the platform's relevant rules.

\[References\]
--------------

1、Australia：[https://www.legislation.gov.au/Details/F2011L00228](https://www.legislation.gov.au/Details/F2011L00228)

2、The European Union: [https://ec.europa.eu/commission/presscorner/detail/en/IP\_07\_325](https://ec.europa.eu/commission/presscorner/detail/en/IP_07_325)

3、Canada：[https://www.canada.ca/en/health-canada/services/consumer-product-safety/reports-publications/industry-professionals/industry-guide-canadian-requirements-lighters.html](https://www.canada.ca/en/health-canada/services/consumer-product-safety/reports-publications/industry-professionals/industry-guide-canadian-requirements-lighters.html)

4、The United States：[https://www.govinfo.gov/content/pkg/CFR-2018-title16-vol2/xml/CFR-2018-title16-vol2-part1210.xml](https://www.govinfo.gov/content/pkg/CFR-2018-title16-vol2/xml/CFR-2018-title16-vol2-part1210.xml)

[https://www.lighterassociation.org/state-laws](https://www.lighterassociation.org/state-laws)

5、Singapore：[https://www.customs.gov.sg/businesses/importing-goods/controlled-and-prohibited-goods-for-import](https://www.customs.gov.sg/businesses/importing-goods/controlled-and-prohibited-goods-for-import)
